# Surah 8 — Al-Anfal

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 90/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.081 · Longest prose run 24 words · Em dashes 0

_Translated by claude-sonnet-5 (opus-4.8 on flagged revisions); graded by gemini-3.1-pro-preview at 2026-07-07T10:52:35.196Z. Quality metrics are surah-level. Review each translation against the Arabic below, never against any other translation._

**Overlap spans to check:** "him as for ali he is the cousin of the messenger of allah and his son in law and he pointed with his hand"

**Examiner verdict:** The translation is generally excellent, but contains two major mistranslations involving misattribution of speakers and actors in narrative accounts.

---

## 8:1 — verse 1

### Translation

# تفسير سورة الأنفال (Interpretation of Surat al-Anfal)

It is Medinan. Its verses number seventy-six. Its words number one thousand, six hundred, and thirty-one. Its letters number five thousand, two hundred, and ninety-four. And Allah knows best.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

Al-Bukhari said: Ibn Abbas said, "Al-Anfal (the spoils): the war booty." [chain] Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: I said to Ibn Abbas, "Surat al-Anfal?" He said, "It was revealed concerning Badr."

As for what he related here from Ibn Abbas as a suspended report, it was likewise narrated by Ali ibn Abi Talha from Ibn Abbas, that he said: "Al-Anfal: the war booty. It belonged exclusively to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, no one else had any share of it." Mujahid, Ikrimah, Ata, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, Ata al-Khurasani, Muqatil ibn Hayyan, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and others besides them said the same, that it means the war booty.

Al-Kalbi said, from Abu Salih, from Ibn Abbas, that he said: "Al-Anfal: the war booty." Labid said concerning it: "Indeed the fear of our Lord is the best nafal (extra gift), and by Allah's leave I am slow and I am swift."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Qasim ibn Muhammad said: I heard a man asking Ibn Abbas about "al-Anfal." Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, said: "The horse is part of the nafal, and the spoils taken from a slain enemy (salab) are part of the nafal." Then the man repeated his question, and Ibn Abbas said the same again. Then the man said, "What are the anfal that Allah mentioned in His Book?" Al-Qasim said: he kept asking him until he nearly cornered him, so Ibn Abbas said, "Do you know what this resembles? It resembles the case of Sabigh, whom Umar ibn al-Khattab struck."

Abd al-Razzaq said: [chain] al-Qasim ibn Muhammad said: Ibn Abbas said: "Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, when asked about something, would say: 'I neither command you nor forbid you.'" Then Ibn Abbas said: "By Allah, Allah never sent His Prophet ﷺ except as one who forbids and commands, who permits and prohibits." Al-Qasim said: then a man was set loose upon Ibn Abbas, asking him about al-Anfal. Ibn Abbas said: "A man would be given as nafal the horse of another man and his weapon." The man repeated the question to him, and he gave him the same answer, then repeated it again until he angered him, so Ibn Abbas said: "Do you know what this resembles? It resembles the case of Sabigh, whom Umar ibn al-Khattab struck until the blood flowed onto his heels," or, "onto his feet." The man said, "As for you, Allah has already taken revenge for Umar against you."

This is a sound chain going back to Ibn Abbas, showing that he interpreted al-nafal as what the leader (imam) grants to certain individuals from the spoils taken from a slain enemy or similar, after the division of the basic booty. This is what most jurists readily understand from the word nafal. And Allah knows best.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: they asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about the fifth (al-khumus) after the four-fifths had been distributed, so there was revealed: {They ask you about the anfal.}

Ibn Mas'ud and Masruq said: "There is no nafal on the day of engagement in battle; the nafal only occurs before the ranks meet." Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this from both of them.

Ibn al-Mubarak and others narrated, from Abd al-Malik ibn Abi Sulayman, from Ata ibn Abi Rabah, concerning {They ask you about the anfal}: "They ask you about what strays from the polytheists to the Muslims without fighting, whether an animal, a male slave, a female slave, or goods. This is nafal for the Prophet ﷺ, who does with it as he wishes."

This indicates that he interpreted al-anfal as fay (spoils taken without battle), which is what is taken from the disbelievers without fighting.

Ibn Jarir said: Others said: it refers to the anfal given to raiding detachments (saraya). [chain] Ali ibn Salih ibn Hayy said: "It has reached me, concerning His statement {They ask you about the anfal}, that it means the raiding detachments."

What is meant by this is what the leader grants to some of the raiding detachments in addition to their share along with the rest of the army. Al-Sha'bi stated this explicitly. Ibn Jarir preferred the view that it refers to additions beyond the regular division, and this is supported by what has been reported concerning the reason for the revelation of the verse, which is what Imam Ahmad narrated, saying: [chain] Sa'd ibn Abi Waqqas said: "On the day of Badr, when my brother Umayr was killed and I killed Sa'id ibn al-As and took his sword, which was called 'Dhu al-Katifah,' I brought it to the Prophet of Allah ﷺ, and he said, 'Go and put it among the collected spoils.'" He said: "I went back with what only Allah knows of grief over my brother's death and the taking of my spoils." He said: "I had gone only a little way when Surat al-Anfal was revealed, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to me, 'Go and take your sword.'"

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Sa'd ibn Malik said: he said, "O Messenger of Allah, Allah has today satisfied me against the polytheists, so grant me this sword." He said, "This sword belongs neither to you nor to me, put it down." He said: "So I put it down, then I went back and said, 'Perhaps this sword will today be given to someone who did not fight as I fought!' Then a man called me from behind me." He said: "I said, 'Has Allah revealed something concerning me?'" He said, "You asked me for the sword, and it was not mine to give, but it has now been granted to me, so it is yours." He said: and Allah revealed this verse: {They ask you about the anfal. Say, 'The anfal belong to Allah and the Messenger.'}

Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and al-Nasa'i narrated it through various chains, from Abu Bakr ibn Ayyash, with this wording. Al-Tirmidhi said: "Hasan sahih (good and authentic)."

Likewise Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi narrated it: [chain] Musab ibn Sa'd narrated from Sa'd, who said: "Four verses were revealed concerning me. I obtained a sword on the day of Badr, so I came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, 'Grant it to me as nafal.' He said, 'Put it back where you took it from,' twice. Then I went back to him again, and the Prophet ﷺ said, 'Put it back where you took it from.' Then this verse was revealed: {They ask you about the anfal...}"

The rest of the hadith concerns the revelation of {And We have enjoined upon man goodness to his parents} [al-Ankabut: 8], and His statement {Indeed, intoxicants and gambling...} [al-Ma'idah: 90], and the verse concerning bequest (al-wasiyyah). Muslim narrated this in his Sahih, from the hadith of Shu'bah, with this wording.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: [chain] I heard Abu Usayd Malik ibn Rabi'ah say: "I obtained the sword of Ibn A'idh on the day of Badr, and the sword was called al-Marzuban. When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded the people to return whatever nafal was in their possession, I came forward and cast it among the nafal. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ never refused anything he was asked for. Al-Arqam ibn Abi al-Arqam al-Makhzumi saw it and asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ for it, so he gave it to him."

Ibn Jarir also narrated this through another route.

[Another reason for the revelation of the verse]

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Umamah said: I asked Ubadah about al-Anfal, and he said: "It was revealed concerning us, the people of Badr, when we disagreed about the nafal and our conduct regarding it became bad. So Allah took it out of our hands and placed it in the hands of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ divided it among the Muslims equally," meaning, "with fairness."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Ubadah ibn al-Samit said: "We went out with the Prophet ﷺ, and I was present with him at Badr. The people met in battle, and Allah, Exalted is He, routed the enemy. One group went off pursuing them, routing and killing them. Another group busied itself gathering and collecting the enemy camp's goods. Another group surrounded the Messenger of Allah ﷺ so that the enemy could not catch him off guard. When night came and the people returned to one another, those who had gathered the spoils said, 'We collected it, so no one else has any share in it.' And those who had gone out pursuing the enemy said, 'You have no more right to it than we do. We are the ones who kept the enemy away from it and routed them.'"

Those who had surrounded the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "You have no greater right than us. We surrounded the Messenger of God ﷺ and feared that the enemy might catch him off guard, so we occupied ourselves with him." Then there was revealed: {They ask you about the spoils of war (al-anfal). Say: the spoils of war belong to God and the Messenger, so fear God and set right the matter between you}. The Messenger of God ﷺ then divided them among the Muslims. The Messenger of God, when he raided in enemy territory, would grant a fourth as a special allotment (nafl), and when he returned with all the people coming back together, he would grant a third. He disliked excessive allotments and would say: "Let the strong among the believers give back to their weak."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah related it from the hadith of Sufyan al-Thawri, from Abd al-Rahman ibn al-Harith, with similar wording, and al-Tirmidhi said: this is a hasan (sound) hadith. Ibn Hibban related it in his Sahih, and al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn al-Harith, and al-Hakim said: its chain of transmission is sound according to the criterion of Muslim, though the two of them (Bukhari and Muslim) did not include it.

Abu Dawud, al-Nasa'i, Ibn Jarir, Ibn Mardawayh (the wording being his), Ibn Hibban, and al-Hakim related through various routes, from Dawud ibn Abi Hind, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: On the day of Badr the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Whoever does such and such shall have such and such." The young men among the fighters hastened to that, while the older men remained beneath the banners. When the spoils were gathered, they came seeking what had been designated for them. The older men said: "Do not prefer yourselves over us, for we were a support for you: had you been overwhelmed, you would have retreated to us." So they disputed, and God Almighty sent down: {They ask you about the spoils of war} up to His saying: {and obey God and His Messenger if you are believers}.

Al-Thawri said, from al-Kalbi, from Abu Salih, from Ibn Abbas, who said: On the day of Badr the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Whoever kills someone shall have such and such, and whoever brings a captive shall have such and such." Abu al-Yasar came with two captives and said: "O Messenger of God, you made us a promise." Sa'd ibn Ubadah then stood and said: "O Messenger of God, if you give these men their due, nothing will remain for your companions. What kept us from this was not reluctance for reward nor cowardice before the enemy; we merely stood our ground to protect you, fearing that the enemy might come upon you from behind." So they disputed, and the Qur'an came down: {They ask you about the spoils of war. Say: the spoils of war belong to God and the Messenger}. He said: and the Qur'an also came down: {And know that whatever spoils you have taken, a fifth of it belongs to God [and to the Messenger]} to the end of the verse [al-Anfal: 41].

The Imam Abu Ubayd al-Qasim ibn Sallam, may God have mercy on him, said in his book "al-Amwal al-Shar'iyyah wa Bayan Jihatiha wa Masarifiha" (Lawful Wealth and an Explanation of Its Categories and Channels of Disbursement): As for al-anfal, these are the spoils of war, everything the Muslims gain from the wealth of the people at war with them. The first spoils of war belonged to the Prophet ﷺ, as God Almighty says: {They ask you about the spoils of war. Say: the spoils of war belong to God and the Messenger}. He then divided them on the day of Badr according to what God willed, without taking out a fifth, as we have mentioned in the hadith of Sa'd. Then afterward the verse of the fifth was revealed, and it abrogated the earlier ruling.

I (Ibn Kathir) say: this is exactly how Ali ibn Abi Talhah related it from Ibn Abbas. Mujahid, Ikrimah, and al-Suddi said the same.

Ibn Zayd said: it is not abrogated; rather it stands as an established ruling (muhkamah).

Abu Ubayd said: there are reports on this matter. The spoils of war in their basic sense mean the collected booty, except that the fifth of it is specifically designated for those entitled to it, as the Book states and the Sunnah confirms in practice. The meaning of al-anfal in the speech of the Arabs is: any favor a person does out of generosity, without it being obligatory upon him. This is the nafl that God permitted the believers to take from the wealth of their enemy. It is something God singled out for them as a bestowal from Himself, given that spoils of war had been forbidden to the nations before them. God then granted this nation the spoils as a special gift, and this is the basic meaning of nafl.

I (Ibn Kathir) say: a supporting proof of this is found in the two Sahihs, from Jabir, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I have been given five things which no one before me was given." He then related the hadith, up to where he said: "and the spoils of war were made lawful for me, and were not made lawful for anyone before me," and he related the rest of the hadith.

Abu Ubayd then said: this is why what the leader (imam) grants to the fighters is called nafl, meaning his giving preference to some of the army over others with something in addition to their shares, doing so according to the degree of benefit they provided to Islam and the harm they inflicted on the enemy. Regarding the nafl that the leader grants, there are four established practices (sunan), each having its own distinct context.

The first: nafl in which there is no fifth taken out, and that is the slain enemy's personal effects (al-salab).

The second: nafl that comes from the spoils after the fifth has been removed, which is when the leader sends out raiding detachments into enemy territory; they bring back spoils, and the detachment receives a fourth or a third of what it brought, after the fifth has been taken out.

The third: nafl from the fifth itself, which is when the entire body of spoils is gathered and then the fifth is taken from it; once the fifth is in the hand of the leader, he grants from it according to what he sees fit.

The fourth: nafl from the total spoils before any fifth has been taken out of it at all, which is when guides, herdsmen of the livestock, and drivers of it are given something. In all of this there is disagreement among scholars.

Al-Rabi' said: al-Shafi'i said: al-anfal means that nothing is taken out from the total spoils before the fifth except the slain enemy's personal effects.

Abu Ubayd said: the second type of nafl is something added to what the fighters were already entitled to, and it comes from the Prophet's ﷺ own fifth, for he was entitled to a fifth of the fifth from every spoil taken. It is fitting for the leader to exercise judgment: when the enemy is numerous and their strength is great, and those facing them among the Muslims are few, he should grant additional shares from it, following the practice of the Messenger of God ﷺ; and when that is not the case, he should not grant such additional shares.

The third type of nafl: when the leader sends out a raiding detachment or an army, and says to them before the encounter, "whoever gains spoils shall have such and such after the fifth," then that belongs to them according to what the leader stipulated, because it was on that basis that they went out to fight, and it was that to which they agreed. End of his statement.

Regarding what he said earlier, namely his statement that "the spoils of Badr were not subjected to a fifth," there is room for reconsideration. It is contradicted by the hadith of Ali ibn Abi Talib concerning his two young she-camels which he obtained from the fifth on the day of Badr. I have explained this matter with a full and satisfying clarification in the Book of the Sirah, and to God belongs praise [and grace].

As for His saying, Almighty: {so fear God and set right the matter between you}, meaning: fear God in your affairs, and set right what is between you; do not wrong one another, do not dispute, and do not quarrel, for what God has given you of guidance and knowledge is better than whatever you might dispute over because of it. {And obey God and His Messenger}, meaning: in his division of it among you according to what God willed, for he divided it as God commanded him, with justice and fairness.

Ibn Abbas said: this is a solemn charge from God upon the believers, that they should fear [God] and set right the matter between them. Mujahid said the same.

Al-Suddi said: {so fear God and set right the matter between you} means: do not revile one another. We mention here a hadith recorded by the Hafiz Abu Ya'la Ahmad ibn Ali ibn al-Muthanna al-Mawsili, may God have mercy on him, in his Musnad, where he said: [chain] Anas, may God be pleased with him, said: While the Messenger of God ﷺ was sitting, we suddenly saw him laugh until his front teeth showed. Umar said: "What has made you laugh, O Messenger of God, may my father and mother be sacrificed for you?" He said: "Two men from my nation knelt before the Lord of Might, blessed and exalted is He, and one of them said: 'O Lord, take for me my due from my brother who wronged me.' God Almighty said: 'Give your brother what is due to him.' He said: 'O Lord, nothing remains of my good deeds.' He said: 'My Lord, then let him carry some of my burdens instead.'" He said: and the eyes of the Messenger of God ﷺ overflowed with tears, then he said: "That is indeed a mighty day, a day when people will need someone to carry away some of their burdens for them." Then God Almighty said to the one seeking his due: "Raise your eyes and look into the gardens of Paradise." He raised his head and said: "O Lord, I see cities of silver and palaces of gold crowned with pearls: for which prophet is this? For which truthful one (siddiq) is this? For which martyr is this?" He said: "This belongs to whoever pays the price for it." He said: "O Lord, and who can possess that?" He said: "You can possess it." He said: "By what, O Lord?" He said: "By pardoning your brother." He said: "O Lord, then I have pardoned him." God Almighty said: "Take your brother by the hand and bring him into Paradise."

Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "So fear Allah and set right the state of affairs between yourselves, for Allah, exalted is He, will set right the affairs between the believers on the Day of Resurrection."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الْأَنْفَالِ

وَهِيَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ آيَاتُهَا سَبْعُونَ وَسِتُّ آيَاتٍ كَلِمَاتُهَا أَلْفُ كَلِمَةٍ، وَسِتُّمِائَةِ كَلِمَةٍ، وَإِحْدَى وَثَلَاثُونَ كَلِمَةً، حُرُوفُهَا خَمْسَةُ آلَافٍ وَمِائَتَانِ، وَأَرْبَعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ حَرْفًا، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ الْأَنْفَالُ: الْغَنَائِمُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحِيمِ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، أَخْبَرَنَا هُشَيْم، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، قَالَ: قُلْتُ لِابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: سُورَةُ الْأَنْفَالِ؟ قَالَ نَزَلَتْ فِي بَدْرٍ.

أَمَّا مَا عَلَّقه عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، فَكَذَلِكَ رَوَاهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "الْأَنْفَالُ": الْغَنَائِمُ، كَانَتْ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَالِصَةً، لَيْسَ لِأَحَدٍ مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَعَطَاءٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَعَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وَمُقَاتِلِ بْنِ حَيَّان، وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ إِنَّهَا الْغَنَائِمُ 

وَقَالَ الْكَلْبِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: الْأَنْفَالُ: الْغَنَائِمُ، قَالَ فِيهَا لَبِيدُ: إِنَّ تَقْوَى رَبّنَا خيرُ نَفَلوَبِإِذْنِ اللهِ رَيثي وَعَجَلْ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي مَالِكُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَجُلًا يَسْأَلُ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ عَنِ "الْأَنْفَالِ"، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: الْفَرَسُ مِنَ النَّفل، وَالسَّلَبُ مِنَ النَّفَلِ. ثُمَّ عَادَ لِمَسْأَلَتِهِ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ ذَلِكَ أَيْضًا. ثُمَّ قَالَ الرَّجُلُ: الْأَنْفَالُ الَّتِي قَالَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ مَا هِيَ؟ قَالَ الْقَاسِمُ: فَلَمْ يَزَلْ يَسْأَلُهُ حَتَّى كَادَ يُحرجه، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَتَدْرُونَ مَا مِثْلُ هَذَا، مِثْلُ صَبِيغٍ الَّذِي ضَرَبَهُ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَرٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ قال: قال ابن عباس: كان عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، إِذَا سُئِلَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ قَالَ: لَا آمُرُكَ وَلَا أَنْهَاكَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَاللَّهِ مَا بَعَثَ اللَّهُ نَبِيَّهُ ﷺ إِلَّا زَاجِرًا آمِرًا مُحِلًّا مُحَرِّمًا. قَالَ الْقَاسِمُ: فَسُلِّطَ عَلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ رَجُلٌ يَسْأَلُهُ عَنِ الْأَنْفَالِ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ الرَّجُلُ يَنْفُلُ فَرَسَ الرَّجُلِ وَسِلَاحَهُ. فَأَعَادَ عَلَيْهِ الرَّجُلُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ أَعَادَ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى أَغْضَبَهُ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَتَدْرُونَ مَا مِثْلُ هَذَا؟ مِثْلُ صَبِيغ الَّذِي ضَرَبَهُ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ، حَتَّى سَالَتِ الدِّمَاءُ عَلَى عَقِبَيْهِ -أَوْ عَلَى: رِجْلَيْهِ فَقَالَ الرَّجُلُ: أَمَّا أَنْتَ فَقَدِ انْتَقَمَ اللَّهُ لِعُمَرَ مِنْكَ 

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ إِلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُ فَسَّرَ النَّفَلَ بِمَا يَنْفُلُهُ الْإِمَامُ لِبَعْضِ الْأَشْخَاصِ مِنْ سَلَبٍ أَوْ نَحْوِهِ، بَعْدَ قَسْمِ أَصْلِ الْمَغْنَمِ، وَهُوَ الْمُتَبَادِرُ إِلَى فَهْمِ كَثِيرٍ مِنَ الْفُقَهَاءِ مِنْ لَفْظِ النَّفَلِ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: إِنَّهُمْ سَأَلُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنِ الْخُمُسِ بَعْدَ الْأَرْبَعَةِ الْأَخْمَاسِ، فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ﴾ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ وَمَسْرُوقٌ: لَا نَفَلَ يَوْمَ الزَّحْفِ، إِنَّمَا النَّفَلُ قَبْلَ الْتِقَاءِ الصُّفُوفِ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْهُمَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ أَبِي رَبَاحٍ: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ﴾ قَالَ: يَسْأَلُونَكَ فِيمَا شَذَّ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ إِلَى الْمُسْلِمِينَ فِي غَيْرِ قِتَالٍ، مِنْ دَابَّةٍ أَوْ عَبْدٍ أَوْ أَمَةٍ أَوْ مَتَاعٍ، فَهُوَ نَفَلٌ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ يَصْنَعُ بِهِ مَا يَشَاءُ.

وَهَذَا يَقْتَضِي أَنَّهُ فَسَّرَ الْأَنْفَالَ بِالْفَيْءِ، وَهُوَ مَا أُخِذَ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ مِنْ غَيْرِ قِتَالٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: هِيَ أَنْفَالُ السَّرَايَا، حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ العزيز، حدثنا علي بن صالح بن حيي قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ﴾ قَالَ: السَّرَايَا.

وَيَعْنِي هَذَا: مَا يَنْفُلُهُ الْإِمَامُ لِبَعْضِ السَّرَايَا زِيَادَةً عَلَى قَسْمِهِمْ مَعَ بَقِيَّةِ

الْجَيْشِ، وَقَدْ صَرَّحَ بِذَلِكَ الشَّعْبِيُّ، وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّهَا الزِّيَادَاتُ عَلَى الْقَسْمِ، وَيَشْهَدُ لِذَلِكَ مَا وَرَدَ فِي سَبَبِ نُزُولِ الْآيَةِ، وَهُوَ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ الشَّيْبَانِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الثَّقَفِيِّ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ أَبِي وَقَّاصٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ، وَقُتِلَ أَخِي عُمَيْر، وَقَتَلْتُ سَعِيدَ بْنَ الْعَاصِ وَأَخَذْتُ سَيْفَهُ، وَكَانَ يُسَمَّى "ذَا الْكَتِيفَةِ"، فَأَتَيْتُ بِهِ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ: "اذْهَبْ فَاطْرَحْهُ فِي الْقَبَضِ". قَالَ: فَرَجَعْتُ وَبِي مَا لَا يَعْلَمُهُ إِلَّا اللَّهُ مِنْ قَتْلِ أَخِي وَأَخْذِ سَلَبِي. قَالَ: فَمَا جَاوَزْتُ إِلَّا يَسِيرًا حَتَّى نَزَلَتْ سُورَةُ الْأَنْفَالِ، فَقَالَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "اذهب فخذ سيفك" وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَسْوَدُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ أَبِي النَّجود، عَنْ مُصْعَبِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: قَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَدْ شَفَانِي اللَّهُ الْيَوْمَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، فَهَبْ لِي هَذَا السَّيْفَ. فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ هَذَا السَّيْفَ لَا لَكَ وَلَا لِي، ضَعْهُ" قَالَ: فَوَضَعْتُهُ، ثُمَّ رَجَعْتُ، قُلْتُ: عَسَى أَنْ يُعْطَى هَذَا السَّيْفُ الْيَوْمَ مَنْ لَا يُبْلِي بَلَائِي! قَالَ: رَجُلٌ يَدْعُونِي مِنْ وَرَائِي، قَالَ: قُلْتُ: قَدْ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِيَّ شَيْئًا؟ قَالَ: "كُنْتَ سَأَلْتَنِي السَّيْفَ، وَلَيْسَ هُوَ لِي وَإِنَّهُ قَدْ وُهِبَ لِي، فَهُوَ لَكَ" قَالَ: وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ قُلِ الأنْفَالُ لِلَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ﴾

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ أَبِي [بَكْرِ] بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنَا شُعْبَةُ، أَخْبَرَنَا سِمَاكُ بْنُ حَرْبٍ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ مُصْعَبَ بْنَ سَعْدٍ، يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ سَعْدٍ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فِيَّ أَرْبَعُ آيَاتٍ: أَصَبْتُ سَيْفًا يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فَأَتَيْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقُلْتُ: نَفِّلْنِيه. فَقَالَ: "ضَعْهُ مِنْ حَيْثُ أَخَذْتَهُ" مَرَّتَيْنِ، ثُمَّ عَاوَدْتُهُ فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "ضَعْهُ مِنْ حَيْثُ أَخَذْتَهُ"، فَنَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: "يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْأَنْفَالِ: 

وَتَمَامُ الْحَدِيثِ فِي نُزُولِ: ﴿وَوَصَّيْنَا الإنْسَانَ بِوَالِدَيْهِ حُسْنًا﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ: ٨] وَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا الْخَمْرُ وَالْمَيْسِرُ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٩٠] وَآيَةِ الْوَصِيَّةِ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، عَنْ بَعْضِ بَنِي سَاعِدَةَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا أُسَيْدٍ مَالِكَ بْنَ رَبِيعَةَ يَقُولُ: أَصَبْتُ سَيْفَ ابْنِ عَائِذٍ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَكَانَ السَّيْفُ يُدْعَى بِالْمَرْزُبَانِ، فَلَمَّا أَمْرَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ النَّاسَ أَنْ يَرُدُّوا مَا فِي أَيْدِيهِمْ مِنَ النَّفَلِ، أَقْبَلْتُ بِهِ فَأَلْقَيْتُهُ فِي النَّفَلِ، وَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَا يَمْنَعُ شَيْئًا يُسْأَلُهُ، فَرَآهُ الْأَرْقَمُ بْنُ أَبِي الْأَرْقَمِ الْمَخْزُومِيُّ، فَسَأَلَهُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ [ﷺ] فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ 

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ.

[سَبَبٌ آخَرُ فِي نُزُولِ الْآيَةِ] :

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنْ مَكْحُولٍ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ عُبَادَةَ عَنِ الْأَنْفَالِ، فَقَالَ: فِينَا -أصحاب بدر- نَزَلَتْ، حِينَ اخْتَلَفْنَا فِي النَّفَلِ، وَسَاءَتْ فِيهِ أَخْلَاقُنَا، فَانْتَزَعَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ أَيْدِينَا، وَجَعَلَهُ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَسَمَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ عَنْ بَوَاءٍ -يَقُولُ: عَنْ سَوَاءٍ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَيَّاشِ بْنِ أَبِي رَبِيعَةَ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَّامٍ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ قَالَ: خَرَجْنَا مَعَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَشَهِدْتُ مَعَهُ بَدْرًا، فَالْتَقَى النَّاسُ، فَهَزَمَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] الْعَدُوَّ، فَانْطَلَقَتْ طَائِفَةٌ فِي آثَارِهِمْ يَهْزِمُونَ وَيَقْتُلُونَ، وَأَكَبَّتْ طَائِفَةٌ عَلَى الْعَسْكَرِ يَحْوُونَهُ وَيَجْمَعُونَهُ. وَأَحْدَقَتْ طَائِفَةٌ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَا يُصِيبُ الْعَدُوُّ مِنْهُ غِرَّةً، حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ اللَّيْلُ، وَفَاءَ النَّاسُ بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ، قَالَ الَّذِينَ جَمَعُوا الْغَنَائِمَ: نَحْنُ حَوَيْنَاهَا، فَلَيْسَ لِأَحَدٍ فِيهَا نَصِيبٌ. وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ خَرَجُوا فِي طَلَبِ الْعَدُوِّ: لَسْتُمْ بِأَحَقَّ بِهِ مِنَّا، نَحْنُ مَنَعْنَا عَنْهَا الْعَدُوَّ وَهَزَمْنَاهُمْ. وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ أَحْدَقُوا بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: لَسْتُمْ بِأَحَقَّ مِنَّا، نَحْنُ أَحْدَقْنَا بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَخِفْنَا أَنْ يُصِيبَ الْعَدُوُّ مِنْهُ غِرَّةً، فَاشْتَغَلْنَا بِهِ، فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ قُلِ الأنْفَالُ لِلَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَصْلِحُوا ذَاتَ بَيْنِكُمْ﴾ فَقَسَمَهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ -وَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِذَا غَارَ فِي أَرْضِ الْعَدُوِّ نَفَّلَ الرُّبُعَ، فَإِذَا أَقْبَلَ وَكُلَّ النَّاسِ رَاجِعًا، نَفَّلَ الثُّلُثَ، وَكَانَ يَكْرَهُ الْأَنْفَالَ وَيَقُولُ: "لِيَرُدَّ قَوِيُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى ضَعِيفِهِمْ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بِهِ نَحْوَهُ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ حِبَّانَ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ وَقَالَ الْحَاكِمُ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ عَلَى شَرْطِ مُسْلِمٍ وَلَمْ يُخْرِجَاهُ.

وَرَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ -وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ -وَابْنُ حِبَّانَ، وَالْحَاكِمُ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ صَنَعَ كَذَا وَكَذَا فَلَهُ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَتَسَارَعَ فِي ذَلِكَ شُبَّانُ الرِّجَالِ، وَبَقِيَ الشُّيُوخُ تَحْتَ الرَّايَاتِ، فَلَمَّا كَانَتِ الْمَغَانِمُ، جَاءُوا يَطْلُبُونَ الَّذِي جُعِلَ لَهُمْ، فَقَالَ الشُّيُوخُ: لَا تَسْتَأْثِرُوا عَلَيْنَا، فَإِنَّا كُنَّا رِدْءًا لَكُمْ، لَوِ انْكَشَفْتُمْ لَفِئْتُمْ إِلَيْنَا. فَتَنَازَعُوا فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأَطِيعُوااللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ 

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْكَلْبِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ قَالَ رَسُولُ الله ﷺ: "مَنْ قَتَلَ قَتِيلًا فَلَهُ كَذَا وَكَذَا، وَمَنْ أَتَى بِأَسِيرٍ فَلَهُ كَذَا وَكَذَا". فَجَاءَ أَبُو اليَسَر بِأَسِيرَيْنِ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَعَدْتَنَا، فَقَامَ سَعْدُ بْنُ عُبَادَةَ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنْ أَعْطَيْتَ هَؤُلَاءِ لَمْ يَبْقَ لِأَصْحَابِكَ شَيْءٌ، وَإِنَّهُ لَمْ يَمْنَعْنَا مِنْ هَذَا زَهَادَةٌ فِي الْأَجْرِ، وَلَا جُبْنٌ عَنِ الْعَدُوِّ، وَإِنَّمَا قُمْنَا هَذَا الْمَقَامَ مُحَافَظَةً عَلَيْكَ، نَخَافُ أَنْ يَأْتُوكَ مِنْ وَرَائِكَ، فَتَشَاجَرُوا، وَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ قُلِ الأنْفَالُ لِلَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ﴾ قَالَ: وَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ: ﴿وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّمَا غَنِمْتُمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَأَنَّ للهِ خُمُسَهُ [وَلِلرَّسُولِ] ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ الْآيَةِ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٤١] 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ سَلَّامٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِ "الْأَمْوَالِ الشَّرْعِيَّةِ وَبَيَانِ جِهَاتِهَا وَمَصَارِفِهَا": أَمَّا الْأَنْفَالُ: فَهِيَ الْمَغَانِمُ، وَكُلُّ نَيْلٍ نَالَهُ الْمُسْلِمُونَ مِنْ أَمْوَالِ أَهْلِ الْحَرْبِ، فَكَانَتِ الْأَنْفَالُ الْأُولَى إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الأنْفَالِ قُلِ الأنْفَالُ لِلَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ﴾ فَقَسَمَهَا يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ عَلَى مَا أَرَادَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يُخَمِّسَهَا عَلَى مَا ذَكَرْنَاهُ فِي حَدِيثِ سَعْدٍ، ثُمَّ نَزَلَتْ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ آيَةُ الْخُمُسِ، فَنَسَخَتِ الْأُولَى 

قُلْتُ: هَكَذَا رَوَى عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، سَوَاءً. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ والسُّدِّيّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: لَيْسَتْ مَنْسُوخَةً، بَلْ هِيَ مُحْكَمَةٌ.

قَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: وَفِي ذَلِكَ آثَارٌ، وَالْأَنْفَالُ أَصْلُهَا جَمْعُ الْغَنَائِمِ، إِلَّا أَنَّ الْخُمُسَ مِنْهَا مَخْصُوصٌ لِأَهْلِهِ عَلَى مَا نَزَلَ بِهِ الْكِتَابُ، وَجَرَتْ بِهِ السُّنَّةُ. وَمَعْنَى الْأَنْفَالِ فِي كَلَامِ الْعَرَبِ: كُلُّ إِحْسَانٍ فَعَلَهُ فَاعِلٌ تَفَضُّلًا مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يَجِبَ ذَلِكَ عَلَيْهِ، فَذَلِكَ النَّفَلُ الَّذِي أَحَلَّهُ اللَّهُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ مِنْ أَمْوَالِ عَدُوِّهُمْ وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ شَيْءٌ خَصَّهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ تَطَوُّلًا مِنْهُ عَلَيْهِمْ بَعْدَ أَنْ كَانَتِ الْمَغَانِمُ مُحَرَّمَةً عَلَى الْأُمَمِ قَبْلَهُمْ، فَنَفَلَهَا اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةَ فَهَذَا أَصْلُ النَّفَلِ.

قُلْتُ: شَاهِدُ هَذَا فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ جَابِرٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم قال: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا لَمْ يُعْطَهُنَّ أَحَدٌ قَبْلِي" فَذَكَرَ الْحَدِيثَ، إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: "وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلِي"، وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ 

ثُمَّ قَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: وَلِهَذَا سُمِّيَ مَا جَعَلَ الْإِمَامُ لِلْمُقَاتِلَةِ نَفَلًا وَهُوَ تَفْضِيلُهُ بَعْضَ الْجَيْشِ عَلَى بَعْضٍ بِشَيْءٍ سِوَى سِهَامِهِمْ، يَفْعَلُ ذَلِكَ بِهِمْ عَلَى قَدْرِ الْغَنَاءِ عَنِ الْإِسْلَامِ وَالنِّكَايَةِ فِي الْعَدُوِّ. وَفِي النَّفَلِ الَّذِي يَنْفُلُهُ الْإِمَامُ سُنَنٌ أَرْبَعٌ، لِكُلِّ وَاحِدَةٍ مِنْهُنَّ مَوْضِعٌ غير موضع الأخرى: فَإِحْدَاهُنَّ: فِي النَّفَلِ لَا خُمُسَ فِيهِ، وَذَلِكَ السَّلَبُ.

وَالثَّانِيَةُ: فِي النَّفَلِ الَّذِي يَكُونُ مِنَ الْغَنِيمَةِ بَعْدَ إِخْرَاجِ الْخُمُسِ، وَهُوَ أَنْ يُوَجِّهَ الْإِمَامُ السَّرَايَا فِي أَرْضِ الْحَرْبِ، فَتَأْتِي بِالْغَنَائِمِ فَيَكُونُ لِلسَّرِيَّةِ مِمَّا جَاءَتْ بِهِ الرُّبُعُ أَوِ الثُّلْثُ بَعْدَ الْخُمُسِ.

وَالثَّالِثَةُ: فِي النَّفَلِ مِنَ الْخُمُسِ نَفْسِهِ، وَهُوَ أَنْ تُحَازَ الْغَنِيمَةُ كُلُّهَا، ثُمَّ تُخَمَّسُ، فَإِذَا صَارَ الْخُمُسُ فِي يَدَيِ الْإِمَامِ نَفَلَ مِنْهُ عَلَى قَدْرِ مَا يَرَى.

وَالرَّابِعَةُ: فِي النَّفَلِ فِي جُمْلَةِ الْغَنِيمَةِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يُخَمَّسَ مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ، وَهُوَ أَنْ يُعْطَى الْأَدِلَّاءُ وَرُعَاةُ الْمَاشِيَةِ والسَّوَّاق لَهَا، وَفِي كُلِّ ذَلِكَ اخْتِلَافٌ.

قَالَ الرَّبِيعُ: قَالَ الشَّافِعِيُّ: الْأَنْفَالُ: أَلَّا يَخْرُجَ مِنْ رَأْسِ الْغَنِيمَةِ قَبْلَ الْخُمُسِ شَيْءٌ غَيْرُ السَّلَبِ.

قَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: وَالْوَجْهُ الثَّانِي مِنَ النَّفَلِ هُوَ شَيْءٌ زِيدُوهُ غَيْرَ الَّذِي كَانَ لَهُمْ، وَذَلِكَ مِنْ خُمُسِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ؛ فَإِنَّ لَهُ خُمُسَ الْخُمُسِ مِنْ كُلِّ غَنِيمَةٍ، فَيَنْبَغِي لِلْإِمَامِ أَنْ يَجْتَهِدَ، فَإِذَا كَثُرَ الْعَدُوُّ وَاشْتَدَّتْ شَوْكَتُهُمْ، وَقَلَّ مَنْ بِإِزَائِهِ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، نَفَلَ مِنْهُ اتِّبَاعًا لِسُنَّةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَإِذَا لَمْ يَكُنْ ذَلِكَ لَمْ يَنْفُلْ.

وَالْوَجْهُ الثَّالِثُ مِنَ النَّفَلِ: إِذَا بَعَثَ الْإِمَامُ سَرِيَّةً أَوْ جَيْشًا، فَقَالَ لَهُمْ قَبْلَ اللِّقَاءِ: مَنْ غَنِمَ شَيْئًا فَلَهُ بَعْدَ الْخُمُسِ، فَذَلِكَ لَهُمْ عَلَى مَا شَرَطَ الْإِمَامُ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ غَزَوْا، وَبِهِ رَضُوا. انْتَهَى كَلَامُهُ 

وَفِيمَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ كَلَامِهِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: "إِنَّ غَنَائِمَ بَدْرٍ لَمْ تُخَمَّسْ"، نَظَرٌ. وَيَرُدُّ عَلَيْهِ حَدِيثُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ فِي شَارِفَيْهِ اللَّذَيْنِ حَصَلَا لَهُ مِنَ الْخُمُسِ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَقَدْ بَيَّنْتُ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابِ السِّيرَةِ بَيَانًا شَافِيًا وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ [وَالْمِنَّةُ] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَصْلِحُوا ذَاتَ بَيْنِكُمْ﴾ أَي: اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ فِي أُمُورِكُمْ، وَأَصْلِحُوا فِيمَا بَيْنَكُمْ وَلَا تَظَالَمُوا وَلَا تَخَاصَمُوا وَلَا تَشَاجَرُوا؛ فَمَا آتَاكُمُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْعِلْمِ خَيْرٌ مِمَّا تَخْتَصِمُونَ بِسَبَبِهِ، ﴿وَأَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي قَسْمِهِ بَيْنَكُمْ عَلَى مَا أَرَادَهُ اللَّهُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَسَّمَهُ كَمَا أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْعَدْلِ وَالْإِنْصَافِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هَذَا تَحْرِيجٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ يَتَّقُوا [اللَّهَ] وَيُصْلِحُوا ذَاتَ بَيْنِهِمْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَصْلِحُوا ذَاتَ بَيْنِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَا تَسْتَبُّوا. وَنَذْكُرُ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثًا أَوْرَدَهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْمُثَنَّى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا مجاهد بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ بَكْرٍ حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادُ بْنُ شَيْبَةَ الْحَبَطِيُّ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: بَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَالِسٌ، إِذْ رَأَيْنَاهُ ضَحِكَ حَتَّى بَدَتْ ثَنَايَاهُ، فَقَالَ عُمَرُ: مَا أَضْحَكَكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ بِأَبِي أَنْتَ وَأُمِّي؟ فَقَالَ: "رَجُلَانِ جَثَيَا مِنْ أُمَّتِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رَبِّ الْعِزَّةِ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، فَقَالَ أَحَدُهُمَا: يَا رَبِّ، خُذْ لِي مَظْلَمَتِي مِنْ أَخِي. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: أَعْطِ أَخَاكَ مَظْلَمَتَكَ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، لَمْ يَبْقَ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِي شَيْءٌ. قَالَ: رَبِّ، فَلْيَحْمِلْ عَنِّي مِنْ أَوْزَارِي" قَالَ: وَفَاضَتْ عَيْنَا رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالْبُكَاءِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَيَوْمٌ عَظِيمٌ، يَوْمٌ يَحْتَاجُ النَّاسُ إِلَى مَنْ يَتَحَمَّلُ عَنْهُمْ مِنْ أَوْزَارِهِمْ، فَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِلطَّالِبِ: ارْفَعْ بَصَرَكَ فَانْظُرْ فِي الْجِنَانِ، فَرَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ فَقَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، أَرَى مَدَائِنَ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ وَقُصُورًا مِنْ ذَهَبٍ مُكَلَّلَةً بِاللُّؤْلُؤِ، لِأَيِّ نَبِيٍّ هَذَا؟ لِأَيِّ صِدِّيقٍ هَذَا؟ لِأَيِّ شَهِيدٍ هَذَا؟ قَالَ: هَذَا لِمَنْ أَعْطَى الثَّمَنَ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، وَمَنْ يَمْلِكُ ذَلِكَ؟ قَالَ: أَنْتَ تَمْلِكُهُ. قَالَ: مَاذَا يَا رَبِّ؟ قَالَ: تَعْفُو عَنْ أَخِيكَ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، فَإِنِّي قَدْ عَفَوْتُ عَنْهُ. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: خُذْ بِيَدِ أَخِيكَ فَأَدْخِلْهُ الْجَنَّةَ". ثُمَّ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَصْلِحُوا ذَاتَ بَيْنِكُمْ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يُصْلِحُ بَيْنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ"

---

## 8:2-4 — verses 2-4 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying: {The believers are only those who, when God is mentioned, their hearts tremble}: he said, the hypocrites, nothing of the remembrance of God enters their hearts when performing His obligatory duties, they do not believe in any of God's signs, they do not place their trust in Him, they do not pray when they are unseen, and they do not pay the zakat on their wealth. So God Most High informed that they are not believers, then He described the believers, saying: {The believers are only those who, when God is mentioned, their hearts tremble}, meaning they fulfill His obligatory duties. {And when His verses are recited to them, it increases them in faith}, meaning in affirmation, {and upon their Lord they rely}, meaning they hope in none other than Him.

Mujahid said: {their hearts tremble} means they are struck with fright, that is, they are alarmed and afraid. Al-Suddi and more than one other said the same.

This is the description of the true believer, the one who, when God is mentioned, his heart trembles, that is, he fears Him, and so he carries out His commands and abstains from what He has forbidden. This is like His saying: {And those who, when they commit an indecency or wrong themselves, remember God and seek forgiveness for their sins, and who forgives sins except God, and do not persist in what they have done while they know} [Al Imran: 135], and like His saying: {But as for one who feared the standing before his Lord and restrained the soul from vain desire, indeed Paradise shall be his abode} [al-Naziat: 40-41]. It is for this reason that Sufyan al-Thawri said: I heard al-Suddi say regarding His saying: {The believers are only those who, when God is mentioned, their hearts tremble}:

He said: this refers to a man who intends to commit wrong, or he said, who resolves upon a sin, and is then told, "fear God," and so his heart trembles.

Al-Thawri also said: [chain] from Umm al-Darda regarding His saying: {The believers are only those who, when God is mentioned, their hearts tremble}. She said: trembling in the heart is like the burning of a palm frond. Do you not feel a shudder from it? He said: yes indeed. She said to me: when you feel that, then call upon God at that moment, for supplication removes it.

Regarding His saying: {And when His verses are recited to them, it increases them in faith, and upon their Lord they rely}, this is like His saying: {And whenever a surah is revealed, there are some of them who say, "Which of you has this increased in faith?" As for those who believe, it increases them in faith, and they rejoice} [al-Tawbah: 124].

Al-Bukhari and other imams have used this verse and similar ones as evidence for the increase of faith and its variation in degree among hearts, as is the position of the majority of the community. Indeed, more than one imam has reported a consensus on this, such as al-Shafii, Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and Abu Ubayd, as we have explained exhaustively at the beginning of the commentary on al-Bukhari. Praise and grace belong to God.

{and upon their Lord they rely}, that is, they hope in none but Him, they intend none but Him, they take refuge in none but His presence, they seek their needs from none but Him, they desire none but Him, and they know that whatever He wills comes to be and whatever He does not will does not come to be, and that He alone disposes of the dominion, with no partner, and that there is no one who can overturn His decree, and that He is swift in reckoning. It is for this reason that Said ibn Jubayr said: reliance upon God is the sum total of faith.

Regarding His saying: {those who establish prayer and spend from what We have provided them}, He draws attention here to their deeds after having mentioned their belief. These deeds encompass all types of good. This is the establishment of prayer, which is the right of God Most High.

Qatadah said: the establishment of prayer means maintaining its prescribed times, its ablution, its bowing, and its prostration.

Muqatil ibn Hayyan said: its establishment means maintaining its prescribed times, performing complete purification for it, completing its bowing and prostration, reciting the Qur'an within it, and the testimony of faith and the invocation of blessing upon the Prophet ﷺ. This is its establishment.

Spending from what God has provided them encompasses the disbursement of zakat and all other rights owed to God's servants, whether obligatory or recommended. All creation are the dependents of God, and the most beloved of them to God is the one most beneficial to His creation.

Qatadah said regarding His saying {and from what We have provided them, they spend}: spend from what God has given you, for indeed these wealths are loans and deposits entrusted to you, O son of Adam, and you are soon to part from them.

Regarding His saying {those are the true believers}, that is, those characterized by these attributes are the believers in the true sense of faith.

The hadith master Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] from al-Harith ibn Malik al-Ansari, that he passed by the Messenger of God ﷺ, who said to him: "How did you wake up this morning, O Harith?" He said: I woke up as a true believer. He said: "Consider what you are saying, for everything has a reality, so what is the reality of your faith?" He said: my soul has turned away from this world, so I have kept myself awake at night and thirsty by day, and it is as though I see the Throne of my Lord manifest before me, and it is as though I see the people of Paradise visiting one another within it, and it is as though I see the people of the Fire wailing within it. He said: "O Harith, you have recognized it, so hold fast to it," three times.

Amr ibn Murrah said regarding His saying {those are the true believers}: the Qur'an was revealed only in the language of the Arabs, as when you say: "so-and-so is truly a chief," while there are chiefs among the people; "so-and-so is truly a merchant," while there are merchants among the people; "so-and-so is truly a poet," while there are poets among the people.

Regarding His saying {theirs are ranks with their Lord}, that is, stations, positions, and ranks within the Gardens, as He says: {they are in ranks with God, and God is All-Seeing of what they do} [Al Imran: 163].

{and forgiveness}, that is, He forgives them their evil deeds and rewards them for their good deeds.

Al-Dahhak said regarding His saying {theirs are ranks with their Lord}: the people of Paradise are some above others, so the one above sees his superiority over the one below him, while the one below does not perceive that anyone has been given superiority over him.

It is for this reason that it is reported in the two Sahihs that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Indeed the people of the highest ranks (Illiyyin) will be seen by those below them just as you see a lingering star in one of the horizons of the sky." They said: O Messenger of God, are those the stations of the prophets, which none but they can attain? He said: "Indeed yes, and by Him in whose hand is my soul, they are men who believed in God and affirmed the truth of the messengers."

And in the other hadith, which Imam Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan collected from the hadith of Atiyyah, from Abu Said, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Indeed the people of Paradise will look upon those of the highest ranks just as you see a lingering star in the horizon of the sky, and indeed Abu Bakr and Umar are among them, and how excellent they are."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الَّذِينَ إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: الْمُنَافِقُونَ لَا يَدْخُلُ قُلُوبُهُمْ شَيْءٌ مِنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ عِنْدَ أَدَاءِ فَرَائِضِهِ، وَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ، وَلَا يَتَوَكَّلُونَ، وَلَا يُصَلُّونَ إِذَا غَابُوا، وَلَا يُؤَدُّونَ زَكَاةَ أَمْوَالِهِمْ، فَأَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ لَيْسُوا بِمُؤْمِنِينَ، ثُمَّ وَصَفَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّمَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الَّذِينَ إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ فَأَدَّوْا فَرَائِضَهُ. ﴿وَإِذَا تُلِيَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتُهُ زَادَتْهُمْ إِيمَانًا﴾ يَقُولُ: تَصْدِيقًا ﴿وَعَلَى رَبِّهِمْ يَتَوَكَّلُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: لَا يَرْجُونَ غَيْرَهُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ فَرِقَتْ، أَيْ: فَزِعَتْ وَخَافَتْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَهَذِهِ صِفَةُ الْمُؤْمِنِ حَقَّ الْمُؤْمِنِ، الَّذِي إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَ قَلْبُهُ، أَيْ: خَافَ مِنْهُ، فَفَعَلَ أَوَامِرَهُ، وَتَرَكَ زَوَاجِرَهُ. كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ إِذَا فَعَلُوا فَاحِشَةً أَوْ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ ذَكَرُوا اللَّهَ فَاسْتَغْفَرُوا لِذُنُوبِهِمْ وَمَنْ يَغْفِرُ الذُّنُوبَ إِلا اللَّهُ وَلَمْ يُصِرُّوا عَلَى مَا فَعَلُوا وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٣٥] وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَمَّا مَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّهِ وَنَهَى النَّفْسَ عَنِ الْهَوَى فَإِنَّ الْجَنَّةَ هِيَ الْمَأْوَى﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ: ٤٠، ٤١] وَلِهَذَا قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ: سَمِعْتُ السُّدِّيَّ يَقُولُ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الَّذِينَ إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾

قَالَ: هُوَ الرَّجُلُ يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَظْلِمَ -أَوْ قَالَ: يَهُمُّ بِمَعْصِيَةٍ-فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: اتَّقِ اللَّهَ فَيجل قَلْبُهُ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ أَيْضًا: عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ خُثَيْمٍ، عَنْ شَهْرِ بْنِ حَوْشَبٍ، عَنْ أُمِّ الدَّرْدَاءِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّمَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الَّذِينَ إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ قَالَتْ: الْوَجَلُ فِي الْقَلْبِ إِحْرَاقُ السَّعَفَةِ، أَمَا تَجِدُ لَهُ قُشَعْرِيرَةً؟ قَالَ: بَلَى. قَالَتْ لِي: إِذَا وَجَدْتَ ذَلِكَ فَادْعُ اللَّهَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، فَإِنَّ الدُّعَاءَ يُذْهِبُ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذَا تُلِيَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتُهُ زَادَتْهُمْ إِيمَانًا [وَعَلَى رَبِّهِمْ يَتَوَكَّلُونَ] ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا مَا أُنزلَتْ سُورَةٌ فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقُولُ أَيُّكُمْ زَادَتْهُ هَذِهِ إِيمَانًا فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فَزَادَتْهُمْ إِيمَانًا وَهُمْ يَسْتَبْشِرُونَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ١٢٤]

وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ وَأَشْبَاهِهَا، عَلَى زِيَادَةِ الْإِيمَانِ وَتَفَاضُلِهِ فِي الْقُلُوبِ، كَمَا هُوَ مَذْهَبُ جُمْهُورِ الْأُمَّةِ، بَلْ قَدْ حَكَى الْإِجْمَاعَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ، كَالشَّافِعِيِّ، وَأَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ، وَأَبِي عُبَيْدٍ، كَمَا بَيَّنَّا ذَلِكَ مُسْتَقْصًى فِي أَوَّلِ الشَّرْحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

﴿وَعَلَى رَبِّهِمْ يَتَوَكَّلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَرْجُونَ سِوَاهُ، وَلَا يَقْصِدُونَ إِلَّا إِيَّاهُ، وَلَا يَلُوذُونَ إِلَّا بِجَنَابِهِ، وَلَا يَطْلُبُونَ الْحَوَائِجَ إِلَّا مِنْهُ، وَلَا يَرْغَبُونَ إِلَّا إِلَيْهِ، وَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ مَا شَاءَ كَانَ، وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ، وَأَنَّهُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي الْمُلْكِ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَلَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، وَهُوَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: التَّوَكُّلُ عَلَى اللَّهِ جِمَاعُ الْإِيمَانِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿الَّذِينَ يُقِيمُونَ الصَّلاةَ وَمِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ يُنْفِقُونَ﴾ يُنَبِّهُ بِذَلِكَ عَلَى أَعْمَالِهِمْ، بَعْدَ مَا ذَكَرَ اعْتِقَادَهُمْ، وَهَذِهِ الْأَعْمَالُ تَشْمَلُ أَنْوَاعَ الْخَيْرِ كُلَّهَا، وَهُوَ إِقَامَةُ الصَّلَاةِ، وَهُوَ حَقُّ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: إِقَامَةُ الصَّلَاةِ: الْمُحَافَظَةُ عَلَى مَوَاقِيتِهَا وَوُضُوئِهَا، وَرُكُوعِهَا، وَسُجُودِهَا.

وَقَالَ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّان: إِقَامَتُهَا: الْمُحَافَظَةُ عَلَى مَوَاقِيتِهَا، وَإِسْبَاغُ الطُّهُورِ فِيهَا، وَتَمَامُ رُكُوعِهَا وَسُجُودِهَا، وَتِلَاوَةُ الْقُرْآنِ فِيهَا، وَالتَّشَهُّدُ وَالصَّلَاةُ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، هَذَا إِقَامَتُهَا.

وَالْإِنْفَاقُ مِمَّا رَزَقَهُمُ اللَّهُ يَشْمَلُ خَرَاجَ الزَّكَاةِ، وَسَائِرَ الْحُقُوقِ لِلْعِبَادِ مِنْ وَاجِبٍ وَمُسْتَحَبٍّ، وَالْخَلْقُ كُلُّهُمْ عِيَالُ اللَّهِ، فَأَحَبُّهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ أَنْفَعُهُمْ لِخَلْقِهِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ ﴿وَمِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ يُنْفِقُونَ﴾ فَأَنْفِقُوا مِمَّا أَعْطَاكُمُ اللَّهُ، فَإِنَّمَا هَذِهِ الْأَمْوَالَ عَوَارِيٌّ وَوَدَائِعُ عِنْدَكَ يَا ابْنَ آدَمَ، أَوْشَكْتَ أَنْ تُفَارِقَهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ حَقًّا﴾ أَي: الْمُتَّصِفُونَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ هم المؤمنون حق الإيمان.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْحَضْرَمِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْب، حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ الحُبَاب، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعَة، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ السَّكْسَكِيّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي هِلَالٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ أَبِي الْجَهْمِ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ؛ أَنَّهُ مَرَّ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ لَهُ: "كَيْفَ أَصْبَحْتَ يَا حَارِثُ؟ " قَالَ: أَصْبَحْتُ مُؤْمِنًا حَقًّا. قَالَ: "انْظُرْ مَاذَا تَقُولُ، فَإِنَّ لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ حَقِيقَةً، فَمَا حَقِيقَةُ إِيمَانِكَ؟ " فَقَالَ: عَزَفَت نَفْسِي عَنِ الدُّنْيَا، فَأَسْهَرْتُ لَيْلِي، وَأَظْمَأْتُ نَهَارِي، وَكَأَنِّي أَنْظُرُ إِلَى عَرْشِ رَبِّي بَارِزًا، وَكَأَنِّي أَنْظُرُ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ يَتَزَاوَرُونَ فِيهَا، وَكَأَنِّي أَنْظُرُ إِلَى أَهْلِ النَّارِ يَتَضاغَوْن فِيهَا، فَقَالَ: "يَا حَارِثُ، عَرَفْتَ فَالْزَمْ" ثَلَاثًا 

وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ مُرَّة فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ حَقًّا﴾ إِنَّمَا أُنزلَ الْقُرْآنُ بِلِسَانِ الْعَرَبِ، كَقَوْلِكَ: فُلَانٌ سَيِّدٌ حَقًّا، وَفِي الْقَوْمِ سَادَةٌ، وَفُلَانٌ تَاجِرٌ حَقًّا، وَفِي الْقَوْمِ تُجَّارٌ، وَفُلَانٌ شَاعِرٌ حَقًّا، وَفِي الْقَوْمِ شُعَرَاءُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَهُمْ دَرَجَاتٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مَنَازِلُ وَمَقَامَاتٌ وَدَرَجَاتٌ فِي الْجَنَّاتِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هُمْ دَرَجَاتٌ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٦٣]

﴿وَمَغْفِرَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: يَغْفِرُ لَهُمُ السَّيِّئَاتِ، وَيَشْكُرُ لَهُمُ الْحَسَنَاتِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَهُمْ دَرَجَاتٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ بَعْضُهُمْ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ، فَيَرَى الَّذِي هُوَ فَوْقُ فَضْلَهُ عَلَى الَّذِي هُوَ أَسْفَلُ مِنْهُ، وَلَا يَرَى الَّذِي هُوَ أسفلُ أَنَّهُ فُضّل عَلَيْهِ أَحَدٌ.

وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ أَهْلَ علِّيين لَيَرَاهُمْ مَنْ أَسْفَلُ مِنْهُمْ كَمَا تَرَوْنَ الْكَوْكَبَ الْغَابِرَ فِي أُفُقٍ مِنْ آفَاقِ السَّمَاءِ"، قَالُوا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، تِلْكَ مَنَازِلُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، لَا يَنَالُهَا غَيْرُهُمْ؟ فَقَالَ: "بَلَى، وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ رِجَالٌ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَصَدَّقُوا الْمُرْسَلِينَ" 

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ [وَ] أَهْلُ السُّنَنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَطية، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ لَيَتَرَاءَوْنَ أَهْلَ الدَّرَجَاتِ الْعُلَى كَمَا تَرَوْنَ الْكَوْكَبَ الْغَابِرَ فِي أُفُقِ السَّمَاءِ، وَإِنَّ أَبَا بَكْرٍ وَعُمَرَ مِنْهُمْ وأنْعَمَا"

---

## 8:5-8 — verses 5-8 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Imam Abu Ja'far al-Tabari said: The commentators differed regarding the reason that brought about this "kaf" (the letter/particle of comparison) in His statement: {Just as your Lord brought you out} Some of them said: it was likened, in terms of what is beneficial for the believers, to their fear of their Lord, their setting right the affairs between them, and their obedience to Allah and His Messenger.

Then he related from Ikrimah something similar to this.

The meaning of this is that Allah, Exalted is He, says: Just as when you disputed about the spoils of war and were stingy over them, so Allah took them away from you and made their division His affair and that of His Messenger ﷺ, and He divided them with justice and equity, and this was the complete benefit for you. Likewise, when you disliked going out to face the enemy in the fight against the party possessing strength, that is, the armed force (al-nafir) that went out to defend their religion and to protect their caravan, the outcome of your dislike for fighting was that Allah decreed it for you and brought you together with your enemy without any prior appointment, and it turned out to be right guidance, victory, and conquest, just as He, Exalted is He, said: {Fighting has been prescribed for you while it is hateful to you. But perhaps you hate a thing which is good for you, and perhaps you love a thing which is bad for you. And Allah knows while you know not.} [al-Baqarah: 216]

Ibn Jarir said: Others said: the meaning of this is: {Just as your Lord brought you out of your house in truth} despite the dislike of a group among the believers, so likewise they dislike the fighting, and they are disputing with you about it after it had become clear to them. Then he related something similar to this from Mujahid, that he said: {Just as your Lord brought you out}, meaning: likewise they dispute with you concerning the truth.

Al-Suddi said: Allah revealed, concerning his going out to Badr and their disputing with him, His statement: {Just as your Lord brought you out of your house in truth, while indeed a party among the believers were averse}, seeking out the polytheists, {disputing with you concerning the truth after it had become clear}

Some of them said: they ask you about the spoils of war in a manner of disputation, just as they disputed with you on the day of Badr, saying: You brought us out for the caravan, and you did not inform us of any fighting so that we could prepare for it.

I (Ibn Kathir) say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ had only gone out from Madinah seeking the caravan of Abu Sufyan, news of which had reached him, that it was coming from Syria carrying abundant wealth belonging to Quraysh. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ called upon the Muslims, those who could move quickly, and he went out with three hundred and some odd men, and he headed toward the coast along the road to Badr. Abu Sufyan learned of the Messenger of Allah's ﷺ going out in pursuit of him, so he sent Damdam ibn Amr as a warner to Makkah, and they rose up with nearly a thousand armed men, between nine hundred and a thousand. Abu Sufyan turned the caravan to the right toward the shore of the sea and thus escaped, while the armed force (al-nafir) came and arrived at the water of Badr. Allah brought together the Muslims and the disbelievers without any prior appointment, because of what Allah, Exalted is He, intended: the exaltation of the word of the Muslims and their victory over their enemy, and the separation between truth and falsehood, as will be explained.

The point is that when news of the going out of the armed force (al-nafir) reached the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, Allah revealed to him, promising him one of the two groups: either the caravan or the armed force. Many of the Muslims desired the caravan, because it was gain without fighting, just as He, Exalted is He, said: {And you wished that the one without armed strength would be yours, while Allah intends to establish the truth by His words and to cut off the roots of the disbelievers}

The hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh said in his tafsir: [chain] Aslam Abu Imran narrated to him that he heard Abu Ayyub al-Ansari say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, while we were in Madinah: "I have been informed about the caravan of Abu Sufyan, that it is approaching. What do you think about going out before this caravan, perhaps Allah will grant us it as spoil?" We said: Yes. So he went out and we went out. When we had traveled a day or two, he said to us: "What do you think about fighting the people, for they have been informed of your going out?" We said: No, by Allah, we have no strength to fight the enemy, but we wanted the caravan. Then he said again: "What do you think about fighting the people?" We said the same thing. Then al-Miqdad ibn Amr said: In that case we will not say to you, O Messenger of Allah, as the people of Musa said to Musa: {So go, you and your Lord, and fight; indeed we will sit here} [al-Ma'idah: 24]. He said: So we, the company of the Ansar, wished that we had said what al-Miqdad said, more than that we should have great wealth. He said: So Allah revealed to His Messenger ﷺ: {Just as your Lord brought you out of your house in truth, while indeed a party among the believers were averse} and he mentioned the rest of the hadith.

Ibn Abi Hatim related it from the hadith of Ibn Lahi'ah, similarly.

Ibn Mardawayh also related it from the hadith of Muhammad ibn Amr ibn Alqamah ibn Waqqas al-Laythi, from his father, from his grandfather, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ went out to Badr, until when he was at al-Rawha, he addressed the people and said: "What do you think?" Abu Bakr said: O Messenger of Allah, news has reached us that they are at such and such a place. Then he addressed the people and said: "What do you think?" Umar said the same as Abu Bakr had said. Then he addressed the people and said: "What do you think?" Sa'd ibn Mu'adh said: O Messenger of Allah, is it us you mean? By the One who honored you with the truth and sent down the Book upon you, I have never traveled this road and I have no knowledge of it, but if you were to travel with us until you reached Bark al-Ghimad in Yemen, we would travel with you, and we will not be like those who said to Musa: {So go, you and your Lord, and fight; indeed we will sit here}, but rather: go, you and your Lord, and fight, we are with you both, following. Perhaps you have gone out for one matter, and Allah has brought about something else for you, so look at what Allah has brought about for you and proceed with it. Join the bonds of whomever you wish, and cut the bonds of whomever you wish, and take as enemy whomever you wish, and make peace with whomever you wish, and take from our wealth whatever you wish. So the Qur'an was revealed in accordance with what Sa'd said: {Just as your Lord brought you out of your house in truth, while indeed a party among the believers were averse} to the end of the verses.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: When the Prophet ﷺ consulted about meeting the enemy, and Sa'd ibn Ubadah said to him what he said, and that was on the day of Badr, he ordered the people and they arrayed themselves for battle, and he commanded them regarding the strength of the enemy, so the people of faith disliked that, and Allah revealed: {Just as your Lord brought you out of your house in truth, while indeed a party among the believers were averse, disputing with you concerning the truth after it had become clear, as if they were being driven to death while they were looking on}

Mujahid said: "disputing with you concerning the truth" means: concerning the fighting. Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: {disputing with you concerning the truth [after it had become clear, as if they were being driven to death while they were looking on]}, that is, out of dislike for meeting the polytheists, and denial regarding the march of Quraysh when they were told about them.

Al-Suddi said: {disputing with you concerning the truth after it had become clear} that is, after it had become clear to them that you do nothing except what Allah has commanded you.

Ibn Jarir said: Others said: what is meant by this are the polytheists.

[chain] Ibn Zayd said, concerning His statement: {disputing with you concerning the truth after it had become clear, as if they were being driven to death while they were looking on}: These are the polytheists, they disputed with him concerning the truth, {as if they were being driven to death} when they were called to Islam, {while they were looking on}. He said: This is not a description continuing from what preceded, this is a description beginning anew concerning the people of disbelief.

Then Ibn Jarir said: There is no sense in what he said, because what precedes His statement {disputing with you concerning the truth} is a report about the people of faith, and what follows it is a report about them as well, and the correct view is the statement of Ibn Abbas and Ibn Ishaq, that it is a report about the believers.

This is what Ibn Jarir supported, and it is the truth, and it is what the context of the speech indicates, and Allah knows best.

The Imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: It was said to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ when he had finished with Badr: Go for the caravan, there is nothing to prevent it. Then al-Abbas ibn Abd al-Muttalib called out to him, Abd al-Razzaq said: while he was a captive in his bonds, then they both agreed: It is not proper for you. He said: Why? He said: Because Allah, Mighty and Majestic, only promised you one of the two groups, and He has already given you what He promised you.

A good chain, and it was not related by [any of the compilers, unspecified here].

The meaning of His statement, Exalted is He: {And you wished that the one without armed strength would be yours}

That is: they loved that the party which had no strength, no defense, and no fighting should be theirs, namely the caravan. {And Allah wills to establish the truth by His words} that is, He wills to bring you together with the party that possesses might and combat, so that He may grant you victory over them and make you prevail over them, and manifest His religion, and raise the word of Islam, and make it prevail over all other religions. He is more knowing of the outcomes of matters, and He is the One who ordered your affairs with the excellence of His ordering, even though the servants might love the opposite of that according to what appears to them, just as He, exalted is He, said: {Fighting has been prescribed for you while it is hateful to you. But perhaps you hate a thing while it is good for you, and perhaps you love a thing while it is bad for you, and Allah knows while you do not know} [al-Baqarah: 216].

Muhammad ibn Ishaq, may Allah have mercy on him, said: Muhammad ibn Muslim al-Zuhri, and 'Asim ibn 'Umar ibn Qatadah, and 'Abdullah ibn Abi Bakr, and Yazid ibn Ruman narrated to me, from 'Urwah ibn al-Zubayr and others among our scholars, from 'Abdullah ibn 'Abbas, each of them having narrated to me part of this account, and their accounts came together in what I have compiled regarding the account of Badr, they said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ heard that Abu Sufyan was approaching from Syria, he called the Muslims to go out against them, and said, "This is the caravan of Quraysh, in which are their wealth, so go out to it, that perhaps Allah may grant it to you as spoils." So the people responded to the call. Some of them went forth lightly and some found it burdensome, because they had not thought that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ would encounter battle.

Abu Sufyan, when he drew near to the Hijaz, had already been on alert, gathering intelligence and asking everyone he met among the travelers, out of fear for the safety of the people, until he obtained news from some travelers that Muhammad had called his companions out against him and his caravan. He grew wary at that, and hired Damdam ibn 'Amr al-Ghifari, sending him to the people of Makkah, commanding him to go to Quraysh and call them out to defend their wealth, and to inform them that Muhammad had set out against it with his companions. So Damdam ibn 'Amr set out quickly for Makkah.

The Messenger of Allah ﷺ set out with his companions until he reached a valley called Dhafiran. He proceeded through it, and when he was partway through, he halted, and news reached him about Quraysh, that they were marching to protect their caravan. The Prophet ﷺ consulted the people and informed them about Quraysh. Abu Bakr, may Allah be pleased with him, stood and spoke well, then 'Umar, may Allah be pleased with him, stood and spoke well, then al-Miqdad ibn 'Amr stood and said: "O Messenger of Allah, proceed with what Allah has commanded you, for we are with you. By Allah, we will not say to you as the Children of Israel said to Musa: {So go, you and your Lord, and fight, indeed we are sitting here} [al-Ma'idah: 24], but rather: go, you and your Lord, and fight, for indeed we shall fight along with the two of you. By Him who sent you with the truth, if you were to march us to Bark al-Ghimad," meaning the city of Abyssinia, "we would fight alongside you against whoever stood in the way until you reached it." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said something good to him and prayed for him with good.

Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Advise me, O people," meaning by this the Ansar in particular, since they made up the majority of the people. This was because when they had given him their pledge at al-'Aqabah they had said, "O Messenger of Allah, we are free of any responsibility for you until you reach our land, but once you reach us, you are under our protection, and we will defend you as we defend our own sons and women." So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ feared that the Ansar might consider that they were only obligated to support him against an enemy that attacked him in Madinah itself, and that they were not obligated to march with him against an enemy outside their own land.

When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said that, Sa'd ibn Mu'adh said to him, "By Allah, it is as though you mean us, O Messenger of Allah?" He said, "Yes." Sa'd said, "We have believed in you, and we have accepted you as true, and we bear witness that what you have brought is the truth, and we have given you our pledges and our covenants upon that, to hear and to obey. So proceed, O Messenger of Allah, to what you intend. By Him who sent you with the truth, if you were to lead us out to this sea and plunge into it, we would plunge into it with you, and not a single man among us would hold back. We do not dislike the thought of meeting our enemy tomorrow with you. Indeed we are patient in war, truthful in encounter, and perhaps Allah will show you from us something that will bring joy to your eyes. So march with us, upon the blessing of Allah."

The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was pleased with Sa'd's words, and this encouraged him. Then he said, "March forth upon the blessing of Allah, and rejoice, for Allah has promised me one of the two parties. By Allah, it is as though I can now see the places where these people will fall."

Al-'Awfi narrated something similar to this from Ibn 'Abbas, and likewise al-Suddi, Qatadah, 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and more than one of the scholars of the earlier and later generations said the same. We have shortened their accounts, being content with the narration of Muhammad ibn Ishaq.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الطَّبَرِيُّ: اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي السَّبَبِ الْجَالِبِ لِهَذِهِ "الْكَافِ" فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ﴾ فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: شُبِّه بِهِ فِي الصَّلَاحِ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ، اتِّقَاؤُهُمْ رَبَّهُمْ، وَإِصْلَاحُهُمْ ذَاتَ بَيْنِهُمْ، وَطَاعَتُهُمُ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ.

ثُمَّ رَوَى عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ نَحْوَ هَذَا.

وَمَعْنَى هَذَا أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: كَمَا أَنَّكُمْ لَمَّا اخْتَلَفْتُمْ فِي الْمَغَانِمِ وَتَشَاحَحْتُمْ فِيهَا فَانْتَزَعَهَا اللَّهُ مِنْكُمْ، وَجَعَلَهَا إِلَى قَسْمِهِ وَقَسْمِ رَسُولِهِ ﷺ فَقَسَّمَهَا عَلَى الْعَدْلِ وَالتَّسْوِيَةِ، فَكَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْمَصْلَحَةَ التَّامَّةَ لَكُمْ، وَكَذَلِكَ لَمَّا كَرِهْتُمُ الْخُرُوجَ إِلَى الْأَعْدَاءِ مِنْ قتال ذات الشوكة -وهم النفير النَّفِيرُ الَّذِينَ خَرَجُوا لِنَصْرِ دِينِهِمْ، وَإِحْرَازِ عِيرِهِمْ -فَكَانَ عَاقِبَةُ، كَرَاهَتِكُمْ لِلْقِتَالِ -بِأَنْ قدَّره لَكُمْ، وجَمَع بِهِ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَ عَدُوِّكُمْ عَلَى غَيْرِ مِيعَادٍ -رَشَدَا وَهُدًى، وَنَصْرًا وَفَتْحًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْقِتَالُ وَهُوَ كُرْهٌ لَكُمْ وَعَسَى أَنْ تَكْرَهُوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ وَعَسَى أَنْ تُحِبُّوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ شَرٌّ لَكُمْ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٦]

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: مَعْنَى ذَلِكَ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ مِنْ بَيْتِكَ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ عَلَى كُرْهٍ مِنْ فَرِيقٍ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، كَذَلِكَ هُمْ كَارِهُونَ لِلْقِتَالِ، فَهُمْ يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِيهِ بَعْدَ مَا تَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ، ثُمَّ رَوَى نَحْوَهُ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ﴾ قَالَ: كَذَلِكَ يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِي خُرُوجِهِ إِلَى بَدْرٍ وَمُجَادَلَتِهِمْ إِيَّاهُ فَقَالَ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ مِنْ بَيْتِكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَإِنَّ فَرِيقًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لَكَارِهُونَ﴾ لِطَلَبِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ ﴿يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ بَعْدَمَا تَبَيَّنَ﴾

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْأَنْفَالِ مُجَادَلَةً، كَمَا جَادَلُوكَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ فَقَالُوا: أَخْرَجْتَنَا للعِير، وَلَمْ تُعْلِمْنَا قِتَالًا فَنَسْتَعِدُّ لَهُ.

قُلْتُ: رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِنَّمَا خَرَجَ مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ طَالِبًا لِعِيرِ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، الَّتِي بَلَغَهُ خَبَرُهَا أَنَّهَا صَادِرَةٌ مِنَ الشَّامِ، فِيهَا أَمْوَالٌ جَزِيلَةٌ لِقُرَيْشٍ فَاسْتَنْهَضَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْمُسْلِمِينَ مَنْ خَف مِنْهُمْ، فَخَرَجَ فِي ثَلَاثِمِائَةٍ وَبِضْعَةَ عَشَرَ رَجُلًا وَطَلَبَ نَحْوَ السَّاحِلِ مِنْ عَلَى طَرِيقِ بَدْرٍ، وَعَلِمَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ بِخُرُوجِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي طَلَبِهِ، فَبَعَثَ ضَمْضَم بْنَ عَمْرٍو نَذِيرًا إِلَى مَكَّةَ، فَنَهَضُوا فِي قَرِيبٍ مِنْ أَلْفِ مُقَنَّع، مَا بَيْنَ التِّسْعِمِائَةِ إِلَى الْأَلْفِ، وَتَيَامَنَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ بِالْعِيرِ إِلَى سَيْفِ الْبَحْرِ فَنَجَا، وَجَاءَ النَّفِيرُ فَوَرَدُوا مَاءَ بَدْرٍ، وَجَمَعَ اللَّهُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ وَالْكَافِرِينَ عَلَى غَيْرِ مِيعَادٍ، لِمَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مِنْ إعلاء كلمة المسلمين وَنَصْرِهِمْ عَلَى عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَالتَّفْرِقَةِ بَيْنَ الْحَقِّ وَالْبَاطِلِ، كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ.

وَالْغَرَضُ: أنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا بَلَغَهُ خُرُوجُ النَّفِيرِ، أَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ يَعدهُ إِحْدَى الطَّائِفَتَيْنِ: إِمَّا الْعِيرَ وَإِمَّا النَّفير، وَرَغِبَ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ إِلَى الْعِيرِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ كَسْبٌ بِلَا قِتَالٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَوَدُّونَ أَنَّ غَيْرَ ذَاتِ الشَّوْكَةِ تَكُونُ لَكُمْ وَيُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُحِقَّ الْحَقَّ بِكَلِمَاتِهِ وَيَقْطَعَ دَابِرَ الْكَافِرِينَ﴾

قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُويه فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا بَكْرُ بْنُ سَهْلٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ يُوسُفَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنْ أَسْلَمَ أَبِي عِمْرَانَ حَدَّثَهُ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا أَيُّوبَ الْأَنْصَارِيَّ يَقُولُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَنَحْنُ بِالْمَدِينَةِ: إِنِّي أُخْبِرْتُ عَنْ عِيرِ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ أَنَّهَا مُقْبِلَةٌ فَهَلْ لَكُمْ أَنْ نَخْرُجَ قَبْلَ هَذِهِ الْعِيرِ لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ يُغْنمناهَا؟ " فَقُلْنَا: نَعَمْ، فَخَرَجَ وَخَرَجْنَا، فَلَمَّا سِرْنا يَوْمًا أَوْ يَوْمَيْنِ قَالَ لَنَا: " مَا تَرَوْنَ فِي قِتَالِ الْقَوْمِ؛ فَإِنَّهُمْ قَدْ أُخْبِرُوا بِمَخْرَجِكُمْ؟ " فَقُلْنَا: لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا لَنَا طَاقَةٌ بِقِتَالِ الْعَدُوِّ، وَلَكِنَّا أَرَدْنَا الْعِيرَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: " مَا تَرَوْنَ فِي قِتَالِ الْقَوْمِ؟ " فَقُلْنَا مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ فَقَالَ الْمِقْدَادُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو: إذًا لَا نَقُولُ لَكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ كَمَا قَالَ قَوْمُ مُوسَى لِمُوسَى: ﴿فَاذْهَبْ أَنْتَ وَرَبُّكَ فَقَاتِلا إِنَّا هَاهُنَا قَاعِدُونَ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٢٤] قَالَ: فَتَمَنَّيْنَا -مَعْشَرَ الْأَنْصَارِ-أَنْ لَوْ قُلْنَا كَمَا قَالَ الْمِقْدَادُ أَحَبُّ إِلَيْنَا مِنْ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَنَا مَالٌ عَظِيمٌ، قَالَ: فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ ﷺ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ مِنْ بَيْتِكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَإِنَّ فَرِيقًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لَكَارِهُونَ﴾ وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ 

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ لَهِيعَةَ، بِنَحْوِهِ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَرْدُوَيْه أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَلْقَمة بْنِ وَقَّاصٍ اللَّيْثِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: خَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى بَدْرٍ، حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ بالرَّوْحاء، خَطَبَ النَّاسَ فَقَالَ: " كَيْفَ تَرَون؟ " فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، بَلَغَنَا أَنَّهُمْ بِمَكَانِ كَذَا وَكَذَا. قَالَ: ثُمَّ خَطَبَ النَّاسَ فَقَالَ: " كَيْفَ تَرَوْنَ؟ " فَقَالَ عُمَرُ مِثْلَ قَوْلِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ. ثُمَّ خَطَبَ النَّاسَ فَقَالَ: " كَيْفَ تَرَوْنَ؟ " فَقَالَ سَعْدُ بْنُ مُعَاذٍ: يا رسول الله إيانا تريد؟ فو الذي أَكْرَمَكَ [بِالْحَقِّ] وَأَنْزَلَ عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ، مَا سَلَكْتُهَا قَطُّ وَلَا لِي بِهَا عِلْمٌ، وَلَئِنْ سِرْتَ [بِنَا] حَتَّى تَأْتِيَ "بَرْك الْغِمَادِ" مِنْ ذِي يَمَنٍ لَنَسِيرَنَّ مَعَكَ، وَلَا نَكُونُ كَالَّذِينِ قَالُوا لِمُوسَى ﴿فَاذْهَبْ أَنْتَ وَرَبُّكَ فَقَاتِلا إِنَّا هَاهُنَا قَاعِدُونَ﴾ وَلَكِنْ اذهب أنت وربك فقاتلا إنا مَعَكُمَا مُتَّبِعُونَ، وَلَعَلَّكَ أَنْ تَكُونَ خَرَجْتَ لِأَمْرٍ، وَأَحْدَثَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْكَ غَيْرَهُ، فَانْظُرِ الَّذِي أَحْدَثَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْكَ، فَامْضِ لَهُ، فَصِلْ حِبَالَ مَنْ شِئْتَ، وَاقْطَعْ حِبَالَ مَنْ شِئْتَ، وَعَادِ مَنْ شِئْتَ، وَسَالِمْ مَنْ شِئْتَ، وَخُذْ مِنْ أَمْوَالِنَا مَا شِئْتَ، فَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ عَلَى قَوْلِ سَعْدٍ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ مِنْ بَيْتِكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَإِنَّ فَرِيقًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لَكَارِهُونَ﴾ الْآيَاتِ.

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَمَّا شَاوَرَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فِي لِقَاءِ الْعَدُوِّ، وَقَالَ له سعد بن عبادة ما قال وَذَلِكَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، أَمَرَ النَّاسَ فَعَبَّئُوا لِلْقِتَالِ، وَأَمَرَهُمْ بِالشَّوْكَةِ، فَكَرِهَ ذَلِكَ أَهْلُ الْإِيمَانِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿كَمَا أَخْرَجَكَ رَبُّكَ مِنْ بَيْتِكَ بِالْحَقِّ وَإِنَّ فَرِيقًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لَكَارِهُونَ يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ بَعْدَ مَا تَبَيَّنَ كَأَنَّمَا يُسَاقُونَ إِلَى الْمَوْتِ وَهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ: فِي الْقِتَالِ. وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: ﴿يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ [بَعْدَ مَا تَبَيَّنَ كَأَنَّمَا يُسَاقُونَ إِلَى الْمَوْتِ وَهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ] ﴾ أَيْ: كَرَاهِيَةً لِلِقَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَإِنْكَارًا لِمَسِيرِ قُرَيْشٍ حِينَ ذُكِرُوا لَهُمْ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: ﴿يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ بَعْدَمَا تَبَيَّنَ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ مَا تَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّكَ لَا تَفْعَلُ إِلَّا مَا أَمَرَكَ اللَّهُ بِهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: عَنَى بِذَلِكَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ.

حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْب قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ بَعْدَمَا تَبَيَّنَ كَأَنَّمَا يُسَاقُونَ إِلَى الْمَوْتِ وَهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ، جَادَلُوهُ فِي الْحَقِّ ﴿كَأَنَّمَا يُسَاقُونَ إِلَى الْمَوْتِ﴾ حِينَ يُدْعَوْنَ إِلَى الْإِسْلَامِ ﴿وَهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: وَلَيْسَ هَذَا مِنْ صِفَةِ الْآخَرِينَ، هَذِهِ صِفَةٌ مُبْتَدَأَةٌ لِأَهْلِ الْكُفْرِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَلَا مَعْنَى لِمَا قَالَهُ؛ لِأَنَّ الَّذِي قَبْلَ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يُجَادِلُونَكَ فِي الْحَقِّ﴾ خَبَرٌ عَنْ أَهْلِ الْإِيمَانِ، وَالَّذِي يَتْلُوهُ خَبَرٌ عَنْهُمْ، وَالصَّوَابُ قَوْلُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ أَنَّهُ خَبَرٌ عَنِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي نَصَرَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هُوَ الْحَقُّ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَدُلُّ عَلَيْهِ سِيَاقُ الْكَلَامِ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ..

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي بُكَيْرٍ وَعَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ سِمَال، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قِيلَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حِينَ فَرَغَ مِنْ بَدْرٍ: عَلَيْكَ بِالْعِيرِ لَيْسَ دُونَهَا شَيْءٌ فَنَادَاهُ الْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ -قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: وَهُوَ أَسِيرٌ فِي وِثَاقِهِ -ثُمَّ اتَّفَقَا: إِنَّهُ لَا يَصْلُحُ لَكَ، قَالَ: وَلِمَ؟ قَالَ: لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ إِنَّمَا وَعَدَكَ إِحْدَى الطَّائِفَتَيْنِ، وَقَدْ أَعْطَاكَ مَا وَعَدَكَ 

إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجْهُ 

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿وَتَوَدُّونَ أَنَّ غَيْرَ ذَاتِ الشَّوْكَةِ تَكُونُ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُحِبُّونَ أَنَّ الطَّائِفَةَ الَّتِي لَا حَدَّ لَهَا وَلَا مَنَعَةَ وَلَا قِتَالَ، تَكُونُ لَهُمْ وَهِيَ الْعِيرُ ﴿وَيُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُحِقَّ الْحَقَّ بِكَلِمَاتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَجْمَعَ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَ الطَّائِفَةِ الَّتِي لَهَا الشَّوْكَةُ وَالْقِتَالُ، ليُظَفِّرَكم بِهِمْ وَيُظْهِرَكُمْ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَيُظْهِرَ دِينَهُ، وَيَرْفَعَ كَلِمَةَ الْإِسْلَامِ، وَيَجْعَلَهُ غَالِبًا عَلَى الْأَدْيَانِ، وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِعَوَاقِبِ الْأُمُورِ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي دبركم بِحُسْنِ تَدْبِيرِهِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ الْعِبَادُ يُحِبُّونَ خِلَافَ ذَلِكَ فِيمَا يَظْهَرُ لَهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْقِتَالُ وَهُوَ كُرْهٌ لَكُمْ وَعَسَى أَنْ تَكْرَهُوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ وَعَسَى أَنْ تُحِبُّوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ شَرٌّ لَكُمْ [وَاللهُ يَعْلَمُ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ] [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٦] ﴾ 

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ الزُّهْرِيُّ، وَعَاصِمُ بْنُ عُمَرَ بْنِ قَتَادَةَ، وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، وَيَزِيدُ بْنُ رُومَانَ، عَنْ عُرْوَة بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ وَغَيْرِهِمْ مِنْ عُلَمَائِنَا، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ -كُلٌّ قَدْ حَدَّثَنِي بَعْضَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، فَاجْتَمَعَ حَدِيثُهُمْ فِيمَا سُقْتُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ بَدْرٍ -قَالُوا: لَمَّا سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِأَبِي سُفْيَانَ مُقْبِلًا مِنَ الشَّامِ نَدب الْمُسْلِمِينَ إِلَيْهِمْ، وَقَالَ: "هَذِهِ عيرُ قُرَيْشٍ فِيهَا أَمْوَالُهُمْ فَاخْرُجُوا إِلَيْهَا لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ أَنْ يُنْفلكُموها" فَانْتَدَبَ الناسُ، فَخَفَّ بَعْضُهُمْ وَثَقُلَ بَعْضُهُمْ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يَظُنُّوا أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَلْقَى حَرْبًا، وَكَانَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ قَدِ اسْتَنْفَرَ حِينَ دَنَا مِنَ الْحِجَازِ يَتَجَسَّسُ الْأَخْبَارَ، وَيَسْأَلُ مَنْ لَقِيَ مَنِ الرُّكْبَانِ، تَخَوُّفًا عَلَى أَمْرِ النَّاسِ، حَتَّى أَصَابَ خَبَرًا مِنْ بَعْضِ الرُّكْبَانِ: أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا قَدِ اسْتَنْفَرَ أَصْحَابَهُ لَكَ وَلِعِيرِكَ، فَحَذِرَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، فَاسْتَأْجَرَ ضَمْضَم بْنَ عَمْرٍو الْغِفَارِيَّ، فَبَعَثَهُ إِلَى أَهْلِ مَكَّةَ، وَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ قُرَيْشًا فَيَسْتَنْفِرَهُمْ إِلَى أَمْوَالِهِمْ، وَيُخْبِرَهُمْ أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا قَدْ عَرَضَ لَهَا فِي أَصْحَابِهِ، فَخَرَجَ ضَمْضَمُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو سَرِيعًا إِلَى مَكَّةَ، وَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي أَصْحَابِهِ حَتَّى بَلَغَ وَادِيًا يُقَالُ لَهُ "ذَفرَان"، فَخَرَجَ مِنْهُ حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ بِبَعْضِهِ نَزَلَ، وَأَتَاهُ الْخَبَرُ عَنْ قُريش بِمَسِيرِهِمْ لِيَمْنَعُوا عِيرَهُمْ فَاسْتَشَارَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ النَّاسَ، وَأَخْبَرَهُمْ عَنْ قُرَيْشٍ، فَقَامَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَقَالَ فَأَحْسَنَ، ثُمَّ قَامَ عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَقَالَ فَأَحْسَنَ، ثُمَّ قَامَ الْمِقْدَادُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، امْضِ لِمَا أَمَرَكَ اللَّهُ بِهِ، فَنَحْنُ مَعَكَ، وَاللَّهِ لَا نَقُولُ لَكَ كَمَا قَالَتْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ لِمُوسَى: ﴿فَاذْهَبْ أَنْتَ وَرَبُّكَ فَقَاتِلا إِنَّا هَاهُنَا قَاعِدُونَ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٢٤] وَلَكِنِ اذْهَبْ أَنْتَ وَرَبُّكَ فَقَاتِلَا إِنَّا مَعَكُمَا مُقَاتِلُونَ، فَوَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ، لَوْ سِرْتَ بِنَا إِلَى "بَرْك الغِماد" -يَعْنِي مَدِينَةَ الْحَبَشَةِ -لَجَالَدْنَا مَعَكَ مَنْ دُونِهِ حَتَّى تَبْلُغَهُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَيْرًا، وَدَعَا لَهُ بِخَيْرٍ، ثُمَّ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ:
