The second: Ibn Jarir also related, as did al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, with a sound chain of transmission, from Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab and al-Zuhri, that they both said: It was revealed regarding the throw of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ on the day of Uhud, when he struck Ubayy ibn Khalaf with the spear while he was in his armor, scratching him on his collarbone. He then kept falling from his horse repeatedly, until his death occurred [from it] some days later, during which he suffered a painful torment connected to the torment of the barzakh (intermediate realm), which in turn is connected to the torment of the Hereafter.

This report from these two imams is also extremely gharib (rare). Perhaps they meant that the verse includes him within its general scope, not that it was revealed specifically about him, as has already been mentioned. And Allah knows best.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: [chain] ... from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, regarding His words: {And that He might test the believers with a good test from Himself}, meaning: that He might make the believers aware of His favor upon them, in giving them victory over their enemy despite their enemy's great numbers and their own small numbers, so that they might recognize thereby His due right, and be grateful thereby for His favor.

Ibn Jarir explained it likewise. And in the hadith: "Every good test, He has tested us with."

His words: {Indeed, Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing}, meaning: Hearing of the supplication, Knowing of who deserves victory and dominance.

His words: {That is so, and Allah weakens the plot of the disbelievers}. This is another glad tiding along with the victory that occurred: that He, the Almighty, informed them that He weakens the plotting of the disbelievers in what is to come, belittling their affair, and that whatever they have will only lead to ruin and destruction. To Allah belongs all praise and grace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُبَيِّنُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ خَالِقُ أَفْعَالِ الْعِبَادِ، وَأَنَّهُ الْمَحْمُودُ عَلَى جَمِيعِ مَا صَدَرَ عَنْهُمْ مِنْ خَيْرٍ؛ لِأَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي وَفَّقَهُمْ لِذَلِكَ وَأَعَانَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَلَمْ تَقْتُلُوهُمْ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ قَتَلَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ بِحَوْلِكُمْ وَقُوَّتِكُمْ قَتَلْتُمْ أَعْدَاءَكُمْ مَعَ كَثْرَةِ عَدَدِهِمْ وَقِلَّةِ عَدَدِكُمْ، أَيْ: بَلْ هُوَ الَّذِي أَظْفَرَكُمْ [بِهِمْ وَنَصَرَكُمْ] عَلَيْهِمْ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ نَصَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ بِبَدْرٍ وَأَنْتُمْ أَذِلَّةٌ [فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ] ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٢٣] . وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَقَدْ نَصَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ فِي مَوَاطِنَ كَثِيرَةٍ وَيَوْمَ حُنَيْنٍ إِذْ أَعْجَبَتْكُمْ كَثْرَتُكُمْ فَلَمْ تُغْنِ عَنْكُمْ شَيْئًا وَضَاقَتْ عَلَيْكُمُ الأرْضُ بِمَا رَحُبَتْ ثُمَّ وَلَّيْتُمْ مُدْبِرِينَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٢٥] يَعْلِمُ -تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى-أَنَّ النَّصْرَ لَيْسَ عَنْ كَثْرَةِ الْعَدَدِ، وَلَا بِلِبْسِ اللَّأْمَةِ وَالْعَدَدِ، وَإِنَّمَا النَّصْرُ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿كَمْ مِنْ فِئَةٍ قَلِيلَةٍ غَلَبَتْ فِئَةً كَثِيرَةً بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ مَعَ الصَّابِرِينَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٤٩] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ أَيْضًا فِي شَأْنِ الْقَبْضَةِ مِنَ التُّرَابِ، الَّتِي حَصَبَ بِهَا وُجُوهَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، حِينَ خَرَجَ مِنَ الْعَرِيشِ بَعْدَ دُعَائِهِ وَتَضَرُّعِهِ وَاسْتِكَانَتِهِ، فَرَمَاهُمْ بِهَا وَقَالَ: " شَاهَتِ الْوُجُوهُ ". ثُمَّ أَمَرَ الصَّحَابَةَ أَنْ يَصْدُقُوا الْحَمْلَةَ إِثْرَهَا، فَفَعَلُوا، فَأَوْصَلَ اللَّهُ تِلْكَ الْحَصْبَاءَ إِلَى أَعْيُنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، فَلَمْ يَبْقَ أَحَدٌ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا نَالَهُ مِنْهَا مَا شَغَلَهُ عَنْ حَالِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ [تعالى] ﴿وَمَارَمَيْتَ إِذْ رَمَيْتَ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الَّذِي بَلَّغَ ذَلِكَ إِلَيْهِمْ، وَكَبَتَهُمْ بِهَا لَا أَنْتَ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: رَفَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَدَيْهِ -يَعْنِي يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ -فَقَالَ: " يَا رَبِّ إِنْ تُهْلِكْ هَذِهِ الْعِصَابَةَ، فَلَنْ تُعْبَدَ فِي الْأَرْضِ أَبَدًا". فَقَالَ لَهُ جِبْرِيلُ: "خُذْ قَبْضَةً مِنَ التُّرَابِ، فَارْمِ بِهَا فِي وُجُوهِهِمْ" فَأَخَذَ قَبْضَةً مِنَ التُّرَابِ، فَرَمَى بِهَا فِي وُجُوهِهِمْ، فَمَا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا أَصَابَ عَيْنَيْهِ وَمِنْخَرَيْهِ وَفَمَهُ تُرَابٌ مِنْ تِلْكَ الْقَبْضَةِ، فَوَلَّوْا مُدْبِرِينَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيّ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِعَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَوْمَ بدر: "أعطني حصبا من الأرض".

فَنَاوَلَهُ حَصَبًا عَلَيْهِ تُرَابٌ، فَرَمَى بِهِ فِي وُجُوهِ الْقَوْمِ، فَلَمْ يَبْقَ مُشْرِكٌ إِلَّا دَخَلَ فِي عَيْنَيْهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ التُّرَابِ شَيْءٌ، ثُمَّ رَدِفَهُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ يَقْتُلُونَهُمْ وَيَأْسِرُونَهُمْ، وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿فَلَمْ تَقْتُلُوهُمْ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ قَتَلَهُمْ وَمَا رَمَيْتَ إِذْ رَمَيْتَ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ رَمَى﴾

وَقَالَ أَبُو مَعْشَرٍ الْمَدَنِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ قَيْس وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ القُرَظِي قَالَا لَمَّا دَنَا الْقَوْمُ بَعْضُهُمْ مِنْ بَعْضٍ، أَخَذَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَبْضَةً مِنْ تُرَابٍ، فَرَمَى بِهَا فِي وُجُوهِ الْقَوْمِ، وَقَالَ: "شَاهَتِ الْوُجُوهُ". فَدَخَلَتْ فِي أَعْيُنِهِمْ كُلِّهِمْ، وَأَقْبَلَ أَصْحَابُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ [ﷺ] يَقْتُلُونَهُمْ وَيَأْسِرُونَهُمْ، وَكَانَتْ هَزِيمَتُهُمْ فِي رَمْية رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا رَمَيْتَ إِذْ رَمَيْتَ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ رَمَى﴾

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: فِي قَوْلِهِ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَمَا رَمَيْتَ إِذْ رَمَيْتَ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ رَمَى﴾ قَالَ: هَذَا يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ، أَخَذَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ ثَلَاثَ حَصَيَاتٍ فَرَمَى بِحَصَاةٍ [فِي] مَيْمَنَةِ الْقَوْمِ، وَحَصَاةٍ فِي مَيْسَرَةِ الْقَوْمِ، وَحَصَاةٍ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، وَقَالَ: "شَاهَتِ الْوُجُوهُ"، فَانْهَزَمُوا.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ فِي هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ عَنْ عُرْوَةَ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وقَتَادَةَ وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ: أَنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي رَمْيَةِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَإِنْ كَانَ قَدْ فَعَلَ ذَلِكَ يَوْمَ حُنَيْنٍ أَيْضًا.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ عِمْرَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ زَمْعَةَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي حَثْمَة، عَنْ حَكِيمِ بْنِ حِزَامٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ، سَمِعْنَا صَوْتًا وَقَعَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، كَأَنَّهُ صَوْتُ حَصَاةٍ وَقَعَتْ فِي طَسْتٍ، وَرَمَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ تِلْكَ الرَّمْيَةَ، فَانْهَزَمْنَا 

غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ. وَهَاهُنَا قَوْلَانِ آخَرَانِ غَرِيبَانِ جِدًّا.

أَحَدُهُمَا: قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَوْفٍ الطَّائِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْمُغِيرَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمَ ابْنِ أَبِي الْحَقِيقِ بِخَيْبَرَ، دَعَا بِقَوْسٍ، فَأَتَى بِقَوْسٍ طَوِيلَةٍ، وَقَالَ: "جيئوني غيرها". فجاؤوا بِقَوْسٍ كَبْدَاءَ، فَرَمَى النَّبِيُّ ﷺ الْحِصْنَ، فَأَقْبَلَ السَّهْمُ يَهْوِي حَتَّى قَتَلَ ابْنَ أَبِي الْحَقِيقِ، وَهُوَ فِي فِرَاشِهِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَمَا رَمَيْتَ إِذْ رَمَيْتَ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ رَمَى﴾ 

وَهَذَا غَرِيبٌ، وَإِسْنَادُهُ جَيِّدٌ إِلَى عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ جُبَيْرِ بْنِ نُفَيْرٍ، وَلَعَلَّهُ اشْتَبَهَ عَلَيْهِ، أَوْ أَنَّهُ أَرَادَ أَنَّ الْآيَةَ تَعُمُّ هَذَا كُلَّهُ، وَإِلَّا فَسِيَاقُ الْآيَةِ فِي سُورَةِ الْأَنْفَالِ فِي قِصَّةِ بَدْرٍ لَا مَحَالَةَ، وَهَذَا مِمَّا لَا يَخْفَى عَلَى أَئِمَّةِ العلم، والله أعلم.

وَالثَّانِي: رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، بِإِسْنَادٍ صَحِيحٍ إِلَى سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ والزُّهْرِيِّ أَنَّهُمَا قَالَا أُنْزِلَتْ فِي رَمْيَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمَ أُحُدٍ أُبَي بْنَ خَلَفٍ بِالْحَرْبَةِ وَهُوَ فِي لَأْمَتِهِ، فَخَدَشَهُ فِي تَرْقُوَتِهِ، فَجَعَلَ يَتَدَأْدَأُ عَنْ فَرَسِهِ مِرَارًا، حَتَّى كَانَتْ وَفَاتُهُ [بِهَا] بَعْدَ أَيَّامٍ، قَاسَى فِيهَا الْعَذَابَ الْأَلِيمَ، مَوْصُولًا بِعَذَابِ الْبَرْزَخِ، الْمُتَّصِلِ بِعَذَابِ الْآخِرَةِ 

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ عَنْ هَذَيْنَ الْإِمَامَيْنِ غَرِيبٌ أَيْضًا جِدًّا، وَلَعَلَّهُمَا أَرَادَا أَنَّ الْآيَةَ تَتَنَاوَلُهُ بِعُمُومِهَا، لَا أَنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِيهِ خَاصَّةً كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عُرْوَة بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلِيُبْلِيَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ مِنْهُ بَلاءً حَسَنًا﴾ أَيْ: ليُعَرّف الْمُؤْمِنِينَ مِنْ نِعْمَتِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، مِنْ إِظْهَارِهِمْ عَلَى عَدُوِّهِمْ مَعَ كَثْرَةِ عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَقِلَّةِ عَدَدِهِمْ، لِيَعْرِفُوا بِذَلِكَ حَقَّهُ، وَيَشْكُرُوا بِذَلِكَ نِعْمَتَهُ.

وَهَكَذَا فَسَّرَ ذَلِكَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا. وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "وَكُلُّ بَلَاءٍ حَسَنٌ أَبْلَانَا".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: سَمِيعُ الدُّعَاءِ، عَلِيمٌ بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ النَّصْرَ وَالْغَلَبَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿ذَلِكُمْ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ مُوهِنُ كَيْدِ الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ هَذِهِ بِشَارَةٌ أُخْرَى مَعَ مَا حَصَلَ مِنَ النَّصْرِ: أَنَّهُ أَعْلَمَهُمْ تَعَالَى بِأَنَّهُ مُضْعِفُ كَيْدِ الْكَافِرِينَ فِيمَا يَسْتَقْبِلُ، مُصَغِّرًا أَمْرَهُمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ كُلُّ مَا لَهُمْ فِي تَبَارٍ وَدَمَارٍ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

---

## 8:19 — verse 19

### Translation

The Almighty says to the disbelievers, {If you seek victory} meaning: you seek help and seek God's judgment and adjudication, that He decide between you and your enemies the believers, then indeed what you asked for has already come to you. As Muhammad ibn Ishaq and others said, on the authority of al-Zuhri, from Abdullah ibn Tha'laba ibn Sughayr, that Abu Jahl said on the Day of Badr: "O God, whichever of us is more severing of kinship ties and has brought us what we do not recognize, then destroy him this morning," and that was a seeking of victory (istiftah) on his part. So it was revealed: {If you seek victory, then victory has already come to you} to the end of the verse.

Imam Ahmad said: Yazid, that is Ibn Harun, related to us, Muhammad ibn Ishaq informed us, al-Zuhri related to me, from Abdullah ibn Tha'laba: that Abu Jahl said when the people met in battle: "O God, whichever of us is more severing of kinship ties and has brought us what we do not recognize, then destroy him this morning," and so he was the one who sought victory (al-mustaftih).

Al-Nasa'i related it in his Tafsir from the hadith of Salih ibn Kaysan, from al-Zuhri, with the same wording. Al-Hakim likewise related it in his Mustadrak by way of al-Zuhri, with the same wording, and said: "authentic according to the criterion of the two sheikhs (al-Bukhari and Muslim), though they did not include it." Something similar to this has been reported from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, al-Dahhak, Qatada, Yazid ibn Ruman, and others.

Al-Suddi said: When the polytheists set out from Mecca to Badr, they took hold of the coverings of the Ka'ba and sought God's help, saying: "O God, grant victory to the higher of the two armies, the more noble of the two groups, and the better of the two tribes." So God said: {If you seek victory, then victory has already come to you}, meaning: I have already granted victory to what you said, and that is Muhammad ﷺ.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: This is [parallel to] what the Almighty says, reporting about them: {And when they said: O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, [then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment]} [al-Anfal: 32].

As for His saying, {And if you cease} meaning: from what you are engaged in of disbelief in God and denial of His Messenger, {then it is better for you} meaning: in this world and the next. [And His saying] {And if you return, We will return} is like His saying {And if you return, We will return} [al-Isra: 8], meaning: and if you return to what you were in of disbelief and misguidance, We will return upon you with the like of this event.

Al-Suddi said: {And if you return} meaning: to seeking victory, {We will return} to granting victory to Muhammad ﷺ, and to helping him, and to giving him triumph over his enemies. But the first interpretation is stronger.

{And your company will not avail you at all, though it be numerous} meaning: even if you gathered as many hosts as you could possibly gather, for whoever has God with him has no one who can overcome him. And God is with the believers, and they are the party of the Prophet, and the noble company of the Chosen One ﷺ.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِلْكُفَّارِ ﴿إِنْ تَسْتَفْتِحُوا﴾ أَيْ: تَسْتَنْصِرُوا وَتَسْتَقْضُوا اللَّهَ وَتَسْتَحْكِمُوهُ أَنْ يَفْصِلَ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَ أَعْدَائِكُمُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ مَا سَأَلْتُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ وَغَيْرُهُ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عبد الله بن ثعلبة بن صُغَيْر؛ أَنَّ أَبَا جَهْلٍ قَالَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ: اللَّهُمَّ أَقْطَعُنَا لِلرَّحِمِ وَآتَانَا بِمَا لَا نَعْرِفُ فَأَحْنِهِ الْغَدَاةَ -وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ اسْتِفْتَاحًا مِنْهُ -فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنْ تَسْتَفْتِحُوا فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمُ الْفَتْحُ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ الْآيَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ هَارُونَ -أَخْبَرَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنِي الزُّهْرِيُّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ ثَعْلَبَةَ: أَنَّ أَبَا جَهْلٍ قَالَ حِينَ الْتَقَى الْقَوْمُ: اللَّهُمَّ، أَقْطَعُنَا لِلرَّحِمِ، وَآتَانَا بِمَا لَا نَعْرِفُ، فَأَحْنِهِ الْغَدَاةَ، فَكَانَ الْمُسْتَفْتِحَ.

وَأَخْرَجَهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ، صَالِحِ بْنِ كَيْسَانَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ وكذا رواه الحاكم فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ مِنْ طَرِيقِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ وَقَالَ: صَحِيحٌ عَلَى شَرْطِ الشَّيْخَيْنِ، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجَاهُ. وَرُوِيَ [نَحْوُ] هَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وقَتَادَةَ، وَيَزِيدَ بْنِ رُومَان، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: كَانَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ حِينَ خَرَجُوا مِنْ مَكَّةَ إِلَى بَدْر، أَخَذُوا بِأَسْتَارِ الْكَعْبَةِ فَاسْتَنْصَرُوا اللَّهَ وَقَالُوا: اللَّهُمَّ انْصُرْ أَعْلَى الْجُنْدَيْنِ، وَأَكْرَمَ الْفِئَتَيْنِ، وَخَيْرَ الْقَبِيلَتَيْنِ. فَقَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿إِنْ تَسْتَفْتِحُوا فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمُ الْفَتْحُ﴾ يَقُولُ: قَدْ نَصَرْتُ مَا قُلْتُمْ، وَهُوَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: هُوَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْهُمْ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ [فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ] ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٢] . 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ تَنْتَهُوا﴾ أَيْ: عَمَّا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ بِاللَّهِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ لِرَسُولِهِ، ﴿فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ. [وَقَوْلُهُ] ﴿وَإِنْ تَعُودُوا نَعُدْ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿وَإِنْ عُدْتُمْ عُدْنَا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٨] مَعْنَاهُ: وَإِنْ عُدْتُمْ إِلَى مَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالضَّلَالَةِ، نَعُدْ لَكُمْ بِمِثْلِ هَذِهِ الْوَاقِعَةِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿وَإِنْ تَعُودُوا﴾ أَيْ: إِلَى الِاسْتِفْتَاحِ ﴿نَعُدْ﴾ إِلَى الْفَتْحِ لِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ، وَالنَّصْرِ لَهُ، وَتَظْفِيرِهِ عَلَى أَعْدَائِهِ، وَالْأَوَّلُ أَقْوَى.

﴿وَلَنْ تُغْنِيَ عَنْكُمْ فِئَتُكُمْ شَيْئًا وَلَوْ كَثُرَتْ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَوْ جَمَعْتُمْ مِنَ الْجُمُوعِ مَا عَسَى أَنْ تَجْمَعُوا، فَإِنَّ مَنْ كَانَ اللَّهُ مَعَهُ فَلَا غَالِبَ لَهُ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَهُمُ الْحِزْبُ النَّبَوِيُّ، وَالْجَنَابُ الْمُصْطَفَوِيُّ.

---

## 8:20-23 — verses 20-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, commands His believing servants to obey Him and obey His Messenger, and He forbids them from opposing him and resembling those who disbelieve in him and are obstinate against him. It is for this reason that He said: {And do not turn away from him}, meaning: do not abandon obedience to him and compliance with his commands, and do not abandon what he forbids, {while you are hearing}, meaning: after you have come to know what he has called you to.

{And do not be like those who said, "We have heard," while they do not hear}: it is said that those meant are the polytheists, and this is the view Ibn Jarir chose.

Ibn Ishaq said: they are the hypocrites, for they display that they have heard and responded, while they are not so in reality.

Then Allah, exalted is He, informs that this class among the sons of Adam is the worst of creation and of created beings, saying: {Indeed, the worst of creatures in the sight of Allah are the deaf}

meaning: deaf to hearing the truth, {the dumb}, meaning: dumb to understanding it. It is for this that He said: {those who do not use reason}. These are the worst of created beings, because every creature besides them is obedient to Allah [mighty and majestic is He] in that for which He created it, while these were created for worship yet disbelieved. It is for this reason that He likened them to cattle in His saying: {And the example of those who disbelieve is like the example of one who calls out to that which hears nothing but a shout and a cry. [Deaf, dumb, and blind, so they do not use reason]} [al-Baqarah: 171]. And He said in another verse: {Those are like cattle, rather they are more astray. Those, they are the heedless} [al-A'raf: 179].

And it is said that those referred to here are a group from Banu 'Abd al-Dar of the Quraysh. This is reported from Ibn 'Abbas and Mujahid, and Ibn Jarir chose this view. Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: they are the hypocrites.

I say: there is no contradiction between the polytheists and the hypocrites being meant here, because each of them has been stripped of sound understanding and of true intent toward righteous action.

Then Allah, exalted is He, informs that they have no sound understanding and no sound intent, even were it supposed that they had some understanding. He said: {And if Allah had known any good in them, He would have made them hear}, meaning: He would have made them understand. The intended sense of the statement is: but there is no good in them, so He did not grant them understanding, because He knows that {even if He had made them hear}, meaning: made them understand, {they would have turned away} from that deliberately and out of obstinacy after having understood it, {while they are averse} to it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَأْمُرُ تَعَالَى عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِطَاعَتِهِ وَطَاعَةِ رَسُولِهِ، وَيَزْجُرُهُمْ عَنْ مُخَالَفَتِهِ وَالتَّشَبُّهِ بِالْكَافِرِينَ بِهِ الْمُعَانِدِينَ لَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلا تَوَلَّوْا عَنْهُ﴾ أَيْ: تَتْرُكُوا طَاعَتَهُ وَامْتِثَالَ أَوَامِرِهِ وَتَرْكَ زَوَاجِرِهِ، ﴿وَأَنْتُمْ تَسْمَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ مَا عَلِمْتُمْ مَا دَعَاكُمْ إِلَيْهِ.

﴿وَلا تَكُونُوا كَالَّذِينَ قَالُوا سَمِعْنَا وَهُمْ لَا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ الْمُشْرِكُونَ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُمُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ؛ فَإِنَّهُمْ يُظْهِرُونَ أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ سَمِعُوا وَاسْتَجَابُوا، وَلَيْسُوا كَذَلِكَ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ هَذَا الضَّرْبَ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ شَرُّ الْخَلْقِ وَالْخَلِيقَةِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ شَرَّ الدَّوَابِّ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ الصُّمُّ﴾

أَيْ: عَنْ سَمَاعِ الْحَقِّ ﴿الْبُكْمُ﴾ عَنْ فَهْمِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ﴾ فَهَؤُلَاءِ شَرُّ الْبَرِيَّةِ؛ لِأَنَّ كُلَّ دَابَّةٍ مِمَّا سِوَاهُمْ مُطِيعَةٌ لِلَّهِ [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] فِيمَا خَلَقَهَا لَهُ، وَهَؤُلَاءِ خُلِقُوا لِلْعِبَادَةِ فَكَفَرُوا؛ وَلِهَذَا شَبَّهَهُمْ بِالْأَنْعَامِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَثَلُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي يَنْعِقُ بِمَا لَا يَسْمَعُ إِلا دُعَاءً وَنِدَاءً [صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ] ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٧١] . وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿أُولَئِكَ كَالأنْعَامِ بَلْ هُمْ أَضَلُّ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْغَافِلُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٧٩] .

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمَذْكُورِينَ نَفَرٌ مِنْ بَنِي عَبْدِ الدَّارِ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ. رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُمُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ.

قُلْتُ: وَلَا مُنَافَاةَ بَيْنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ فِي هَذَا؛ لِأَنَّ كُلًّا مِنْهُمْ مَسْلُوبُ الْفَهْمِ الصَّحِيحِ، وَالْقَصْدِ إِلَى الْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى بِأَنَّهُمْ لَا فَهْمَ لَهُمْ صَحِيحٌ، وَلَا قَصْدَ لَهُمْ صَحِيحٌ، لَوْ فُرِضَ أَنَّ لَهُمْ فَهْمًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا لأسْمَعَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَأَفْهَمَهُمْ، وَتَقْدِيرُ الْكَلَامِ: وَلَكِنْ لَا خَيْرَ فِيهِمْ فَلَمْ يُفْهِمْهُمْ؛ لِأَنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ ﴿وَلَوْ أَسْمَعَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَفْهَمَهُمْ ﴿لَتَوَلَّوْا﴾ عَنْ ذَلِكَ قَصْدًا وَعِنَادًا بَعْدَ فَهْمِهِمْ ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَهُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ عَنْهُ.

---

## 8:24 — verse 24

### Translation

Al-Bukhari said: {astajibu} means "respond," {lima yuhyikum} means "to what will set you right."

He said: Ishaq related to us, Rawh related to us, Shu'bah related to us, from Khubayb ibn Abd al-Rahman, who said: I heard Hafs ibn Asim relating from Abu Sa'id ibn al-Mu'alla, who said: I was praying, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by me and called me, but I did not come to him until I had finished my prayer. Then I came to him, and he said: "What kept you from coming to me?" Did Allah not say: {O you who believe, respond to Allah and to the Messenger when he calls you to what will give you life}? Then he said: "I shall certainly teach you the greatest surah in the Qur'an before I leave." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ then went to leave, and I reminded him of it. Mu'adh said: Shu'bah related to us, from Khubayb ibn Abd al-Rahman, who heard Hafs ibn Asim, who heard Abu Sa'id, a man among the Companions of the Prophet ﷺ, relating this same account, and he said: "It is {al-Hamdu lillahi Rabbi'l-'Alamin}, the seven oft-repeated verses."

This is his wording exactly, and the discussion of this hadith, with mention of its various chains, has already been given at the beginning of the commentary on al-Fatiha.

Mujahid said regarding His statement {lima yuhyikum}: "the truth."

Qatadah said regarding {lima yuhyikum}: "It is this Qur'an, in which is deliverance, safeguarding, and life."

Al-Suddi said regarding {lima yuhyikum}: "In Islam is their revival after their death caused by disbelief."

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Muhammad ibn Ja'far ibn al-Zubayr, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, regarding {O you who believe, respond to Allah and to the Messenger when he calls you to what will give you life}: that is, "to the battle by which Allah, may He be exalted, honored you after humiliation, strengthened you after weakness, and protected you from your enemy after they had overpowered you."

And His statement, may He be exalted: {and know that Allah comes between a man and his heart}. Ibn Abbas said: "He comes between the believer and disbelief, and between the disbeliever and belief."

Al-Hakim related this in his Mustadrak as a mawquf (halted report), and said: "Sound, though the two [Bukhari and Muslim] did not include it." Ibn Marduyah related it by another route as marfu' (elevated to the Prophet ﷺ), but it is not sound due to the weakness of its chain, and the mawquf version is more authentic. Mujahid, Sa'id, Ikrimah, al-Dahhak, Abu Salih, Atiyyah, Muqatil ibn Hayyan, and al-Suddi said likewise.

In one report from Mujahid regarding His statement {He comes between a man and his heart}: "until He leaves him unable to reason."

Al-Suddi said: "He comes between a person and his heart, so that he cannot believe nor disbelieve except by His permission."

Qatadah said this is like His statement: {and We are nearer to him than his jugular vein} [Qaf: 16].

Hadiths have come down from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that correspond to the meaning of this verse.

Imam Ahmad said: Abu Mu'awiyah related to us, from al-A'mash, from Abu Sufyan, from Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Prophet ﷺ used to say frequently: "O Turner of hearts, make my heart firm upon Your religion." He said: We said, O Messenger of Allah, we have believed in you and in what you brought, so do you fear for us? He said: "Yes, for hearts are between two of the fingers of Allah, may He be exalted, and He turns them as He wills."

This is how al-Tirmidhi related it in the "Book of Predestination" of his Jami', from Hannad ibn al-Sari, from Abu Mu'awiyah Muhammad ibn Hazim al-Darir, from al-A'mash (whose name is Sulayman ibn Mihran), from Abu Sufyan (whose name is Talhah ibn Nafi'), from Anas. He then said: "Hasan (good)." It has likewise been related by more than one narrator from al-A'mash; some of them relate it from him, from Abu Sufyan, from Jabir, from the Prophet ﷺ, but the hadith of Abu Sufyan from Anas is more authentic.

Another hadith: Abd ibn Humayd said in his Musnad: Abd al-Malik ibn Amr related to us, Shu'bah related to us, from al-Hakam, from Ibn Abi Layla, from Bilal, may Allah be pleased with him, that the Prophet ﷺ used to pray: "O Turner of hearts, make my heart firm upon Your religion."

This is a hadith with a good chain, though it contains a break in transmission; nevertheless, it meets the standard of the compilers of the Sunan works, though they did not include it.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: al-Walid ibn Muslim related to us, saying: I heard Ibn Jabir say: Busr ibn Abdullah al-Hadrami related to me, that he heard Abu Idris al-Khawlani say: I heard al-Nawwas ibn Sam'an al-Kilabi, may Allah be pleased with him, say: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "There is no heart except that it is between two of the fingers of the Most Merciful, Lord of the Worlds. If He wishes to keep it upright, He keeps it upright, and if He wishes to make it deviate, He makes it deviate." And he used to say: "O Turner of hearts, make our hearts firm upon Your religion." He said: "And the scale is in the hand of the Most Merciful, He lowers it and raises it."

This is how al-Nasa'i and Ibn Majah related it, from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid ibn Jabir, mentioning the same account.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Yunus related to us, Hammad ibn Zayd related to us, from al-Mu'alla ibn Ziyad, from al-Hasan, that A'ishah said: Among the supplications the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to make was: "O Turner of hearts, make my heart firm upon Your religion." She said: So I said, O Messenger of Allah, you make this supplication frequently. He said: "The heart of the human being is between two of the fingers of Allah; if He wishes He makes it deviate, and if He wishes He keeps it upright."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Hashim related to us, Abd al-Hamid related to us, Shahr related to me, saying: I heard Umm Salamah relate that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to say frequently in his supplication: "O Allah, O Turner of hearts, make my heart firm upon Your religion." She said: So I said, O Messenger of Allah, are hearts truly turned about? He said: "Yes, Allah, mighty and exalted, has not created any human being among the children of Adam except that his heart is between two of the fingers of Allah, mighty and exalted; if He wills, He keeps it upright, and if He wills, He makes it deviate. So we ask Allah our Lord not to let our hearts deviate after He has guided us, and we ask Him to grant us mercy from Himself, for He is the Bestower." She said: I said, O Messenger of Allah, will you not teach me a supplication I may make for myself? He said: "Certainly, say: O Allah, Lord of the Prophet Muhammad, forgive me my sin, remove the rage of my heart, and protect me from the misleading trials for as long as You give me life."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Abu Abd al-Rahman related to us, Hayweh related to us, Abu Hani' informed me, that he heard Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Hubuli, who heard Abdullah ibn Amr, who heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "The hearts of the children of Adam are between two of the fingers of the Most Merciful, like a single heart, which He directs as He wills." Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "O Allah, Director of hearts, direct our hearts toward obedience to You."

Muslim alone related this, apart from al-Bukhari, and al-Nasa'i related it along with him, from the hadith of Hayweh ibn Shurayh al-Misri, by the same chain.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: ﴿اسْتَجِيبُوا﴾ أَجِيبُوا، ﴿لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ لِمَا يُصْلِحُكُمْ. حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ، حَدَّثَنَا رَوْحٌ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ خُبَيْبِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ حَفْصَ بْنَ عَاصِمٍ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُعَلَّى قَالَ: كُنْتُ أُصَلِّي، فَمَرَّ بِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَدَعَانِي فَلَمْ آتِهِ حَتَّى صَلَّيْتُ، ثُمَّ أَتَيْتُهُ فَقَالَ: "مَا مَنَعَكَ أَنْ تَأْتِيَنِي؟ " أَلَمْ يَقُلِ اللَّهُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اسْتَجِيبُوا لِلَّهِ وَلِلرَّسُولِ إِذَا دَعَاكُمْ لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ: "لَأُعَلِّمَنَّكَ أَعْظَمَ سُورَةٍ فِي الْقُرْآنِ قَبْلَ أَنْ أَخْرُجَ"، فَذَهَبَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِيَخْرُجَ، فَذَكَرْتُ لَهُ -وَقَالَ مُعَاذٌ: حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ خُبَيْب بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، سَمِعَ حَفْصَ بْنَ عَاصِمٍ، سَمِعَ أَبَا سَعِيدٍ رَجُلًا مِنْ أَصْحَابِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بِهَذَا -وَقَالَ: " هِيَ ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ السَّبْعُ الْمَثَانِي" 

هَذَا لَفْظُهُ بِحُرُوفِهِ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ بِذِكْرِ طُرُقِهِ فِي أَوَّلِ تَفْسِيرِ الْفَاتِحَةِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قوله: ﴿لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ قال: الحق.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ ﴿لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ، فِيهِ النَّجَاةُ وَالتُّقَاةُ وَالْحَيَاةُ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيّ: ﴿لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ فَفِي الْإِسْلَامِ إِحْيَاؤُهُمْ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهِمْ بِالْكُفْرِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اسْتَجِيبُوا لِلَّهِ وَلِلرَّسُولِ إِذَا دَعَاكُمْ لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لِلْحَرْبِ الَّتِي أَعَزَّكُمُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِهَا بَعْدَ الذُّلِّ، وَقَوَّاكُمْ بِهَا بَعْدَ الضَّعْفِ، وَمَنَعَكُمْ مِنْ عَدُوِّكُمْ بَعْدَ الْقَهْرِ مِنْهُمْ لَكُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَحُولُ بَيْنَ الْمَرْءِ وَقَلْبِهِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَحُولُ بَيْنَ الْمُؤْمِنِ وَبَيْنَ الْكُفْرِ، وَبَيْنَ الْكَافِرِ وَبَيْنَ الْإِيمَانِ.

رَوَاهُ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ مَوْقُوفًا، وَقَالَ: صَحِيحٌ وَلَمْ يُخْرِجَاهُ وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَرْدُوَيه مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ مَرْفُوعًا وَلَا يَصِحُّ لِضَعْفِ إِسْنَادِهِ، وَالْمَوْقُوفُ أَصَحُّ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَعَطِيَّةُ، ومُقَاتِل بْنُ حيَّان، والسُّدِّيّ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَحُولُ بَيْنَ الْمَرْءِ وَقَلْبِهِ﴾ حَتَّى تَرَكَهُ لَا يَعْقِلُ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: يَحُولُ بَيْنَ الْإِنْسَانِ وَقَلْبِهِ، فَلَا يَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ يُؤْمِنَ وَلَا يَكْفُرَ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ هُوَ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَنَحْنُ أَقْرَبُ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ حَبْلِ الْوَرِيدِ﴾ [ق: ١٦] .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَتِ الْأَحَادِيثُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِمَا يُنَاسِبُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: كَانَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ يُكْثِرُ أَنْ يَقُولُ: " يَا مُقَلِّب الْقُلُوبِ، ثَبِّتْ قَلْبِي عَلَى دِينِكَ". قَالَ: فَقُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، آمَنَّا بِكَ وَبِمَا جِئْتَ بِهِ، فَهَلْ تَخَافُ عَلَيْنَا؟ قَالَ نَعَمْ، إِنَّ الْقُلُوبَ بَيْنَ إِصْبَعَيْنِ مِنْ أَصَابِعِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى يُقَلِّبُهَا".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي "كِتَابِ الْقَدَرِ" مِنْ جَامِعِهِ، عَنْ هَنَّادِ بْنِ السَّرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حَازِمٍ الضَّرِيرِ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ -وَاسْمُهُ سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ مِهْرَانَ -عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ -وَاسْمُهُ طَلْحَةُ بْنُ نَافِعٍ -عَنْ أَنَسٍ ثُمَّ قَالَ: حَسَنٌ. وَهَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ غَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، رَوَاهُ بَعْضُهُمْ عَنْهُ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، وَحَدِيثُ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ عَنْ أَنَسٍ أَصَحُّ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ عَبْدُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ الْحَكَمِ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، عَنْ بِلَالٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ كَانَ يَدْعُو: "يَا مُقَلِّب الْقُلُوبِ ثَبِّت قَلْبِي عَلَى دينك".

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ جَيِّدُ الْإِسْنَادِ إِلَّا أَنَّ فِيهِ انْقِطَاعًا وَهُوَ -مَعَ ذَلِكَ -عَلَى شَرْطِ أَهْلِ السُّنَنِ وَلَمْ يُخْرِجُوهُ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ ابْنَ جَابِرٍ يَقُولُ: حَدَّثَنِي بُسْرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْحَضْرَمِيُّ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا إِدْرِيسَ الْخَوْلَانِيَّ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ النَّوَّاسَ بْنَ سَمْعَان الْكِلَابِيَّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: " مَا مِنْ قَلْبٍ إِلَّا وَهُوَ بَيْنُ أُصْبُعَيْنِ مِنْ أَصَابِعِ الرَّحْمَنِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ، إِذَا شَاءَ أَنْ يُقِيمَهُ أَقَامَهُ، وَإِذَا شَاءَ أَنْ يُزِيغَهُ أَزَاغَهُ". وَكَانَ يَقُولُ: "يَا مُقَلِّبَ الْقُلُوبِ، ثَبِّتْ قُلُوبَنَا عَلَى دِينِكَ". قَالَ: "وَالْمِيزَانُ بِيَدِ الرَّحْمَنِ يَخْفِضُهُ وَيَرْفَعُهُ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ جَابِرٍ فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْمُعَلَّى بْنِ زِيَادٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ؛ أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: دَعَوَاتٌ كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَدْعُو بِهَا: "يَا مُقَلِّبَ الْقُلُوبِ، ثَبِّتْ قَلْبِي عَلَى دِينِكَ". قَالَتْ: فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّكَ تُكْثِرُ تَدْعُو بِهَذَا الدُّعَاءِ. فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ قَلْبَ الْآدَمِيِّ بَيْنَ إِصْبَعَيْنِ مِنْ أَصَابِعِ اللَّهِ، فَإِذَا شَاءَ أَزَاغَهُ وَإِذَا شَاءَ أَقَامَهُ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْحَمِيدِ، حَدَّثَنِي شَهْرٌ، سَمِعْتُ أُمَّ سَلَمَةَ تُحَدِّثُ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يُكْثِرُ فِي دُعَائِهِ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ يَا مُقَلِّبَ الْقُلُوبِ، ثَبِّتْ قَلْبِي عَلَى دِينِكَ". قالت: فقلت يا رسول الله، أو إن الْقُلُوبَ لَتُقَلَّبُ ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، مَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَشَرٍ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ إِلَّا أَنَّ قَلْبَهُ بَيْنَ أُصْبُعَيْنِ مِنْ أَصَابِعِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَإِنْ شَاءَ أَقَامَهُ، وَإِنْ شَاءَ أَزَاغَهُ. فَنَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ رَبَّنَا أَنْ لَا يُزِيغَ قُلُوبَنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَانَا، وَنَسْأَلُهُ أَنْ يَهَبَ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْهُ رَحْمَةً إِنَّهُ هُوَ الْوَهَّابُ". قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَلَا تُعَلِّمُنِي دَعْوَةً أَدْعُو بِهَا لِنَفْسِي؟ قَالَ: " بَلَى، قُولِي: اللَّهُمَّ رَبَّ النَّبِيِّ مُحَمَّدٍ، اغْفِرْ لِي ذَنْبِي، وَأَذْهِبْ غَيْظَ قَلْبِي، وَأَجِرْنِي مِنْ مُضِلَّاتِ الْفِتَنِ مَا أَحْيَيْتَنِي" 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَيْوَةُ، أَخْبَرَنِي أَبُو هَانِئٍ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الحُبَلي أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يَقُولُ: " إِنَّ قُلُوبَ بَنِي آدَمَ بَيْنَ إِصْبَعَيْنِ مِنْ أَصَابِعِ الرَّحْمَنِ، كَقَلْبٍ وَاحِدٍ يُصَرِّف كَيْفَ شَاءَ . ثُمَّ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اللَّهُمَّ مُصَرِّف الْقُلُوبِ، صَرِّف قُلُوبَنَا إلى طاعتك".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ عَنِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، فَرَوَاهُ مَعَ النَّسَائِيِّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَيْوَة بْنِ شُرَيْح الْمِصْرِيِّ، بِهِ.

---

## 8:25 — verse 25

### Translation

The Exalted warns His believing servants of {a trial (fitnah)}, meaning a testing and an ordeal, that will encompass both the wrongdoer and others, not being confined to the people of sin or to those who directly commit the offense, but rather encompassing both of them, since it is not repelled and lifted away. As Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Abu Sa'id, freedman of Banu Hashim... from Mutarrif, who said: We said to al-Zubayr: O Abu Abdullah, what brought you here? You neglected the caliph who was killed, then you came seeking his blood? Al-Zubayr, may Allah be pleased with him, said: We used to recite, in the time of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and of Abu Bakr, Umar, and Uthman, may Allah be pleased with them: {And beware of a trial that will not afflict only those among you who have done wrong}, and we never supposed that we were its people, until it befell us where it befell us.

Al-Bazzar related it from the hadith of Mutarrif from al-Zubayr and said: We do not know of Mutarrif relating from al-Zubayr anything other than this hadith.

Al-Nasa'i related from the hadith of Jarir ibn Hazim, from al-Hasan, from al-Zubayr, something similar to this.

Ibn Jarir related: [chain] al-Harith... from al-Hasan, who said: al-Zubayr said: We were indeed warned by it, meaning the saying [of the Exalted] {And beware of a trial that will not afflict only those among you who have done wrong}, while we were with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and we never thought that we in particular were singled out by it.

Likewise Humayd related it from al-Hasan from al-Zubayr, may Allah be pleased with him.

Dawud ibn Abi Hind said, from al-Hasan, regarding this verse: it was revealed concerning Ali, Uthman, Talha, and al-Zubayr, may Allah be pleased with them.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from al-Salt ibn Dinar, from Uqbah ibn Suhban: I heard al-Zubayr say: I recited this verse for a long time and did not consider us to be among its people, but it turns out we are indeed the ones meant by it: {And beware of a trial that will not afflict only those among you who have done wrong, and know that Allah is severe in punishment}.

It has been related through more than one route from al-Zubayr ibn al-Awwam.

Al-Suddi said: it was revealed concerning the people of Badr specifically, and it befell them on the Day of the Camel, when they fought each other.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding the saying of the Exalted {And beware of a trial that will not afflict only those among you who have done wrong}: meaning the Companions of the Prophet ﷺ specifically.

He said, in another report from Ibn Abbas, in explaining this verse: Allah commanded the believers not to let wrongdoing remain established in their midst without opposing it, lest Allah encompass them all with punishment.

This is a very fine explanation. That is why Mujahid said, regarding the saying of the Exalted {And beware of a trial that will not afflict only those among you who have done wrong}: it applies to you as well. Al-Dahhak, Yazid ibn Abi Habib, and others said the same.

Ibn Mas'ud said: There is not one among you but he carries within himself some trial. Allah the Exalted says: {Your wealth and your children are but a trial} [al-Taghabun: 15]. So whichever of you wishes to seek refuge, let him seek refuge with Allah from the misguiding trials. Related by Ibn Jarir.

The view that this warning encompasses the Companions and others as well, even though the address was directed to them, is the correct one. This is indicated by the hadiths that have come down warning against trials, and there is an independent book, God willing, that clarifies this, just as the scholars have done, devoting separate compilations to it. Among the most relevant things to mention here is what Imam Ahmad related, saying:

[chain] Ahmad ibn al-Hajjaj... Abdullah, meaning Ibn al-Mubarak... Sayf ibn Abi Sulayman, who said: I heard Adi ibn Adi al-Kindi say: A freedman of ours told me that he heard my grandfather, meaning Adi ibn Amirah, say: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Indeed Allah, Mighty and Majestic, does not punish the general mass for the deed of a particular group until they see wrongdoing being committed openly in their midst, while being capable of opposing it, and yet they do not oppose it. When they do that, Allah punishes both the particular group and the general mass."

In it there is an unnamed man, and it was not included by any of the Six Books. Allah knows best.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Sulayman al-Hashimi... Isma'il, meaning Ibn Ja'far... Amr ibn Abi Amr, from Abdullah ibn Abd al-Rahman al-Ashhali, from Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you will surely command good and forbid evil, or Allah will swiftly send upon you a punishment from Himself, then you will call upon Him and He will not answer you."

He also related it from Abu Sa'id, from Isma'il ibn Ja'far, and said: "or Allah will surely send against you a people, then you will call upon Him and He will not answer you."

Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah ibn Numayr... Razin ibn Habib al-Juhani... Abu al-Ruqad, who said: I went out with my master, and I was brought before Hudhayfah while he was saying: A man used to speak a single word in the time of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and become a hypocrite because of it, yet I hear the same from one of you in a single sitting four times over. You will surely command good, and forbid evil, and urge one another to good, or Allah will sweep you all away with a punishment, or He will place your worst over you as rulers, after which your best will call upon Him and not be answered.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Yahya ibn Sa'id, from Zakariyya... Amir, who said: I heard al-Nu'man ibn Bashir, may Allah be pleased with him, delivering a sermon, saying, while gesturing with his two fingers toward his ears: The likeness of one who upholds the limits set by Allah, and one who transgresses them, or who compromises regarding them, is like a people who boarded a ship. Some of them were placed in its lower part, its roughest and worst section, while others were placed in its upper part. Whenever those in the lower part wanted water, they would pass by those above them and cause them harm. So they said: What if we made a hole in our own section, so that we might draw water from it, and not harm those above us? If the others leave them to do as they wish, they will all perish together, but if they seize their hands and stop them, they will all be saved together.

Al-Bukhari alone related it, without Muslim, in the Book of Partnership and the Book of Testimonies, and al-Tirmidhi related it in the Book of Trials through more than one route, from Sulayman ibn Mihran al-A'mash, from Amir ibn Sharahil al-Sha'bi, with this wording.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Husayn... Khalaf ibn Khalifah, from Layth, from Alqamah ibn Marthad, from al-Ma'rur ibn Suwayd, from Umm Salamah, wife of the Prophet ﷺ, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "When sins become manifest among my nation, Allah will encompass them with a punishment from Himself." I said: O Messenger of Allah, are there not among them righteous people? He said: "Yes." She said: What then will happen to them? He said: "What befalls the people will befall them too, but then they will end up receiving forgiveness and good pleasure from Allah."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Hajjaj ibn Muhammad... Sharik, from Abu Ishaq, from al-Mundhir ibn Jarir, from his father, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no people who commit sins, among whom there is a man mightier and more capable than they of stopping them, who fail to change it, but Allah will encompass them all with punishment, or the punishment will befall them."

Abu Dawud related it from Musaddad, from Abu al-Ahwas, from Abu Ishaq, with this wording.

Ahmad also said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Ja'far... Shu'bah, who said: I heard Abu Ishaq relate, from Ubaydullah ibn Jarir, from his father, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no people among whom sins are committed, while they are mightier and more numerous than those who commit them, and yet they fail to change it, but Allah will encompass them all with punishment."

He also related it from Waki', from Isra'il, and from Abd al-Razzaq, from Ma'mar, and from Aswad, from Sharik and Yunus, all of them from Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i, with this wording.

Ibn Majah brought it out from Ali ibn Muhammad, from Waki', with this wording.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Sufyan... Jami' ibn Abi Rashid, from Mundhir, from al-Hasan ibn Muhammad, from his wife, from Aishah, who traced it to the Prophet ﷺ: "When evil becomes manifest on the earth, Allah sends down His might upon the people of the earth." She said: Even though among them are people obedient to Allah? He said: "Yes, but then they will end up receiving the mercy of Allah."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُحَذِّرُ تَعَالَى عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ﴿فِتْنَةً﴾ أَيِ: اخْتِبَارًا وَمِحْنَةً، يَعُمُّ بِهَا الْمُسِيءَ وَغَيْرَهُ، لَا يَخُصُّ بِهَا أَهْلَ الْمَعَاصِي وَلَا مَنْ بَاشَرَ الذَّنْبَ، بَلْ يَعُمُّهُمَا، حَيْثُ لَمْ تُدْفَعُ وَتُرْفَعُ. كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَدَّاد بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا غَيْلان بْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ مُطَرِّف قَالَ: قُلْنَا لِلزُّبَيْرِ: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، مَا جَاءَ بِكُمْ؟ ضَيَّعْتُمُ الْخَلِيفَةَ الَّذِي قُتِلَ، ثُمَّ جِئْتُمْ تَطْلُبُونَ بِدَمِهِ؟ فَقَالَ الزُّبَيْرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: إِنَّا قَرَأْنَا عَلَى عَهْدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَأَبِي بَكْرٍ وَعُمَرَ وَعُثْمَانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ: ﴿وَاتَّقُوا فِتْنَةً لَا تُصِيبَنَّ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْكُمْ خَاصَّةً﴾ لَمْ نَكُنْ نَحْسَبُ أَنَّا أَهْلُهَا حَتَّى وَقَعَتْ مِنَّا حَيْثُ وَقَعَتْ 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُطَرِّفٍ، عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، وَقَالَ: لَا نَعْرِفُ مُطَرِّفًا رَوَى عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ غَيْرَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ 

وَقَدْ رَوَى النَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ جَرِيرِ بْنِ حَازِمٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ نَحْوَ هَذَا 

وَرَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُبَارَكُ بْنُ فَضَالة، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: قَالَ الزُّبَيْرُ: لَقَدْ خُوِّفْنَا بِهَا، يَعْنِي قَوْلَهُ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَاتَّقُوا فِتْنَةً لَا تُصِيبَنَّ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْكُمْ خَاصَّةً﴾ وَنَحْنُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَمَا ظَنَنَّا أَنَّا خُصِصْنَا بِهَا خَاصَّةً.

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ حُمَيْدٌ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ 

وَقَالَ دَاوُدُ بْنُ أَبِي هِنْد، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي عَلِيٍّ، وَعُثْمَانَ وَطَلْحَةَ وَالزُّبَيْرِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ عَنِ الصَّلت بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ بْنِ صُهْبان، سَمِعْتُ الزُّبَيْرَ يَقُولُ: لَقَدْ قَرَأْتُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ زَمَانًا وَمَا أَرَانَا مِنْ أَهْلِهَا فَإِنْ نَحْنُ الْمَعْنِيُّونَ بِهَا: ﴿وَاتَّقُوا فِتْنَةً لَا تُصِيبَنَّ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْكُمْ خَاصَّةً وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ بْنِ الْعَوَّامِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيّ: نَزَلَتْ فِي أَهْلِ بدر خاصة، فأصابتهم يوم الجمل، فاقتتلوا.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاتَّقُوا فِتْنَةً لَا تُصِيبَنَّ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْكُمْ خَاصَّةً﴾ يَعْنِي: أَصْحَابَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ خَاصَّةً

وَقَالَ فِي رِوَايَةٍ لَهُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: أَمَرَ اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَلَّا يُقِرُّوا الْمُنْكَرَ بَيْنَ ظَهْرَانِيهِمْ إِلَيْهِمْ فَيَعُمَّهُمُ اللَّهُ بِالْعَذَابِ.

وَهَذَا تَفْسِيرٌ حَسَنٌ جِدًّا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاتَّقُوا فِتْنَةً لَا تُصِيبَنَّ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْكُمْ خَاصَّةً﴾ هِيَ أَيْضًا لَكُمْ، وَكَذَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَيَزِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: مَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ إِلَّا وَهُوَ مُشْتَمِلٌ عَلَى فِتْنَةٍ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَأَوْلادُكُمْ فِتْنَةٌ﴾ [التَّغَابُنِ: ١٥] فَأَيُّكُمُ اسْتَعَاذَ فَلْيَسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ مُضِلَّاتِ الْفِتَنِ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَالْقَوْلُ بِأَنَّ هَذَا التَّحْذِيرَ يَعُمُّ الصَّحَابَةَ وَغَيْرَهُمْ -وَإِنْ كَانَ الْخِطَابُ مَعَهُمْ -هُوَ الصَّحِيحُ، وَيَدُلُّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ الْأَحَادِيثُ الْوَارِدَةُ فِي التَّحْذِيرِ مِنَ الْفِتَنِ، وَلِذَلِكَ كِتَابٌ مُسْتَقِلٌّ يُوَضَّحُ فِيهِ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، كَمَا فَعَلَهُ الْأَئِمَّةُ وَأَفْرَدُوهُ بِالتَّصْنِيفِ وَمِنْ أَخَصِّ مَا يُذْكَرُ هَاهُنَا مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ حَيْثُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ الْمُبَارَكِ-أَنْبَأَنَا سَيْفُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ، سَمِعْتُ عَدِيّ بْنَ عَدِيّ الْكِنْدِيَّ يَقُولُ: حَدَّثَنِي مَوْلًى لَنَا أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ جَدِّي -يَعْنِي عَدِيّ بْنَ عَمِيرَةَ -يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لَا يُعَذِّبُ الْعَامَّةَ بِعَمَلِ الْخَاصَّةِ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْمُنْكَرَ بَيْنَ ظَهْرَانَيْهم، وَهُمْ قَادِرُونَ عَلَى أَنْ يُنْكِرُوهُ فَلَا يُنْكِرُوهُ، فَإِذَا فَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ عَذَّب اللَّهُ الْخَاصَّةَ وَالْعَامَّةَ" 

فِيهِ رَجُلٌ مُبْهَمٌ، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجُوهُ فِي الْكُتُبِ السِّتَّةِ، وَلَا وَاحِدَ مِنْهُمْ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ الْهَاشِمِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ جَعْفَرٍ -أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ أَبِي عَمْرٍو، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْأَشْهَلِ، عَنْ حُذَيفة بْنِ الْيَمَانِ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: " وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَتَأْمُرُنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَلَتَنْهَوُنَّ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، أَوْ لَيُوشِكَنَّ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَبْعَثَ عَلَيْكُمْ عِقابا مِنْ عِنْدِهِ، ثُمَّ لتَدعُنّه فَلَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَكُمْ" 

وَرَوَاهُ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، وَقَالَ: "أَوْ لَيَبْعَثَنَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمْ قَوْمًا ثُمَّ تَدْعُونَهُ فَلَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَكُمْ " 

وَقَالَ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ نُمَيْرٍ، قَالَ حَدَّثَنَا رَزِين بْنُ حَبِيبٍ الجُهَني، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو الرُّقاد قَالَ: خَرَجْتُ مَعَ مَوْلَايَ، فَدُفِعْتُ إِلَى حُذَيْفَةَ وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: إِنْ كَانَ الرَّجُلُ لَيَتَكَلَّمُ بِالْكَلِمَةِ عَلَى عَهْدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَيَصِيرُ مُنَافِقًا، وَإِنِّي لَأَسْمَعُهَا مِنْ أَحَدِكُمْ فِي الْمَقْعَدِ الْوَاحِدِ أَرْبَعَ مَرَّاتٍ؛ لَتَأْمُرُنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَلَتَنْهَوُنَّ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، ولَتَحَاضُّن عَلَى الْخَيْرِ، أَوْ لَيَسْحَتَنَّكم اللَّهُ جَمِيعًا بعذاب، أو ليؤمرَنّ عليكم شِرَارَكُمْ، ثُمَّ يَدْعُو خِيَارُكُمْ فَلَا يُسْتَجَابُ لَهُمْ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ زَكَرِيَّا، حَدَّثَنَا عَامِرٌ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ النُّعْمَانَ بْنَ بَشِيرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَخْطُبُ يَقُولُ -وَأَوْمَأَ بِإِصْبَعَيْهِ إِلَى أُذُنَيْهِ -يَقُولُ: مَثَلُ الْقَائِمِ عَلَى حُدُودِ اللَّهِ وَالْوَاقِعِ فيها -أو المُداهن فِيهَا -كَمَثَلِ قَوْمٍ رَكِبُوا سَفِينَةً، فَأَصَابَ بَعْضُهُمْ أَسْفَلَهَا وَأَوْعَرَهَا وَشَرَّهَا، وَأَصَابَ بَعْضُهُمْ أَعْلَاهَا، فَكَانَ الَّذِينَ فِي أَسْفَلِهَا إِذَا اسْتَقَوُا الْمَاءَ مَرُّوا عَلَى مَنْ فَوْقَهُمْ فَآذُوهُمْ، فَقَالُوا: لَوْ خَرَقْنا فِي نَصِيبِنَا خَرْقا، فَاسْتَقَيْنَا مِنْهُ، وَلَمْ نُؤْذِ مَنْ فَوْقَنَا، فَإِنْ تَرَكُوهُمْ وَأَمْرَهُمْ هَلَكوا جَمِيعًا، وَإِنْ أَخَذُوا عَلَى أَيْدِيهِمْ نَجَوْا جَمِيعًا.

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ دُونَ مُسْلِمٍ، فَرَوَاهُ فِي "الشَّرِكَةِ" و "الشَّهَادَاتِ"، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي الْفِتَنِ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مِهْرَانَ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ عَامِرِ بْنِ شَرَاحيل الشَّعْبِيِّ، بِهِ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حُسَيْنٌ، حَدَّثَنَا خَلَف بْنُ خَلِيفَةَ، عَنْ لَيْث، عَنْ عَلْقَمَة بْنِ مَرْثد، عَنِ الْمَعْرُورِ بْنِ سُوَيْد، عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ زَوْجَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَتْ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِذَا ظَهَرَتِ الْمَعَاصِي فِي أُمَّتِي، عَمَّهم اللَّهُ بِعَذَابٍ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ". فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَمَا فِيهِمْ أُنَاسٌ صَالِحُونَ؟ قَالَ: "بَلَى"، قَالَتْ: فَكَيْفَ يَصْنَعُ أُولَئِكَ؟ قَالَ: "يُصِيبُهُمْ مَا أَصَابَ النَّاسُ، ثُمَّ يَصِيرُونَ إِلَى مَغْفِرَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرِضْوَانٍ" 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاج بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا شَرِيكٌ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الْمُنْذِرِ بْنِ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ قَوْمٍ يَعْمَلُونَ بِالْمَعَاصِي، وَفِيهِمْ رَجُلٌ أَعَزُّ مِنْهُمْ وَأَمْنَعُ لَا يُغَيِّرُونَ، إِلَّا عَمَّهُمُ اللَّهُ بِعِقَابٍ -أَوْ: أَصَابَهُمُ الْعِقَابُ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ مُسَدَّد، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ سَمِعْتُ أَبَا إِسْحَاقَ يُحَدِّثُ، عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ قَوْمٍ يُعْمَل فِيهِمْ بِالْمَعَاصِي، هُمْ أعَزّ وَأَكْثَرُ مِمَّنْ يَعْمَلُهُ، لَمْ يُغَيِّرُوهُ، إِلَّا عَمَّهُمُ اللَّهُ بِعِقَابٍ" 

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ أَيْضًا عَنْ وَكِيع، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ -وَعَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر -وَعَنْ أَسْوَدَ، عَنْ شَرِيكٍ وَيُونُسَ -كُلُّهُمْ عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ السَّبِيعي، بِهِ.

وَأَخْرَجَهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ وَكِيعٍ، بِهِ [حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ] وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، حَدَّثَنَا جَامِعُ بْنُ أَبِي رَاشِدٍ، عَنْ مُنْذِر، عَنْ حَسَنِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنِ امْرَأَتِهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ تَبْلُغُ بِهِ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ: "إِذَا ظَهَرَ السُّوءُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ بِأَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ بَأْسَهُ". قَالَتْ: وَفِيهِمْ أَهْلُ طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، ثُمَّ يَصِيرُونَ إِلَى رحمة الله"

---

## 8:26 — verse 26

### Translation

God most high alerts His believing servants to His favors upon them and His kindness toward them, in that they were few and He made them many, they were weak and fearful and He strengthened them and gave them victory, they were poor and destitute and He provided for them from the good and wholesome things, and He sought their gratitude, so they obeyed Him and complied with everything He commanded them.

This was the state of the believers during their stay in Mecca: few in number, hiding, under duress, fearing that people from every land of God would snatch them away, whether polytheist, Magian, or Byzantine, all of whom were enemies to them because of their small number and their lack of strength. This remained their condition continually until God permitted them to migrate to Medina. He gave them shelter there and prepared for them its people, who sheltered them and gave them victory on the day of Badr and on other occasions, who shared with them their wealth, and who gave freely of their very lives in obedience to God and obedience to His Messenger.

Qatadah ibn Di'amah al-Sadusi, may God have mercy on him, said regarding the words of God most high, {And remember when you were few, deemed weak in the land}: This tribe among the Arabs was the most abased of people in humiliation, the most wretched in livelihood, the hungriest in stomachs, the most exposed of skin, the clearest in error, muzzled atop a rock between the two lions, Persia and Byzantium. No, by God, there was nothing in their lands in those days that anyone would envy them for. Whoever among them lived, lived in wretchedness, and whoever among them died was cast down into the Fire. They were the ones eaten, not the ones who ate. By God, we do not know of any settled tribe among the people of the earth in those days who were in a worse condition than they were, until God brought Islam, and through it established them firmly in the land, and through it widened their provision, and through it made them kings over the necks of other people. It was through Islam that God gave what you have seen. So give thanks to God for His favors, for your Lord is a Bestower of favor who loves gratitude, and the people of gratitude are ever increasing from God [most high].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُنَبِّهُ تَعَالَى عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى نِعَمِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَإِحْسَانِهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، حَيْثُ كَانُوا قَلِيلِينَ فكثَّرهم، وَمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ خَائِفِينَ فقوَّاهم وَنَصَرَهُمْ، وَفُقَرَاءَ عَالَةً فَرَزَقَهُمْ مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ، وَاسْتَشْكَرَهُمْ فَأَطَاعُوهُ، وَامْتَثَلُوا جَمِيعَ مَا أَمَرَهُمْ. وَهَذَا كَانَ حَالَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ حَالَ مُقَامِهِمْ بِمَكَّةَ قَلِيلِينَ مُسْتَخْفِينَ مُضْطَرِّينَ يَخَافُونَ أَنْ يَتَخَطَّفَهُمُ النَّاسُ مِنْ سَائِرِ بِلَادِ اللَّهِ، مِنْ مُشْرِكٍ وَمَجُوسِيٍّ وَرُومِيٍّ، كُلُّهُمْ أَعْدَاءٌ لَهُمْ لِقِلَّتِهِمْ وَعَدَمِ قُوَّتِهِمْ، فَلَمْ يَزَلْ ذَلِكَ دَأْبُهُمْ حَتَّى أَذِنَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ فِي الْهِجْرَةِ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، فَآوَاهُمْ إِلَيْهَا، وقَيَّض لَهُمْ أَهْلَهَا، آوَوْا وَنَصَرُوا يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ وَغَيْرَهُ وآسَوا بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ، وَبَذَلُوا مُهَجهم فِي طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ وَطَاعَةِ رَسُولِهِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ بْنُ دِعَامة السَّدوسي، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاذْكُرُوا إِذْ أَنْتُمْ قَلِيلٌ مُسْتَضْعَفُونَ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ هَذَا الْحَيُّ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ أَذَلَّ النَّاسِ ذُلا وَأَشْقَاهُ عَيْشًا، وَأَجْوَعَهُ بُطُونًا، وَأَعْرَاهُ جُلُودًا، وَأَبْيَنَهُ ضَلَالًا مَكْعُومِينَ عَلَى رَأْسِ حَجَرٍ، بَيْنَ الْأَسَدَيْنِ فَارِسَ وَالرُّومِ، وَلَا وَاللَّهِ مَا فِي بِلَادِهِمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ مِنْ شَيْءٍ يُحْسَدُونَ عَلَيْهِ، مَنْ عَاشَ مِنْهُمْ عَاشَ شَقِيًّا، وَمَنْ مَاتَ مِنْهُمْ رُدِّيَ فِي النَّارِ، يُؤْكَلُونَ وَلَا يَأْكُلُونَ، وَاللَّهِ مَا نَعْلَمُ قَبِيلا مِنْ حَاضِرِ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ يَوْمَئِذٍ كَانُوا أَشَرَّ مَنْزِلًا مِنْهُمْ، حَتَّى جَاءَ اللَّهُ بِالْإِسْلَامِ فَمَكَّنَ بِهِ فِي الْبِلَادِ، وَوَسَّعَ بِهِ فِي الرِّزْقِ، وَجَعَلَهُمْ بِهِ مُلُوكًا عَلَى رِقَابِ النَّاسِ. وَبِالْإِسْلَامِ أَعْطَى اللَّهُ مَا رَأَيْتُمْ، فَاشْكُرُوا لِلَّهِ نِعَمَهُ، فَإِنَّ رَبَّكُمْ مُنْعِم يُحِبُّ الشُّكْرَ، وَأَهْلُ الشُّكْرِ فِي مَزِيدٍ مِنَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى]

---

## 8:27-28 — verses 27-28 (shared commentary)

### Translation

'Abdullah ibn Abi Qatadah and al-Zuhri said: it was revealed concerning Abu Lubabah ibn al-Mundhir, when the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sent him to Banu Qurayzah so that they would submit to the judgment of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. They sought his counsel about that, and he gestured to them indicating that, pointing his hand to his throat, meaning: it is slaughter. Then Abu Lubabah became aware, and saw that he had betrayed Allah and His Messenger, so he swore not to taste any food until he died or until Allah accepted his repentance. He went to the mosque of Medina and bound himself to one of its pillars, and remained thus for nine days, until he would collapse unconscious from the strain, until Allah revealed his repentance to His Messenger. The people came to give him the good news of Allah's acceptance of his repentance, and wanted to release him from the pillar, but he swore that none would release him from it except the Messenger of Allah, may Allah's peace and blessings be upon him, with his own hand. So he released him, and Abu Lubabah said: "O Messenger of Allah, I had vowed to give up my wealth entirely as charity." He said, "A third of it suffices you to give as charity."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Harith told me, Abd al-Aziz told us, Yunus ibn al-Harith al-Ta'ifi told us, Muhammad ibn Ubaydullah Abu Awn al-Thaqafi told us, from al-Mughirah ibn Shu'bah, who said: this verse was revealed concerning the killing of Uthman, may Allah be pleased with him: {O you who believe, do not betray Allah and the Messenger} the verse.

Ibn Jarir also said: [chain] al-Qasim ibn Bishr ibn Ma'ruf told us, Shababah ibn Sawwar told us, Muhammad ibn al-Muharrim told us, who said: I met Ata ibn Abi Rabah and he related to me, saying: Jabir ibn Abdullah related to me that Abu Sufyan left Mecca, and Jibril (peace be upon him) came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said: Abu Sufyan is in such and such a place. The Prophet ﷺ said to his companions: "Abu Sufyan is in such and such a place, so go out to him and keep this secret." A man among the hypocrites then wrote to them: "Muhammad intends to move against you, so take your precaution." So Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed {Do not betray Allah and the Messenger, nor betray your trusts} the verse.

This is a very gharib (singular) report, and there is doubt regarding its chain and its wording.

In the two Sahihs is the account of Hatib ibn Abi Balta'ah, who wrote to the Quraysh informing them of the Messenger of Allah's ﷺ intent to move against them in the year of the Conquest. Allah made His Messenger aware of this, so he sent someone after the letter and retrieved it, and summoned Hatib, who admitted to what he had done. Umar ibn al-Khattab stood and said: "O Messenger of Allah, shall I not strike off his neck? He has betrayed Allah, His Messenger, and the believers." The Prophet ﷺ said: "Leave him, for he was present at Badr. What do you know? Perhaps Allah looked upon the people of Badr and said: 'Do what you wish, for I have forgiven you.'"

I say: the correct view is that the verse is general in application, and even if it is authentic that it came down regarding a specific occasion, the position of the majority of scholars is to take the general wording rather than restrict it to the specific occasion. Betrayal encompasses sins both small and great, whether they concern one's own person or extend to others.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: {nor betray your trusts}, the trust refers to the deeds which Allah entrusted to His servants, meaning the obligatory duties. He is saying: do not betray them, meaning do not break them.

He said in another report: {Do not betray Allah and the Messenger} means: by abandoning his sunnah and committing disobedience to him.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Ja'far ibn al-Zubayr told me, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, regarding this verse: meaning, do not outwardly show to Allah the truth that pleases Him from you, then secretly act contrary to it toward something else, for that is destruction of your trusts and betrayal of yourselves.

Al-Suddi said: when they betray Allah and the Messenger, they have indeed betrayed their trusts.

He also said: they used to hear a matter from the Prophet ﷺ and then spread it until it reached the polytheists. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: He has forbidden you to betray Allah and the Messenger, as the hypocrites did.

Concerning the statement of the Exalted, {And know that your wealth and your children are but a trial}, meaning: a test and an examination from Him for you, since He gave them to you in order to know whether you would be grateful to Him for them and obey Him regarding them, or whether you would become preoccupied with them away from Him, and take them as a substitute for Him. As the Exalted said: {Your wealth and your children are but a trial, and with Allah is a great reward} [al-Taghabun: 15], and He said: {And We test you with evil and with good as a trial} [al-Anbiya: 35], and the Exalted said: {O you who believe, let not your wealth and your children divert you from the remembrance of Allah, and whoever does that, then those are the losers} [al-Munafiqun: 9], and the Exalted said: {O you who believe, indeed among your spouses and your children are enemies for you, so beware of them} the verse [al-Taghabun: 14].

Concerning His statement, {and that with Allah is a great reward}, meaning: His reward, His giving, and His gardens are better for you than wealth and children. For indeed an enemy may be found among them, and most of them will not avail you anything, and Allah, glory be to Him, is the One who disposes and possesses this world and the next, and with Him is abundant reward on the Day of Resurrection.

In the athar (report), Allah the Exalted says: "O son of Adam, seek Me and you will find Me. If you find Me, you find everything, and if you miss Me, you miss everything, and I am more beloved to you than everything."

In the authentic hadith, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he said: "Three things, whoever has them will find in them the sweetness of faith: whoever has Allah and His Messenger more beloved to him than anything else; whoever loves a person and loves him only for the sake of Allah; and whoever finds being thrown into the fire more preferable to him than returning to disbelief after Allah has saved him from it."

Rather, love for His Messenger takes precedence over children, wealth, and one's own self, as is established in the authentic hadith that he, peace be upon him, said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, none of you truly believes until I am more beloved to him than his own self, his family, his wealth, and all people."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ والزُّهْرِيُّ: أُنْزِلَتْ فِي أَبِي لُبابة بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُنْذِرِ، حِينَ بَعَثَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى بَنِي قُرَيْظة لِيَنْزِلُوا عَلَى حُكْمِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَاسْتَشَارُوهُ فِي ذَلِكَ، فَأَشَارَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِذَلِكَ -وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى حَلْقِهِ -أَيْ: إِنَّهُ الذَّبْحُ، ثُمَّ فَطِنَ أَبُو لُبَابَةَ، وَرَأَى أَنَّهُ قَدْ خَانَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ، فَحَلَفَ لَا يَذُوقُ ذَوَاقًا حَتَّى يَمُوتَ أَوْ يَتُوبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَانْطَلَقَ إِلَى مَسْجِدِ الْمَدِينَةِ، فَرَبَطَ نَفْسَهُ فِي سَارِيَةٍ مِنْهُ، فَمَكَثَ كَذَلِكَ تِسْعَةَ أَيَّامٍ، حَتَّى كَانَ يَخِرُّ مَغْشِيًّا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْجَهْدِ، حَتَّى أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَوْبَتَهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ. فَجَاءَ النَّاسُ يُبَشِّرُونَهُ بِتَوْبَةِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ، وَأَرَادُوا أَنْ يَحُلُّوهُ مِنَ السَّارِيَةِ، فَحَلَفَ لَا يَحُلُّهُ مِنْهَا إِلَّا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ [وَسَلَّمَ] بِيَدِهِ، فَحَلَّهُ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي كُنْتُ نَذَرْتُ أَنْ أَنْخَلِعَ مِنْ مَالِي صَدَقَةً، فَقَالَ يَجْزِيكَ الثُّلُثُ أَنْ تَصدَّقَ بِهِ" 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ الطَّائِفِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ أَبُو عَوْنٍ الثَّقَفِيُّ، عَنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ بْنِ شُعْبَةَ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي قَتْلِ عُثْمَانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَخُونُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ بِشْر بْنِ مَعْرُوفٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَبَابة بْنُ سَوَّار، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْمُحْرِمِ قَالَ: لَقِيتُ عَطَاءَ بْنَ أَبِي رَبَاحٍ فَحَدَّثَنِي قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي جَابِرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ؛ أَنَّ أَبَا سُفْيَانَ خَرَجَ مِنْ مَكَّةَ، فَأَتَى جِبْرِيلُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ أَبَا سُفْيَانَ فِي كَذَا وَكَذَا. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ لِأَصْحَابِهِ: "إِنَّ أَبَا سُفْيَانَ فِي مَوْضِعِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَاخْرُجُوا إِلَيْهِ وَاكْتُمُوا" فَكَتَبَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ إِلَيْهِ: إِنَّ مُحَمَّدًا يُرِيدُكُمْ، فَخُذُوا حِذْرَكُمْ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] ﴿لَا تَخُونُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ وَتَخُونُوا أَمَانَاتِكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ 

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، وَفِي سَنَدِهِ وَسِيَاقِهِ نَظَرٌ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ قِصَّةُ "حَاطِبِ بْنِ أَبِي بَلْتَعَة" أَنَّهُ كَتَبَ إِلَى قُرَيْشٍ يُعْلِمُهُمْ بِقَصْدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِيَّاهُمْ عَامَ الْفَتْحِ، فَأَطْلَعَ اللَّهُ رَسُولَهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، فَبَعَثَ فِي إِثْرِ الْكِتَابِ فَاسْتَرْجَعَهُ، وَاسْتَحْضَرَ حَاطِبًا فَأَقَرَّ بِمَا صَنَعَ، فَقَامَ عمر بن الخطاب فقال: يا رسول الله، أَلَا أَضْرِبُ عُنُقَهُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ خَانَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَالْمُؤْمِنِينَ؟ فَقَالَ: " دَعْهُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ شَهِدَ بَدْرًا، مَا يُدْرِيكَ لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ اطَّلَعَ عَلَى أَهْلِ بَدْرٍ فَقَالَ: "اعْمَلُوا مَا شِئْتُمْ فَقَدْ غَفَرْتُ لَكُمْ" 

قُلْتُ: وَالصَّحِيحُ أَنَّ الْآيَةَ عَامَّةٌ، وَإِنْ صَحَّ أَنَّهَا وَرَدَتْ عَلَى سَبَبٍ خَاصٍّ، فَالْأَخْذُ بِعُمُومِ اللَّفْظِ لَا بِخُصُوصِ السَّبَبِ عِنْدَ الْجَمَاهِيرِ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ. وَالْخِيَانَةُ تَعُمُّ الذُّنُوبَ الصِّغَارَ وَالْكِبَارَ اللَّازِمَةَ وَالْمُتَعَدِّيَةَ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَتَخُونُوا أَمَانَاتِكُمْ﴾ الْأَمَانَةُ الْأَعْمَالُ الَّتِي ائْتَمَنَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا الْعِبَادَ -يَعْنِي الْفَرِيضَةَ يَقُولُ: لَا تَخُونُوا: لَا تَنْقُضُوهَا.

وَقَالَ فِي رِوَايَةٍ: ﴿لَا تَخُونُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ﴾ يَقُولُ: بِتَرْكِ سُنَّتِهِ وَارْتِكَابِ مَعْصِيَتِهِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، أَيْ: لَا تُظْهِرُوا لِلَّهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ مَا يَرْضَى بِهِ مِنْكُمْ، ثُمَّ تُخَالِفُوهُ فِي السِّرِّ إِلَى غَيْرِهِ، فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ هَلَاكٌ لِأَمَانَاتِكُمْ، وَخِيَانَةٌ لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيّ: إِذَا خَانُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ، فَقَدْ خَانُوا أَمَانَاتِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: كَانُوا يَسْمَعُونَ مِنَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ الْحَدِيثَ فَيُفْشُونَهُ حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ. وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ [بْنِ أَسْلَمَ] نَهَاكُمْ أَنْ تَخُونُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ، كَمَا صَنَعَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّمَا أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَأَوْلادُكُمْ فِتْنَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: اخْتِبَارٌ وَامْتِحَانُ مِنْهُ لَكُمْ؛ إِذْ أَعْطَاكُمُوهَا لِيَعْلَمَ أَتَشْكُرُونَهُ عَلَيْهَا وَتُطِيعُونَهُ فِيهَا، أَوْ تَشْتَغِلُونَ بِهَا عَنْهُ، وَتَعْتَاضُونَ بِهَا مِنْهُ؟ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَأَوْلادُكُمْ فِتْنَةٌ وَاللَّهُ عِنْدَهُ أَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ [التَّغَابُنِ: ١٥] ،وَقَالَ: ﴿وَنَبْلُوكُمْ بِالشَّرِّ وَالْخَيْرِ فِتْنَةً﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٣٥] ،وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُلْهِكُمْ أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَلا أَوْلادُكُمْ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَلِكَ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ [الْمُنَافِقُونَ: ٩] ،وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِنَّ مِنْ أَزْوَاجِكُمْ وَأَوْلادِكُمْ عَدُوًّا لَكُمْ فَاحْذَرُوهُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ [التَّغَابُنِ: ١٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ عِنْدَهُ أَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: ثَوَابُهُ وَعَطَاؤُهُ وَجَنَّاتُهُ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ مِنَ الْأَمْوَالِ وَالْأَوْلَادِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ يُوجَدُ مِنْهُمْ عَدُوٌّ، وَأَكْثَرُهُمْ لَا يُغْنِي عَنْكَ شَيْئًا، وَاللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ، هُوَ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ الْمَالِكُ لِلدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، وَلَدَيْهِ الثَّوَابُ الْجَزِيلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَفِي الْأَثَرِ يَقُولُ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: "ابْنَ آدَمَ، اطْلُبْنِي تَجدني، فَإِنْ وَجَدْتَنِي وجَدْتَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَإِنْ فُتُّكَ فَاتَكَ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ، وَأَنَا أَحَبُّ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ".

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ [أَنَّهُ قَالَ] ثَلَاثٌ مَنْ كُنَّ فِيهِ وَجَدَ بِهِنَّ حَلَاوَةَ الْإِيمَانِ: مَنْ كَانَ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَحَبَّ إِلَيْهِ مِمَّا سِوَاهُمَا، وَمَنْ كَانَ يُحِبُّ الْمَرْءَ لَا يُحِبُّهُ إِلَّا لِلَّهِ، وَمَنْ كَانَ أَنْ يُلْقَى فِي النَّارِ أَحَبَّ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ أَنْ يَرْجِعَ إِلَى الْكُفْرِ بَعْدَ إِذْ أَنْقَذَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْهُ" 

بَلْ حُبُّ رَسُولِهِ مُقَدَّمٌ عَلَى الْأَوْلَادِ وَالْأَمْوَالِ وَالنُّفُوسِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَا يُؤْمِنُ أَحَدُكُمْ حَتَّى أَكُونَ أَحَبَّ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ نَفْسِهِ وَأَهْلِهِ وَمَالِهِ وَالنَّاسِ أَجْمَعِينَ"

---

## 8:29 — verse 29

### Translation

Ibn Abbas, al-Suddi, Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, and Muqatil ibn Hayyan said regarding {furqan}: it means a way out.

Mujahid added: in this world and the next.

In another report from Ibn Abbas: {furqan} means deliverance. And in another report from him: it means help/victory.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: {furqan} means a distinction between truth and falsehood.

This explanation from Ibn Ishaq is more general than what preceded, and it may well necessitate all of it. For whoever fears Allah by carrying out His commands and abandoning what He has forbidden is granted the ability to distinguish truth from falsehood, and this becomes a cause of his help, his deliverance, and his way out from the affairs of this world, and of his happiness on the Day of Resurrection, and of the expiation of his sins (which is their erasure) and their forgiveness (which is their concealment from the people), becoming thereby a means of attaining Allah's abundant reward, as the Exalted said: {O you who believe, fear Allah and believe in His Messenger; He will give you a double portion of His mercy, and make for you a light by which you may walk, and forgive you, and Allah is Forgiving, Merciful} [al-Hadid: 28].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، والسُّدِّيّ، ومُجاهِد، وعِكْرِمة، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وقَتَادة، ومُقَاتِل بن حَيَّان: ﴿فُرْقَانًا﴾

مَخْرَجًا. زَادَ مُجَاهِدٌ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فُرْقَانًا﴾ نَجَاةً. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ: نَصْرًا.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: ﴿فُرْقَانًا﴾ أَيْ: فَصْلًا بَيْنَ الْحَقِّ وَالْبَاطِلِ.

وَهَذَا التَّفْسِيرُ مِنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ أَعَمُّ مِمَّا تَقَدَّمَ وَقَدْ يَسْتَلْزِمُ ذَلِكَ كُلَّهُ؛ فَإِنَّ مَنِ اتَّقَى اللَّهَ بِفِعْلِ أَوَامِرِهِ وَتَرْكِ زَوَاجِرِهِ، وُفِّقَ لِمَعْرِفَةِ الْحَقِّ مِنَ الْبَاطِلِ، فَكَانَ ذَلِكَ سَبَبَ نَصْرِهِ وَنَجَاتِهِ وَمَخْرَجِهِ مِنْ أُمُورِ الدُّنْيَا، وَسَعَادَتِهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَتَكْفِيرِ ذُنُوبِهِ -وَهُوَ مَحْوُهَا -وَغَفْرُهَا: سَتْرُهَا عَنِ النَّاسِ -سَبَبًا لِنَيْلِ ثَوَابِ اللَّهِ الْجَزِيلِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَآمِنُوا بِرَسُولِهِ يُؤْتِكُمْ كِفْلَيْنِ مِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ وَيَجْعَلْ لَكُمْ نُورًا تَمْشُونَ بِهِ وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ: ٢٨] .

---

## 8:30 — verse 30

### Translation

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and Qatadah said: {li-yuthbituka} [that is]: to shackle you, to bind you fast.

Atta and Ibn Zayd said: to imprison you.

Al-Suddi said: "al-ithbat" (the fixing/detaining) means confinement and binding.

This encompasses what both groups said, and it is the combination of the sayings, and it is what predominates in the conduct of one who intends harm against another.

Sunayd said, from Hajjaj, from Ibn Jurayj: Atta said: I heard Ubayd ibn Umayr say: When they conspired against the Prophet ﷺ to detain him, or kill him, or expel him, his uncle Abu Talib said to him: "Do you know what they have conspired against you?" He said: "They wish to bewitch me, or kill me, or expel me." Abu Talib said: "Who told you this?" He said: "My Lord." Abu Talib said: "What an excellent Lord your Lord is. Ask Him to treat you well." He said: "Should I ask Him to treat me well? Rather, He treats me well."

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: Muhammad ibn Isma'il al-Basri, known as al-Waswasi, related to me: Abd al-Hamid ibn Abi Rawwad informed us, from Ibn Jurayj, from Atta, from Ubayd ibn Umayr, from al-Muttalib ibn Abi Wada'ah, that Abu Talib said to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "What are your people conspiring against you?" He said: "They wish to bewitch me, or kill me, or expel me." He said: "Who told you this?" He said: "My Lord." He said: "What an excellent Lord your Lord is. Ask Him to treat you well." He said: "Should I ask Him to treat me well? Rather, He treats me well." He said: Then {And [remember] when those who disbelieved plotted against you, to detain you, or kill you, or expel you} was revealed, the verse.

The mention of Abu Talib in this account is very strange, indeed objectionable, because this verse is Medinan. Moreover, this story, the gathering of Quraysh for this conspiracy and consultation over detention, expulsion, or killing, occurred on the very night of the Hijrah, and that was about three years after the death of Abu Talib, when they were emboldened and dared to act against the Prophet ﷺ after the death of his uncle Abu Talib, who used to protect him, support him, and bear his burdens.

The proof of the correctness of what we have said is what the imam Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar, author of "al-Maghazi," related from Abdullah ibn Abi Najih, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas, who said: and al-Kalbi related to me, from Bathan, the freedman of Umm Hani, from Ibn Abbas: that a group of Quraysh, from the nobles of every tribe, gathered to enter the Dar al-Nadwah. Iblis appeared before them in the form of a dignified old man. When they saw him they said: "Who are you?" He said: "An old man from Najd. I heard that you had gathered, and I wished to be present with you, and my counsel and advice will not fail you." They said: "Very well, enter." So he entered with them.

He said: "Consider the matter of this man. By Allah, he is about to leap upon you in your own affair with his cause." One of them said: "Confine him in bonds, then wait for the turns of fate to befall him until he perishes as the poets before him perished, Zuhayr and al-Nabighah; he is merely like one of them." The enemy of Allah, the old man from Najd, cried out and said: "By Allah, this is not sound counsel for you. By Allah, his Lord will bring him out of his confinement to his companions, and they will soon rise up against him until they take him from your hands and protect him from you, and I do not feel secure for you that they might then drive you out of your own land. So consider something other than this."

Then one of them said: "Expel him from among you and be rid of him. For once he is gone, whatever he does and wherever he ends up will not harm you; his harm will be absent from you and you will be at ease, and his affair will concern others, not you." The old man from Najd said: "By Allah, this is not sound counsel for you either. Have you not seen the sweetness of his speech and the charm of his tongue, and how hearts are captured by what they hear from him? By Allah, if you do this, then he will canvass the Arabs, and they will unite against you, and then they will come against you until they drive you from your land and kill your nobles." They said: "He speaks truly, by Allah. So consider some other course than this."

Then Abu Jahl, may Allah curse him, said: "By Allah, I shall propose to you a plan which I do not think you will reject afterward; I see no other." They said: "What is it?" He said: "We take from every tribe a young, sturdy, well-built youth, and each youth is given a sharp sword, and then they strike him with a single blow, all together as one man. If they kill him thus, his blood will be scattered among all the tribes, and I do not think this clan of Banu Hashim will have the strength to fight all of Quraysh together. When they see this, they will accept blood money, and we will be at ease and rid of his harm."

The old man from Najd said: "This, by Allah, is the sound plan. The word is what this young man has said, no other view is sound." They then dispersed on this basis, resolved upon it.

Then Gabriel came to the Prophet ﷺ and commanded him not to spend that night in the place where he usually slept, and informed him of the people's plot.

So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ did not spend that night in his house, and Allah then gave him permission to depart. Allah revealed to him, after his arrival in Medina, Surat al-Anfal, recounting His favors upon him and His trial of him: {And [remember] when those who disbelieved plotted against you, to detain you, or kill you, or expel you. They plotted, but Allah [also] plotted, and Allah is the best of plotters}. And Allah revealed, concerning their saying "wait for the turns of fate to befall him until he perishes as the poets before him perished": {Or do they say, 'A poet, we await for him the turns of fate'} [al-Tur: 30]. That day came to be called "the Day of the Crowding" because of the gathering and the decision they had reached that day.

A similar account is related from al-Suddi. Regarding their wish to expel him, Allah revealed His saying: {And indeed, they were about to unsettle you from the land, to drive you out of it, and then they would not have remained after you except for a little} [al-Isra: 76].

Similarly, al-Awfi related from Ibn Abbas. And something similar is related from Mujahid, Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, Musa ibn Uqbah, Qatadah, Miqsam, and others.

Yunus ibn Bukayr said, from Ibn Ishaq: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ remained waiting for Allah's command, until when Quraysh had gathered and plotted against him, intending against him what they intended, Gabriel (peace be upon him) came to him and commanded him not to spend that night in the place where he used to sleep. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ called Ali ibn Abi Talib and instructed him to sleep in his bed and to cover himself with his green cloak, which he did. Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ went out past the people, who were at his door, taking with him a handful of dust, which he began scattering over their heads. Allah took away their sight from His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ, while he recited: {Ya Sin. By the wise Qur'an} up to His saying: {and We have covered them, so they do not see} [Ya Sin: 1-9].

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi said: It is related from Ikrimah something that confirms this.

Ibn Hibban related in his Sahih, and al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Uthman ibn Khuthaym, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Fatimah came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ weeping. He said: "What makes you weep, little daughter?" She said: "O father, how could I not weep, when these nobles of Quraysh are in the Hijr, swearing by al-Lat and al-Uzza and Manat, the third, the other, that if they see you they will rise up against you and kill you, and there is not one of them but has already claimed his share of your blood." He said: "O little daughter, bring me water for ablution." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ performed ablution, then went out to the mosque.
