When they saw him, they said: "There he is," and they lowered their heads, and their chins dropped before them, and they could not raise their eyes. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ took a handful of dust and threw it at them, saying: "May the faces be disgraced." And not one of them was struck by even a single pebble of it but was killed as a disbeliever on the day of Badr.

Al-Hakim then said: sound according to the criterion of Muslim, though neither of them (Bukhari and Muslim) recorded it, and I know of no defect in it.

Imam Ahmad said: Abd al-Razzaq related to us, Ma'mar informed us, Uthman al-Jazari informed me, from Miqsam, the freedman of Ibn Abbas, who informed him, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying {And [remember] when those who disbelieved plotted against you, to detain you}: he said: Quraysh consulted together one night in Mecca. Some of them said: "When morning comes, bind him fast," meaning the Prophet ﷺ. Others said: "Rather, kill him." Others said: "Rather, expel him." Allah informed His Prophet of this, so Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, spent that night in the bed of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ went out until he reached the cave. The polytheists spent the night guarding Ali, thinking him to be the Prophet ﷺ. When morning came, they rushed at him, but when they saw it was Ali, Allah had turned back their plot. They said: "Where is your companion?" He said: "I do not know." So they tracked his trail, but when they reached the mountain, it became confused for them. They climbed the mountain and passed by the cave, and they saw a spider's web over its entrance, and they said: "If he had entered here, there would not be a spider's web over its entrance." So he remained there three nights.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Muhammad ibn Ja'far ibn al-Zubayr, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, regarding His saying {They plotted, but Allah [also] plotted, and Allah is the best of plotters}: that is, "I plotted against them with My firm strategy, until I delivered you from them."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وقَتَادَةُ: ﴿لِيُثْبِتُوكَ﴾ [أَيْ] : لِيُقَيِّدُوكَ.

وَقَالَ عَطَاءٌ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ: لِيَحْبِسُوكَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيّ: "الْإِثْبَاتُ". هُوَ الْحَبْسُ وَالْوَثَاقُ.

وَهَذَا يَشْمَلُ مَا قَالَهُ هَؤُلَاءِ وَهَؤُلَاءِ، وَهُوَ مَجْمَعُ الْأَقْوَالِ وَهُوَ الْغَالِبُ مِنْ صَنِيعِ مَنْ أَرَادَ غَيْرَهُ بِسُوءٍ.

وَقَالَ سُنَيْد، عَنْ حَجَّاجٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، قَالَ عَطَاءٌ: سَمِعْتُ عُبَيْد بْنَ عُمَيْر يَقُولُ: لَمَّا ائْتَمَرُوا بِالنَّبِيِّ ﷺ لِيُثْبِتُوهُ أَوْ يَقْتُلُوهُ أَوْ يُخْرِجُوهُ، قَالَ لَهُ عَمُّهُ أَبُو طَالِبٍ: هَلْ تَدْرِي مَا ائْتَمَرُوا بِكَ؟ قَالَ: "يُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَسْحَرُونِي أَوْ يَقْتُلُونِي أَوْ يُخْرِجُونِي"، فَقَالَ: مَنْ أَخْبَرَكَ بِهَذَا؟ قَالَ: "رَبِّي"، قَالَ: نِعْمَ الرَّبُّ رَبُّكَ، اسْتَوْصِ بِهِ خَيْرًا فَقَالَ: "أَنَا أَسْتَوْصِي بِهِ؟ ! بَلْ هُوَ يَسْتَوْصِي بِي" 

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ الْبَصْرِيُّ، الْمَعْرُوفُ بِالْوَسَاوِسِيِّ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ الْحَمِيدِ بْنُ أَبِي رَوَّاد عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، عَنِ الْمُطَّلِبِ بْنِ أَبِي وَدَاعةِ، أَنَّ أَبَا طَالِبٍ قَالَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: مَا يَأْتَمِرُ بِكَ قَوْمُكَ؟ قَالَ: "يُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَسْحَرُونِي أَوْ يَقْتُلُونِي أَوْ يُخْرِجُونِي". فَقَالَ: مَنْ أَخْبَرَكَ بِهَذَا؟ قَالَ: "رَبِّي"، قَالَ: نِعْمَ الرَّبُّ رَبُّكَ، فَاسْتَوْصِ بِهِ خَيْرًا، "قَالَ: أَنَا أَسْتَوْصِي بِهِ؟! بَلْ هُوَ يَسْتَوْصِي بِي". قَالَ: فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَإِذْ يَمْكُرُ بِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لِيُثْبِتُوكَ أَوْ يَقْتُلُوكَ أَوْ يُخْرِجُوكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ وذِكر أَبِي طَالِبٍ فِي هَذَا، غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، بَلْ مُنْكَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ، ثُمَّ إِنَّ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةَ وَاجْتِمَاعَ قُرَيْشٍ عَلَى هَذَا الِائْتِمَارِ وَالْمُشَاوَرَةِ عَلَى الْإِثْبَاتِ أَوِ النَّفْيِ أَوِ الْقَتْلِ، إِنَّمَا كَانَ لَيْلَةَ الْهِجْرَةِ سَوَاءً، وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ بِنَحْوٍ مِنْ ثَلَاثِ سِنِينَ لَمَّا تَمَكَّنُوا مِنْهُ وَاجْتَرَءُوا عَلَيْهِ بَعْدَ مَوْتِ عَمِّهِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، الَّذِي كَانَ يَحُوطُهُ وَيَنْصُرُهُ وَيَقُومُ بِأَعْبَائِهِ. وَالدَّلِيلُ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا قُلْنَا: مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَار صَاحِبُ "الْمُغَازِي" عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: وَحَدَّثَنِي الْكَلْبِيُّ، عَنْ بَاذَانَ مَوْلَى أُمِّ هَانِئٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ نَفَرًا مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ مِنْ أَشْرَافِ كُلِّ قَبِيلَةٍ، اجْتَمَعُوا لِيَدْخُلُوا دَارَ النَّدْوَةِ، فَاعْتَرَضَهُمْ إِبْلِيسُ فِي صُورَةِ شَيْخٍ جَلِيلٍ، فَلَمَّا رَأَوْهُ قَالُوا: مَنْ أَنْتَ؟ قَالَ: شَيْخٌ مِنْ نَجْدٍ، سَمِعْتُ أَنَّكُمُ اجْتَمَعْتُمْ، فَأَرَدْتُ أَنْ أَحْضُرَكُمْ وَلَنْ يُعْدِمَكُمْ رَأْيِي وَنُصْحِي. قَالُوا: أَجَلْ، ادْخُلْ فَدَخَلَ مَعَهُمْ فَقَالَ: انْظُرُوا فِي شَأْنِ هَذَا الرَّجُلِ، وَاللَّهِ لَيُوشِكَنَّ أَنْ يُوَاثِبَكُمْ فِي أَمْرِكُمْ بِأَمْرِهِ. قَالَ: فَقَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ: احْبِسُوهُ فِي وِثَاقٍ، ثُمَّ تَرَبَّصُوا بِهِ رَيْبَ الْمَنُونِ، حَتَّى يَهْلِكَ كَمَا هَلَكَ مَنْ كَانَ قَبْلَهُ مِنَ الشُّعَرَاءِ: زُهَيْرٌ وَالنَّابِغَةٌ، إِنَّمَا هُوَ كَأَحَدِهِمْ، قَالَ: فَصَرَخَ عَدُوُّ اللَّهِ الشَّيْخُ النَّجْدِيُّ فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا هَذَا لَكُمْ بِرَأْيٍ، وَاللَّهِ لَيُخْرِجَنَّهُ رَبُّهُ مِنْ مَحْبِسِهِ إِلَى أَصْحَابِهِ، فَلَيُوشِكَنَّ أَنْ يَثِبُوا عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى يَأْخُذُوهُ مِنْ أَيْدِيكُمْ، فَيَمْنَعُوهُ مِنْكُمْ، فَمَا آمَنُ عَلَيْكُمْ أَنْ يُخْرِجُوكُمْ مِنْ بِلَادِكُمْ. قَالَ: فَانْظُرُوا فِي غَيْرِ هَذَا.

قَالَ: فَقَالَ قَائِلٌ مِنْهُمْ: أَخْرِجُوهُ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِكُمْ تَسْتَرِيحُوا مِنْهُ، فَإِنَّهُ إِذَا خَرَجَ لَنْ يَضُرَّكُمْ مَا صَنَعَ وَأَيْنَ وَقَعَ، إِذَا غَابَ عَنْكُمْ أَذَاهُ وَاسْتَرَحْتُمْ، وَكَانَ أَمْرُهُ فِي غَيْرِكُمْ، فَقَالَ الشَّيْخُ النَّجْدِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ مَا هَذَا لَكُمْ بِرَأْيٍ، أَلَمْ تَرَوْا حَلَاوَةَ [قَوْلِهِ] وَطَلَاوَةَ لِسَانِهِ، وَأَخْذَ الْقُلُوبِ مَا تَسْمَعُ مِنْ حَدِيثِهِ؟ وَاللَّهِ لَئِنْ فَعَلْتُمْ، ثُمَّ اسْتَعْرَضَ الْعَرَبَ، لَيَجْتَمِعَنَّ عَلَيْكُمْ ثُمَّ لَيَأْتِيَنَّ إِلَيْكُمْ حَتَّى يُخْرِجَكُمْ مِنْ بِلَادِكُمْ وَيَقْتُلَ أَشْرَافَكُمْ. قَالُوا: صَدَقَ وَاللَّهِ، فَانْظُرُوا بَابًا غَيْرَ هَذَا.

قَالَ: فَقَالَ أَبُو جَهْلٍ، لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ: وَاللَّهِ لَأُشِيرَنَّ عَلَيْكُمْ بِرَأْيٍ مَا أَرَاكُمْ تَصْرِمُونَهُ بَعْدُ، مَا أَرَى غَيْرَهُ. قَالُوا: وَمَا هُوَ؟ قَالَ: نَأْخُذُ مِنْ كُلِّ قَبِيلَةٍ غُلَامًا شَابًّا وَسِيطًا نَهِدًا، ثُمَّ يُعْطَى كُلُّ غُلَامٍ مِنْهُمْ سَيْفًا صَارِمًا، ثُمَّ يَضْرِبُونَهُ ضَرْبَةَ رَجُلٍ وَاحِدٍ، فَإِذَا قَتَلُوهُ تَفَرَّقَ دَمُهُ فِي الْقَبَائِلِ [كُلِّهَا] فَلَا أَظُنُّ هَذَا الْحَيَّ مِنْ بَنِي هَاشِمٍ يَقْوَوْنَ عَلَى حَرْبِ قُرَيْشٍ كُلِّهَا. فَإِنَّهُمْ إِذَا رَأَوْا ذَلِكَ قَبِلُوا الْعَقْلَ، وَاسْتَرَحْنَا وَقَطَعْنَا عَنَّا أَذَاهُ.

قَالَ: فَقَالَ الشَّيْخُ النَّجْدِيُّ: هَذَا وَاللَّهِ الرَّأْيُ. الْقَوْلُ مَا قَالَ الْفَتَى لَا رَأْيَ غَيْرَهُ، قَالَ: فَتَفَرَّقُوا عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَهُمْ مُجْمِعُونَ لَهُ 

فَأَتَى جِبْرِيلُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، فَأَمَرَهُ أَلَّا يَبِيتَ فِي مَضْجَعِهِ الَّذِي كَانَ يَبِيتُ فِيهِ، وَأَخْبَرَهُ بمكر القوم.

فَلَمْ يَبِتْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي بَيْتِهِ تِلْكَ اللَّيْلَةَ، وَأَذِنَ اللَّهُ لَهُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ بِالْخُرُوجِ، وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ بَعْدَ قُدُومِهِ الْمَدِينَةَ "الْأَنْفَالَ" يَذْكُرُ نِعَمَهُ عَلَيْهِ وَبَلَاءَهُ عِنْدَهُ: ﴿وَإِذْ يَمْكُرُ بِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لِيُثْبِتُوكَ أَوْ يَقْتُلُوكَ أَوْ يُخْرِجُوكَ وَيَمْكُرُونَ وَيَمْكُرُ اللَّهُ وَاللَّهُ خَيْرُ الْمَاكِرِينَ﴾ وَأَنْزَلَ [اللَّهُ] فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: "تَرَبَّصُوا بِهِ رَيْبَ الْمَنُونِ، حَتَّى يَهْلِكَ كَمَا هَلَكَ مَنْ كَانَ قَبْلَهُ مِنَ الشُّعَرَاءِ"، ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ شَاعِرٌ نَتَرَبَّصُ بِهِ رَيْبَ الْمَنُونِ﴾ [الطَّوْرِ: ٣٠] وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمُ يُسَمَّى "يَوْمَ الزَّحْمَةِ" لِلَّذِي اجْتَمَعُوا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الرَّأْيِ 

وَعَنِ السُّدِّيّ نَحْوُ هَذَا السِّيَاقِ، وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِي إِرَادَتِهِمْ إِخْرَاجَهُ قَوْلَهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ كَادُوا لَيَسْتَفِزُّونَكَ مِنَ الأرْضِ لِيُخْرِجُوكَ مِنْهَا وَإِذًا لَا يَلْبَثُونَ خِلافَكَ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٧٦] .

وَكَذَا رَوَى العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَرُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وعُرْوة بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، وَمُوسَى بْنِ عُقْبَة، وقَتَادَةَ، ومِقْسَم، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ، نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ يُونُسُ بْنُ بُكَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ: فَأَقَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَنْتَظِرُ أَمْرَ اللَّهِ، حَتَّى إِذَا اجْتَمَعَتْ قُرَيْشٌ فَمَكَرَتْ بِهِ، وَأَرَادُوا بِهِ مَا أَرَادُوا، أَتَاهُ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَأَمَرَهُ أَلَّا يَبِيتَ فِي مَكَانِهِ الَّذِي كَانَ يَبِيتُ فِيهِ فَدَعَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلِيَّ بْنَ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، فَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يَبِيتَ عَلَى فِرَاشِهِ وَأَنْ يَتَسَجَّى ببُرد لَهُ أَخْضَرَ، فَفَعَلَ. ثُمَّ خَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَى الْقَوْمِ وَهُمْ عَلَى بَابِهِ، وخَرَج مَعَهُ بِحَفْنَةٍ مِنْ تُرَابٍ، فَجَعَلَ يذرها على رؤوسهم، وَأَخَذَ اللَّهُ بِأَبْصَارِهِمْ عَنْ نَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ وَهُوَ يَقْرَأُ: ﴿يس وَالْقُرْآنِ الْحَكِيمِ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَأَغْشَيْنَاهُمْ فَهُمْ لَا يُبْصِرُونَ﴾ [يس: ١-٩] .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: رُوِيَ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ مَا يُؤَكِّدُ هَذَا 

وَقَدْ رَوَى [أَبُو حَاتِمِ] ابْنُ حِبَّان فِي صَحِيحِهِ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ خُثَيْم، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: دَخَلَتْ فاطمةُ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهِيَ تَبْكِي، فَقَالَ: "مَا يُبْكِيكِ يَا بُنَيَّة؟ " قَالَتْ: يَا أَبَتِ، [وَ] مَا لِي لَا أَبْكِي، وَهَؤُلَاءِ الْمَلَأُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ فِي الحجْر يَتَعَاقَدُونَ بِاللَّاتِ والعُزَّى وَمَنَاةَ الثَّالِثَةِ الْأُخْرَى، لَوْ قَدْ رَأَوْكَ لَقَامُوا إِلَيْكَ فَيَقْتُلُونَكَ، وَلَيْسَ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا مَنْ قَدْ عَرَفَ نَصِيبَهُ مِنْ دَمِكَ. فَقَالَ: "يَا بُنَيَّةُ، ائْتِنِي بوَضُوء". فَتَوَضَّأَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، ثُمَّ خَرَجَ إِلَى الْمَسْجِدِ. فَلَمَّا رَأَوْهُ قَالُوا: إِنَّمَا هُوَ ذَا فطأطؤوا رؤوسهم، وَسَقَطَتْ أَذْقَانُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ، فَلَمْ يَرْفَعُوا أَبْصَارَهُمْ. فَتَنَاوَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَبْضَةً مِنْ تُرَابٍ فَحَصَبَهُمْ بِهَا، وَقَالَ: "شَاهَتِ الْوُجُوهُ". فَمَا أَصَابَ رَجُلًا مِنْهُمْ حَصَاة مِنْ حَصَيَاتِهِ إِلَّا قُتل يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ كَافِرًا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْحَاكِمُ: صَحِيحٌ عَلَى شَرْطِ مُسْلِمٍ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ، ولا أعرف له علة وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، أَخْبَرَنِي عُثْمَانُ الجَزَري، عَنْ مِقْسَم مَوْلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَخْبَرَهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذْ يَمْكُرُ بِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لِيُثْبِتُوكَ﴾ قَالَ: تَشَاوَرَتْ قُرَيْشٌ لَيْلَةً بِمَكَّةَ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: إِذَا أَصْبَحَ فَأَثْبِتُوهُ بِالْوِثَاقِ -يُرِيدُونَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ -وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: بَلِ اقْتُلُوهُ. وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: بَلْ أَخْرِجُوهُ. فَأَطْلَعُ اللَّهُ نَبِيَّهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، فَبَاتَ عَلِيٌّ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ عَلَى فِرَاشِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى لَحِقَ بِالْغَارِ، وَبَاتَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ يَحْرُسُونَ عَلِيًّا يَحْسَبُونَهُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، فَلَمَّا أَصْبَحُوا ثَارُوا إِلَيْهِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَوْا عَلِيًّا رَدَّ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مَكْرَهُمْ، فَقَالُوا: أَيْنَ صَاحِبُكَ هَذَا؟ قَالَ: لَا أَدْرِي. فَاقْتَصَّا أَثَرَهُ، فَلَمَّا بَلَغُوا الْجَبَلَ اخْتَلَطَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَصَعَدُوا فِي الْجَبَلِ فَمَرُّوا بِالْغَارِ، فَرَأَوْا عَلَى بَابِهِ نَسْجَ الْعَنْكَبُوتِ، فَقَالُوا: لَوْ دَخَلَ هَاهُنَا لَمْ يَكُنْ نَسْجُ الْعَنْكَبُوتِ عَلَى بَابِهِ، فَمَكَثَ فِيهِ ثَلَاثَ لَيَالٍ 

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عُرْوَة بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَيَمْكُرُونَ وَيَمْكُرُ اللَّهُ وَاللَّهُ خَيْرُ الْمَاكِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَمَكَرْتُ بِهِمْ بِكَيْدِيَ الْمَتِينِ، حَتَّى خَلَّصْتُكَ مِنْهُمْ.

---

## 8:31-33 — verses 31-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Almighty informs us of the disbelief of the Quraysh, their haughtiness, their rebellion and obstinacy, and their false claim when His verses were recited to them, that they would say: {We have already heard. If we wished we could say the like of this.} This was mere talk on their part, not action. Otherwise, they had been challenged more than once to bring forth a surah like it, and they found no way to do so. This was only a statement by which they deceived themselves and those who followed them in their falsehood.

It has been said that the one who said this was al-Nadr ibn al-Harith, may God curse him, as was stated explicitly by Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Suddi, Ibn Jurayj and others. He, may God curse him, had gone to the land of Persia and learned there the tales of their kings, Rustam and Isfandiyar. When he returned he found that the Messenger of God ﷺ had already been sent by God and was reciting the Qur'an to the people. So whenever the Prophet ﷺ rose from a gathering, al-Nadr would sit in his place and relate to them those stories, then say: "By God, whose tales are better, mine or Muhammad's?" For this reason, when God empowered the Muslims over him on the day of Badr and he fell among the captives, the Messenger of God ﷺ ordered that his neck be struck in captivity before him, and this was done, and praise belongs to God. The one who had captured him was al-Miqdad ibn al-Aswad, may God be pleased with him, as Ibn Jarir said:

[chain] Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: The Prophet ﷺ had 'Uqbah ibn Abi Mu'ayt, Tu'aymah ibn 'Adi, and al-Nadr ibn al-Harith executed in captivity on the day of Badr. Al-Miqdad had captured al-Nadr, and when the Prophet ordered his execution, al-Miqdad said, "O Messenger of God, my captive!" The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "He used to say concerning the Book of God, Mighty and Majestic, what he used to say." So the Messenger of God ﷺ ordered his execution. Al-Miqdad said again, "O Messenger of God, my captive!" The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "O God, enrich al-Miqdad from Your bounty." Al-Miqdad said, "This is what I wanted." Ibn Jubayr said: It was concerning him that this verse was revealed: {And when Our verses are recited to them they say, We have already heard. If we wished we could say the like of this. This is nothing but tales of the ancients.}

Hushaym likewise related it from Abu Bishr Ja'far ibn Abi Wahshiyyah, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said "al-Mut'im ibn 'Adi" instead of "Tu'aymah," but this is a mistake, because al-Mut'im ibn 'Adi was not alive on the day of Badr. This is why the Messenger of God ﷺ said on that day, "If al-Mut'im were alive and asked me concerning these foul ones," meaning the captives, "I would have granted them to him," because al-Mut'im had given the Messenger of God ﷺ protection on the day he returned from Ta'if.

The meaning of {tales of the ancients}, which is the plural of usturah (legendary tale), is that these were their books which he had gathered, learning from them and reciting them to the people. This is sheer falsehood, as God informs us of them in the other verse: {And they say, Tales of the ancients which he has had written down, so they are dictated to him morning and evening. Say: He who knows the secret in the heavens and the earth has sent it down. Indeed He is ever Forgiving and Merciful} [al-Furqan: 5-6], meaning, forgiving and merciful toward whoever repents to Him and turns back, for He accepts from him and pardons him.

Concerning His saying: {And when they said, O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment}, this stemmed from the depth of their ignorance, their haughtiness, their obstinacy, and the intensity of their denial. This is one of the things for which they are blamed. It would have been more fitting for them to say, "O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then guide us to it and grant us success in following it." But instead they sought to hasten their own ruin, and they hastened the punishment and its advance, as God Almighty says: {And they urge you to hasten the punishment. Were it not for an appointed term, the punishment would have come to them, and it will surely come upon them suddenly while they perceive it not} [al-'Ankabut: 53], {And they said, Our Lord, hasten for us our share before the Day of Reckoning} [Sad: 16], {A questioner asked concerning a punishment about to befall the disbelievers, which none can avert, from God, Lord of the ascending stairways} [al-Ma'arij: 1-3]. Likewise the ignorant among the past nations spoke this way, as the people of Shu'ayb (peace be upon him) said to him: {Then cause fragments of the sky to fall upon us, if you are among the truthful} [al-Shu'ara: 187]. And these people said: {O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment}.

Shu'bah reported, from 'Abd al-Hamid, the companion of al-Ziyadi, from Anas ibn Malik, who said: He was Abu Jahl ibn Hisham, who said, {O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment}. So there was revealed: {And God would not punish them while you are among them, and God would not punish them while they seek forgiveness}, the verse.

Al-Bukhari related it from Ahmad and Muhammad ibn al-Nadr, both from 'Ubayd Allah ibn Mu'adh, from his father, from Shu'bah, with this chain.

This Ahmad is Ahmad ibn al-Nadr ibn 'Abd al-Wahhab, as stated by al-Hakim Abu Ahmad and al-Hakim Abu 'Abdillah al-Nisaburi. God knows best.

Al-A'mash said, from a man, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, concerning His saying: {And when they said, O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment}: he said, this was al-Nadr ibn al-Harith ibn Kaladah. He said: So God sent down: {A questioner asked concerning a punishment about to befall the disbelievers, which none can avert} [al-Ma'arij: 1-2]. Mujahid, 'Ata', Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Suddi said likewise, that it was al-Nadr ibn al-Harith. 'Ata' added: So God Almighty said, {And they said, Our Lord, hasten for us our share before the Day of Reckoning} [Sad: 16], and He said, {And you have indeed come to Us alone, just as We created you the first time} [al-An'am: 94], and He said, {A questioner asked concerning a punishment about to befall the disbelievers, which none can avert} [al-Ma'arij: 1-2]. 'Ata' said: Indeed some ten-odd verses of the Book of God, Mighty and Majestic, were revealed concerning him.

Ibn Murdawayh said: [chain] Ibn Buraydah, from his father, who said: I saw 'Amr ibn al-'As standing on the day of Uhud upon a horse, saying, "O God, if what Muhammad says is true, then make me and my horse sink into the earth."

Qatadah said, concerning His saying, {And when they said, O God, if this is indeed the truth from You}, the verse: he said, this was said by the fools and ignorant ones of this ummah, and so God, through His grace and mercy, turned back His mercy upon the fools and ignorant ones of this ummah.

Concerning His saying: {And God would not punish them while you are among them, and God would not punish them while they seek forgiveness}, Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn 'Abbas said: The polytheists used to circle the House saying, "At Your service, O God, at Your service, at Your service, You have no partner." Then the Prophet ﷺ would say, "Enough, enough!" And they would say, "You have no partner, except a partner who is Yours, whom You possess along with what he possesses." And they would say, "Your forgiveness, Your forgiveness." So God sent down: {And God would not punish them while you are among them, and God would not punish them while they seek forgiveness}. Ibn 'Abbas said: There were two safeguards among them: the Prophet ﷺ, and seeking forgiveness. The Prophet ﷺ departed, but seeking forgiveness remained.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Yazid ibn Ruman and Muhammad ibn Qays said: The Quraysh said to one another, "Muhammad, may God honor him among us," and they said: {O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring upon us a painful punishment}. But when evening came they regretted what they had said, and said, "Your forgiveness, O God!" So God, Mighty and Majestic, sent down: {And God would not punish them while you are among them, and God would not punish them while they seek forgiveness}, up to His saying, {but most of them do not know} [al-Anfal: 34].

'Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn 'Abbas, concerning {And God would not punish them while you are among them}: he said, God would not punish a people while their prophets are still living among them, until He removes them. Then he said, concerning {And God would not punish them while they seek forgiveness}: he said, among them were those for whom God had already decreed entry into faith, which is seeking forgiveness, meaning they prayed, referring by this to the people of Mecca.

Similar has been related from Mujahid, 'Ikrimah, 'Atiyyah al-'Awfi, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Suddi.

Al-Dahhak and Abu Malik said: {And Allah would not punish them while they seek forgiveness} means the believers who were in Mecca.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Abd al-Ghaffar ibn Dawud narrated to us, al-Nadr ibn Arabi narrated to us, [he said]: Ibn Abbas said: Allah placed in this ummah two securities that continue to protect them and shield them from the onslaughts of punishment as long as they remain present among them. One security Allah has already taken back to Himself, and one security remains among you. This is His saying: {And Allah would not punish them while you are among them, and Allah would not punish them while they seek forgiveness.}

Abu Salih Abd al-Ghaffar said: one of our companions told me that al-Nadr ibn Arabi narrated this hadith to him, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas.

Ibn Mardawayh and Ibn Jarir narrated something similar from Abu Musa al-Ashari, and likewise it was narrated from Qatadah and Abu al-Ala al-Nahwi al-Muqri.

Al-Tirmidhi said: [chain] Sufyan ibn Waki narrated to us, Ibn Numayr narrated to us, from Ismail ibn Ibrahim ibn Muhajir, from Abbad ibn Yusuf, from Abu Burdah ibn Abi Musa, from his father, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah has sent down to me two securities for my ummah: {And Allah would not punish them while you are among them, and Allah would not punish them while they seek forgiveness.} When I have passed away, I leave among them seeking forgiveness until the Day of Resurrection."

Corroborating this is what Imam Ahmad narrated in his Musnad, and al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Wahb: Amr ibn al-Harith informed me, from Darraj, from Abu al-Haytham, from Abu Said, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Satan said: 'By Your might, O Lord, I will not cease to lead Your servants astray as long as their spirits remain in their bodies.' The Lord said: 'By My might and majesty, I will not cease to forgive them as long as they seek My forgiveness.'"

Then al-Hakim said: its chain is authentic (sahih), and the two of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) did not record it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Muawiyah ibn Amr narrated to us, Rishdin, that is, ibn Sad, narrated to us, Muawiyah ibn Sad al-Tujibi narrated to me, from one who narrated to him, from Fadalah ibn Ubayd, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "The servant is secure from Allah's punishment as long as he seeks Allah's forgiveness, Mighty and Majestic is He."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ كُفْرِ قُرَيْشٍ وعُتُوِّهم وتمرُّدهم وَعِنَادِهِمْ، وَدَعْوَاهُمُ الْبَاطِلَ عِنْدَ سَمَاعِ آيَاتِهِ حِينَ تُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ أَنَّهُمْ يَقُولُونَ: ﴿قَدْ سَمِعْنَا لَوْ نَشَاءُ لَقُلْنَا مِثْلَ هَذَا﴾ وَهَذَا مِنْهُمْ قَوْلٌ لَا فِعْلٌ، وَإِلَّا فَقَدَ تُحُدُّوا غَيْرَ مَا مَرَّةٍ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِسُورَةٍ مِنْ مِثْلِهِ فَلَا يَجِدُونَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ سَبِيلًا. وَإِنَّمَا هَذَا قَوْلٌ مِنْهُمْ يَغُرّون بِهِ أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَهُمْ عَلَى بَاطِلِهِمْ.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ الْقَائِلَ لِذَلِكَ هُوَ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ -كَمَا قَدْ نَصَّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر، والسُّدِّيّ، وَابْنُ جُرَيج وَغَيْرُهُمْ؛ فَإِنَّهُ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ -كَانَ قَدْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى بِلَادِ فَارِسَ، وَتَعَلَّمَ مِنْ أَخْبَارِ مُلُوكِهِمْ رُسْتم وَاسْفَنْدِيَارَ، وَلَمَّا قَدِمَ وَجَدَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَدْ بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ، وَهُوَ يَتْلُو عَلَى النَّاسِ الْقُرْآنَ، فَكَانَ إِذَا قَامَ ﷺ مِنْ مَجْلِسٍ، جَلَسَ فِيهِ النَّضْرُ فَيُحَدِّثُهُمْ مِنْ أَخْبَارِ أُولَئِكَ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: بِاللَّهِ أَيُّهُمَا أَحْسَنُ قَصَصًا؟ أَنَا أَوْ مُحَمَّدٌ؟ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا أَمْكَنَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مِنْهُ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ وَوَقَعَ فِي الْأُسَارَى، أَمْرَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنْ تُضْرَبَ رَقَبَتُهُ صَبْرًا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، ففُعل ذَلِكَ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ. وَكَانَ الَّذِي أسره المقداد بن الْأَسْوَدِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بشَّار، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَة، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْر، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر قَالَ: قَتَل النَّبِيُّ ﷺ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ صَبْرًا عُقْبَةَ بْنَ أَبِي مُعَيْط وطُعَيْمة بْنَ عَدِي، وَالنَّضْرَ بْنَ الْحَارِثِ. وَكَانَ الْمِقْدَادُ أَسَرَ النَّضْرَ، فَلَمَّا أَمَرَ بِقَتْلِهِ، قَالَ الْمِقْدَادُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَسِيرِي. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: " إِنَّهُ كَانَ يَقُولُ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مَا يَقُولُ". فَأَمَرَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِقَتْلِهِ، فَقَالَ الْمِقْدَادُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَسِيرِي. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اللَّهُمَّ أَغْنِ الْمِقْدَادَ مِنْ فَضْلِكَ". فَقَالَ الْمِقْدَادُ: هَذَا الَّذِي أَرَدْتُ. قَالَ: وَفِيهِ أُنْزِلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَإِذَا تُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتُنَا قَالُوا قَدْ سَمِعْنَا لَوْ نَشَاءُ لَقُلْنَا مِثْلَ هَذَا إِنْ هَذَا إِلا أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ 

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ هُشَيْم، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي وَحْشِيّة، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر؛ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "الْمُطْعِمَ بْنَ عَدِيٍّ" "بَدَلَ طُعَيْمَةَ" وَهُوَ غَلَطٌ؛ لِأَنَّ الْمُطْعِمَ بْنَ عَدِيٍّ لَمْ يَكُنْ حَيًّا يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمَئِذٍ: "لَوْ كَانَ الْمُطْعِمُ حَيًّا، ثُمَّ سَأَلَنِي فِي هَؤُلَاءِ النَّتْنَى لَوَهَبْتُهُمْ لَهُ" -يَعْنِي: الْأُسَارَى -لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ قَدْ أَجَارَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمَ رَجَعَ مِنَ الطَّائِفِ.

وَمَعْنَى: ﴿أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ وَهُوَ جَمْعُ أُسْطُورَةٍ، أَيْ: كُتُبُهُمُ اقْتَبَسَهَا، فَهُوَ يَتَعَلَّمُ مِنْهَا وَيَتْلُوهَا عَلَى النَّاسِ. وَهَذَا هُوَ الْكَذِبُ الْبَحْتُ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَقَالُوا أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ اكْتَتَبَهَا فَهِيَ تُمْلَى عَلَيْهِ بُكْرَةً وَأَصِيلا قُلْ أَنزلَهُ الَّذِي يَعْلَمُ السِّرَّ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ إِنَّهُ كَانَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٥، ٦] .أَيْ: لِمَنْ تَابَ إِلَيْهِ وَأَنَابَ؛ فَإِنَّهُ يَتَقَبَّلُ مِنْهُ وَيَصْفَحُ عَنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ هَذَا مِنْ كَثْرَةِ جَهْلِهِمْ وعُتُوِّهم وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَشِدَّةِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ، وَهَذَا مِمَّا عِيبُوا بِهِ، وَكَانَ الْأَوْلَى لَهُمْ أَنْ يَقُولُوا: "اللَّهُمَّ، إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ، فَاهْدِنَا لَهُ، وَوَفِّقْنَا لِاتِّبَاعِهِ". وَلَكِنِ اسْتَفْتَحُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَاسْتَعْجَلُوا الْعَذَابَ، وَتَقْدِيمَ الْعُقُوبَةِ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَلَوْلا أَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى لَجَاءَهُمُ الْعَذَابُ وَلَيَأْتِيَنَّهُمْ بَغْتَةً وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ:٥٣] ، ﴿وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا عَجِّلْ لَنَا قِطَّنَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ [ص:١٦] ، ﴿سَأَلَ سَائِلٌ بِعَذَابٍ وَاقِعٍ لِلْكَافِرينَ لَيْسَ لَهُ دَافِعٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ ذِي الْمَعَارِجِ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١-٣] ،وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ الْجَهَلَةُ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ السَّالِفَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ قَوْمُ شُعَيْبٍ لَهُ: ﴿فَأَسْقِطْ عَلَيْنَا كِسَفًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١٨٧] ،وَقَالَ هَؤُلَاءِ: ﴿اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾

قَالَ شُعْبَة، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ، صَاحِبِ الزِّيَادِيِّ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: هُوَ أَبُو جَهْلِ بْنُ هِشَامٍ قَالَ: ﴿اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّمِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ فَنَزَلَتْ ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ أَحْمَدَ وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ النَّضْرِ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنُ مُعَاذ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، بِهِ 

وَأَحْمَدُ هَذَا هُوَ: أَحْمَدُ بْنُ النَّضْرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْوَهَّابِ. قَالَهُ الْحَاكِمُ أَبُو أَحْمَدَ، وَالْحَاكِمُ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ النَّيْسَابُورِيُّ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ كَلَدَةَ، قَالَ: فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿سَأَلَ سَائِلٌ بِعَذَابٍ وَاقِعْ لِلْكَافِرِينَ لَيْسَ لَهُ دَافِع﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١-٢] وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعَطَاءٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: إِنَّهُ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ -زَادَ عَطَاءٌ: فَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا عَجِّلْ لَنَا قِطَّنَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِالْحِسَابِ﴾ [ص: ١٦] وَقَالَ ﴿وَلَقَدْ جِئْتُمُونَا فُرَادَى كَمَا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٤] وَقَالَ ﴿سَأَلَ سَائِلٌ بِعَذَابٍ وَاقِعٍ لِلْكَافِرينَ لَيْسَ لَهُ دَافِعٌ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١، ٢] ، قَالَ عَطَاءٌ: وَلَقَدْ أُنْزِلَ فِيهِ بِضْعَ عَشْرَةَ آيَةً مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مُرْدُوَيْه: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ اللَّيْثِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو غَسَّانَ حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو تُمَيْلة، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، عَنِ ابْنِ بُرَيْدة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: رَأَيْتُ عَمْرَو بْنَ الْعَاصِ وَاقِفًا يَوْمَ أُحُد عَلَى فَرَسٍ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنْ كَانَ مَا يَقُولُ مُحَمَّدٌ حَقًّا، فَاخْسِفْ بِي وَبِفَرَسِي".

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: قَالَ ذَلِكَ سَفَهَةُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ وَجَهَلَتُهَا فَعَادَ اللَّهُ بِعَائِدَتِهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ عَلَى سَفَهَةِ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ وَجَهَلَتِهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو حُذَيْفَةَ مُوسَى بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عِكْرِمة بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي زُمَيْل سِمَاك الْحَنَفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ يَطُوفُونَ بِالْبَيْتِ وَيَقُولُونَ: لَبَّيْكَ اللَّهُمَّ لَبَّيْكَ، لَبَّيْكَ لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ فَيَقُولُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "قَدْ قَدْ"! وَيَقُولُونَ: لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ، إِلَّا شَرِيكًا هُوَ لَكَ، تَمْلِكُهُ وَمَا مَلَكَ. وَيَقُولُونَ: غُفْرَانَكَ، غُفْرَانَكَ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ فِيهِمْ أَمَانَانَ: النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، وَالِاسْتِغْفَارُ، فَذَهَبَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ وبقي الاستغفار وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مَعْشَر، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ رُومَان وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ قَالَا قَالَتْ قُرَيْشٌ بَعْضُهَا لِبَعْضٍ: مُحَمَّدٌ أَكْرَمُهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَيْنِنَا: ﴿اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ فَلَمَّا أَمْسَوْا نَدِمُوا عَلَى مَا قَالُوا، فَقَالُوا: غُفْرَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ! فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ [لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ] مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ:٣٤] .

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: مَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَ قَوْمًا وَأَنْبِيَاؤُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهِمْ حَتَّى يُخْرِجَهُمْ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: وَفِيهِمْ مَنْ قَدْ سَبَقَ لَهُ مِنَ اللَّهِ الدخولُ فِي الْإِيمَانِ، وَهُوَ الِاسْتِغْفَارُ -يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ، يَعْنِي: يُصَلُّونَ -يَعْنِي بِهَذَا أَهْلَ مَكَّةَ.

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ مُجاهد، وعِكْرِمَة، وَعَطِيَّةَ العَوْفي، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، والسُّدِّيّ نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ وَأَبُو مَالِكٍ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا بِمَكَّةَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْغَفَّارِ بْنُ دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ عَرَبي [قَالَ] قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ جَعَلَ فِي هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ أَمَانَيْنِ لَا يَزَالُونَ مَعْصُومِينَ مُجَارِينَ مِنْ قَوَارِعِ الْعَذَابِ مَا دَامَا بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهُمْ: فَأَمَانٌ قَبَضَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ، وَأَمَانٌ بَقِيَ فِيكُمْ، قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾

قَالَ أَبُو صَالِحٍ عَبْدُ الْغَفَّارِ: حَدَّثَنِي بَعْضُ أَصْحَابِنَا، أَنَّ النَّضْرَ بْنَ عَرَبِيٍّ حَدَّثَهُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَرْدُوَيه وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ نَحْوًا مِنْ هَذَا وَكَذَا رُوي عَنْ قَتَادَةَ وَأَبِي الْعَلَاءِ النَّحْوِيِّ الْمُقْرِئِ.

وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ نُمَيْر، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنْ عَبَّادِ بْنِ يُوسُفَ، عَنْ أَبِي بُرْدَةَ بْنِ أَبِي مُوسَى، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عليَّ أَمَانَيْنِ لِأُمَّتِي: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ فَإِذَا مَضَيْتُ، تركتُ فِيهِمُ الِاسْتِغْفَارَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ" 

وَيَشْهَدُ لِهَذَا مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ: أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ دَرَاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم قَالَ: "إِنَّ الشَّيْطَانَ قَالَ: وَعَزَّتِكَ يَا رَبِّ، لَا أَبْرَحُ أغْوِي عِبَادَكَ مَا دَامَتْ أَرْوَاحُهُمْ فِي أَجْسَادِهِمْ. فَقَالَ الرَّبُّ: وَعِزَّتِي وَجَلَالِي، لَا أَزَالُ أَغْفِرُ لَهُمْ مَا اسْتَغْفَرُونِي".

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْحَاكِمُ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا رِشْدِين -هُوَ ابْنُ سَعْدٍ -حَدَّثَنِي مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ التُّجيبي، عَمَّنْ حَدَّثَهُ، عَنْ فَضَالة بْنِ عُبَيد، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "الْعَبْدُ آمِنٌ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ مَا استغفر الله، عز وجل"

---

## 8:34-35 — verses 34-35 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that they were deserving of His punishment, but this was not brought down upon them out of blessing for the station of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ being among them. Thus when he departed from among them, Allah brought His might down upon them on the day of Badr: their chieftains were killed and their notables taken captive. And the Almighty guided them toward seeking forgiveness for the sins in which they were entangled, of shirk (associating partners with Allah) and corruption.

Qatadah, al-Suddi, and others said: the people were not seeking forgiveness, and had they been seeking forgiveness they would not have been punished.

Ibn Jarir preferred this view: had it not been for the weak believers who remained among them seeking forgiveness, the irrevocable punishment would have been brought down upon them, but it was averted from them because of those believers, just as the Almighty said regarding the day of al-Hudaybiyyah: {It is they who disbelieved and barred you from al-Masjid al-Haram, and the sacrificial animals, prevented from reaching their place of sacrifice. Had it not been for believing men and believing women whom you did not know, whom you might have trampled underfoot and on whose account guilt might have come upon you unknowingly, so that Allah might admit into His mercy whom He wills. Had they been clearly separated, We would have punished those of them who disbelieved with a painful punishment} [al-Fath: 25].

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Abza said: The Prophet ﷺ was in Mecca, so Allah revealed: {And Allah would not punish them while you are among them}. He said: Then the Prophet ﷺ went out to Medina, so Allah revealed: {Nor is Allah to punish them while they seek forgiveness}. He said: Those were the remnant of believers who remained there seeking forgiveness, meaning in Mecca. Then when they left, Allah revealed: {But why should Allah not punish them when they bar people from al-Masjid al-Haram and they are not its guardians}. He said: So Allah permitted the conquest of Mecca, and that was the punishment He had promised them.

Something similar to this has been narrated from Ibn Abbas, Abu Malik, al-Dahhak, and others.

It has also been said that this verse abrogates His statement, {Nor is Allah to punish them while they seek forgiveness}, on the basis that what is meant is the seeking of forgiveness proceeding from them themselves.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ikrimah and al-Hasan al-Basri said, regarding "al-Anfal": {And Allah would not punish them while you are among them, nor is Allah to punish them while they seek forgiveness}, this was abrogated by the verse that follows it: {But why should Allah not punish them} up to His statement {So taste the punishment for your disbelief}. So they were fought at Mecca, and hunger and hardship befell them there.

Ibn Abi Hatim likewise narrated this from the hadith of Abu Tumaylah Yahya ibn Wadih.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, regarding {Nor is Allah to punish them while they seek forgiveness}: then He excepted the people of shirk, saying [the Almighty]: {But why should Allah not punish them when they bar people from al-Masjid al-Haram}.

Regarding His statement: {But why should Allah not punish them when they bar people from al-Masjid al-Haram, and they are not its guardians? None are its guardians except the God-fearing, but most of them do not know}, meaning: how could Allah not punish them when they bar people from al-Masjid al-Haram, that is, the one at Bakkah, barring the believers who are its rightful people from praying there and circumambulating it. This is why He said: {and they are not its guardians}, meaning they are not the people of al-Masjid al-Haram; rather its people are the Prophet ﷺ and his Companions, as the Almighty said: {It is not for the polytheists to maintain the mosques of Allah while bearing witness against themselves of disbelief. Those are the ones whose deeds are void, and in the Fire they will abide forever. Only he maintains the mosques of Allah who believes in Allah and the Last Day, establishes prayer, gives zakat, and fears none but Allah. It is hoped that those will be among the rightly guided} [al-Tawbah: 17-18]. And the Almighty said: {And barring from the way of Allah, and disbelief in Him, and al-Masjid al-Haram, and expelling its people from it, is greater in the sight of Allah, and persecution is greater than killing} [al-Baqarah: 217].

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh said in his tafsir of this verse: [chain] Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked, "Who are your family (al)?" He said, "Every God-fearing person," and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited: {None are its guardians except the God-fearing}.

Al-Hakim said in his Mustadrak: [chain] Rifa'ah's grandson said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ gathered the Quraysh and said, "Is there anyone among you who is not one of you?" They said, "Among us is our sister's son, among us is our ally, and among us is our client." He said, "Our ally is from us, our sister's son is from us, and our client is from us. Indeed my guardians from among you are the God-fearing."

He then said: this hadith is sound (sahih), though the two of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) did not narrate it. Urwah, al-Suddi, and Muhammad ibn Ishaq said regarding His statement {None are its guardians except the God-fearing}: they are Muhammad ﷺ and his Companions, may Allah be pleased with them.

Mujahid said: they are those who strive (al-mujahidun), whoever they are and wherever they are.

Then the Almighty mentions what they used to rely on and practice at al-Masjid al-Haram, saying: {And their prayer at the House was nothing but whistling and clapping}. Abdullah ibn Umar, Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Abu Raja' al-Utaridi, Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, Hujr ibn Anbas, Nubayt ibn Shurayt, Qatadah, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam all said: it is whistling. Mujahid added: they used to put their fingers in their mouths.

Al-Suddi said: al-muka' is whistling like that of a white bird called "al-muka'", found in the land of the Hijaz.

Al-tasdiyah is clapping.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said regarding His statement {And their prayer at the House was nothing but whistling and clapping}: the Quraysh used to circumambulate the Ka'bah naked, whistling and clapping. Al-muka' is whistling, and they were likened to the whistling of birds, and al-tasdiyah to clapping.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah and al-Awfi likewise narrated from Ibn Abbas. Something similar has also been narrated from Ibn Umar, Mujahid, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, Abu Salamah ibn Abd al-Rahman, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, Atiyyah al-Awfi, Hujr ibn Anbas, and Ibn Abza.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Umar said regarding His statement {And their prayer at the House was nothing but whistling and clapping}: al-muka' is whistling, and al-tasdiyah is clapping. Qurrah said: Atiyyah described to us Ibn Umar's action, so Ibn Umar whistled, tilted his cheek, and clapped his hands.

It is also reported from Ibn Umar that he said: they used to place their cheeks on the ground, clapping and whistling. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this in his tafsir with his chain from him.

Ikrimah said: they used to circumambulate the House going leftward (counter to the normal direction).

Mujahid said: they only did that in order to confuse the Prophet ﷺ in his prayer.

Al-Zuhri said: they were mocking the believers.

From Sa'id ibn Jubayr and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd, regarding {and clapping}: it means their barring of people from the way of Allah, Mighty and Majestic.

Regarding His statement {So taste the punishment for what you used to disbelieve}: al-Dahhak, Ibn Jurayj, and Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: this refers to what befell them on the day of Badr, of killing and captivity. Ibn Jarir preferred this view and related no other.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Mujahid said: the punishment of those who acknowledged (the truth, but disbelieved outwardly) was by the sword, and the punishment of those who denied outright was by the Cry and the earthquake.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ أَهْلٌ لِأَنْ يُعَذِّبَهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَمْ يُوقِعْ ذَلِكَ بِهِمْ لِبَرَكَةِ مَقَامِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا خَرَجَ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهُمْ، أَوْقَعَ اللَّهُ بِهِمْ بَأْسَهُ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فقُتل صَنَادِيدُهُمْ وَأُسِرَتْ سُراتهم. وَأَرْشَدَهُمْ تَعَالَى إِلَى الِاسْتِغْفَارِ مِنَ الذُّنُوبِ، الَّتِي هُمْ مُتَلَبِّسُونَ بِهَا مِنَ الشِّرْكِ وَالْفَسَادِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ والسُّدِّي وَغَيْرُهُمَا: لَمْ يَكُنِ الْقَوْمُ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ، وَلَوْ كَانُوا يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ لَمَا عُذِّبُوا.

وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، فَلَوْلَا مَا كَانَ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهِمْ مِنَ الْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الْمُسْتَغْفِرِينَ، لَأُوقِعَ بِهِمُ الْبَأْسُ الَّذِي لَا يُرَدُّ، وَلَكِنْ دُفِعَ عَنْهُمْ بِسَبَبِ أُولَئِكَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي يَوْمِ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ: ﴿هُمُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَصَدُّوكُمْ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ وَالْهَدْيَ مَعْكُوفًا أَنْ يَبْلُغَ مَحِلَّهُ وَلَوْلا رِجَالٌ مُؤْمِنُونَ وَنِسَاءٌ مُؤْمِنَاتٌ لَمْ تَعْلَمُوهُمْ أَنْ تَطَئُوهُمْ فَتُصِيبَكُمْ مِنْهُمْ مَعَرَّةٌ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ لِيُدْخِلَ اللَّهُ فِي رَحْمَتِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ لَوْ تَزَيَّلُوا لَعَذَّبْنَا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا﴾ [الْفَتْحِ:٢٥] .

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيد، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبْزَى قَالَ: كَانَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ بِمَكَّةَ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: فَخَرَجَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: وَكَانَ أُولَئِكَ الْبَقِيَّةُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الَّذِينَ بَقُوا فِيهَا يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ -يَعْنِي بِمَكَّةَ-فَلَمَّا خَرَجُوا، أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ أَلا يُعَذِّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَهُمْ يَصُدُّونَ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ وَمَا كَانُوا أَوْلِيَاءَهُ﴾ قَالَ: فَأَذِنَ اللَّهُ فِي فَتْحِ مَكَّةَ، فَهُوَ الْعَذَابُ الَّذِي وَعَدَهُمْ.

ورُوي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبِي مَالِكٍ وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ نَحْوُ هَذَا.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ نَاسِخَةٌ لِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ عَلَى أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ صُدُورَ الِاسْتِغْفَارِ مِنْهُمْ أنفسهم.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيد، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ وَاضِحٍ، عَنِ الْحُسَيْنِ بْنِ وَاقِدٍ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ النَّحْوِيِّ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ وَالْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ قَالَا قَالَ فِي "الْأَنْفَالِ": ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَأَنْتَ فِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ فَنَسَخَتْهَا الْآيَةُ الَّتِي تَلِيهَا: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ أَلا يُعَذِّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْفُرُونَ﴾ فقُوتلوا بِمَكَّةَ، فَأَصَابَهُمْ فِيهَا الْجُوعُ وَالضُّرُّ.

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي تُمَيْلة يَحْيَى بْنِ وَاضِحٍ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الصَّبَّاحِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج وَعُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ مُعَذِّبَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ﴾ ثُمَّ اسْتَثْنَى أَهْلَ الشِّرْكِ فَقَالَ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ أَلا يُعَذِّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَهُمْ يَصُدُّونَ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ أَلا يُعَذِّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَهُمْ يَصُدُّونَ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ وَمَا كَانُوا أَوْلِيَاءَهُ إِنْ أَوْلِيَاؤُهُ إِلا الْمُتَّقُونَ وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَكَيْفَ لَا يُعَذِّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَهُمْ يَصُدُّونَ عَنِ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ أَي الَّذِي بِبَكَّةَ، يَصُدُّونَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الَّذِينَ هُمْ أَهْلُهُ عَنِ الصَّلَاةِ عِنْدَهُ وَالطَّوَافِ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا كَانُوا أَوْلِيَاءَهُ﴾ أَيْ: هُمْ لَيْسُوا أَهْلَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ، وَإِنَّمَا أَهْلُهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ وَأَصْحَابُهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ أَنْ يَعْمُرُوا مَسَاجِدَ اللَّهِ شَاهِدِينَ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ بِالْكُفْرِ أُولَئِكَ حَبِطَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ وَفِي النَّارِ هُمْ خَالِدُونَ إِنَّمَا يَعْمُرُ مَسَاجِدَ اللَّهِ مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الآخِرِ وَأَقَامَ الصَّلاةَ وَآتَى الزَّكَاةَ وَلَمْ يَخْشَ إِلا اللَّهَ فَعَسَى أُولَئِكَ أَنْ يَكُونُوا مِنَ الْمُهْتَدِينَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ١٧، ١٨] ،وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَصَدٌّ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَكُفْرٌ بِهِ وَالْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ وَإِخْرَاجُ أَهْلِهِ مِنْهُ أَكْبَرُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ [وَالْفِتْنَةُ أَكْبَرُ مِنَ الْقَتْلِ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٧] . .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُوَيه فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ -هُوَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ-حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ إِلْيَاسَ بْنِ صَدَقَةَ الْمِصْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا نُعَيْم بْنُ حَمَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا نُوحُ بْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَنْ آلُكَ؟ قَالَ كُلُّ تَقِيٍّ"، وَتَلَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: ﴿إِنْ أَوْلِيَاؤُهُ إِلا الْمُتَّقُونَ﴾ 

وَقَالَ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ الشَّافِعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو حُذَيْفَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ خُثَيْم عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عُبَيْدِ بْنِ رِفَاعَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: جَمَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قُرَيْشًا فَقَالَ: "هَلْ فِيكُمْ مِنْ غَيْرِكُمْ؟ " قَالُوا: فِينَا ابْنُ أُخْتِنَا وَفِينَا حَلِيفُنَا، وَفِينَا مَوْلَانَا. فَقَالَ: "حَلِيفُنَا مِنَّا، وَابْنُ أُخْتِنَا مِنَّا، وَمَوْلَانَا مِنَّا، إِنَّ أَوْلِيَائِي مِنْكُمُ الْمُتَّقُونَ".

ثُمَّ قَالَ: هَذَا [حَدِيثٌ] صَحِيحٌ، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجَاهُ وَقَالَ عُرْوَة، والسُّدِّي، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنْ أَوْلِيَاؤُهُ إِلا الْمُتَّقُونَ﴾ قَالَ: هُمْ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ وَأَصْحَابُهُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هُمُ الْمُجَاهِدُونَ، مَنْ كَانُوا، وَحَيْثُ كَانُوا.

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى مَا كَانُوا يَعْتَمِدُونَهُ عِنْدَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ، وَمَا كَانُوا يُعَامِلُونَهُ بِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ صَلاتُهُمْ عِنْدَ الْبَيْتِ إِلا مُكَاءً وَتَصْدِيَةً﴾ قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَرَ، وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، وَأَبُو رَجَاءٍ الْعُطَارِدِيُّ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيُّ، وحُجْر بْنُ عَنْبَس، ونُبَيْط بْنُ شُرَيْط، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: هُوَ الصَّفِيرُ -وَزَادَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَكَانُوا يُدْخِلُونَ أَصَابِعَهُمْ فِي أَفْوَاهِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: المُكَاء: الصَّفِيرُ عَلَى نَحْوِ طَيْرٍ أَبْيَضَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "المُكَاء"، وَيَكُونُ بِأَرْضِ الْحِجَازِ.

وَالتَّصْدِيَةُ: التَّصْفِيقُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو خَلاد سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ خَلَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْمُؤَدِّبُ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْأَشْعَرِيَّ -حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ صَلاتُهُمْ عِنْدَ الْبَيْتِ إِلا مُكَاءً وَتَصْدِيَةً﴾ قَالَ: كَانَتْ قُرَيْشٌ تَطُوفُ بِالْكَعْبَةِ عُرَاةً تُصَفِّرُ وَتُصَفِّقُ. وَالْمُكَاءُ: الصَّفِيرُ، وَإِنَّمَا شُبِّهُوا بِصَفِيرِ الطَّيْرِ وَتَصْدِيَةِ التَّصْفِيقِ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ والعَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، وَأَبِي سَلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وقَتَادَةَ، وَعَطِيَّةَ الْعَوْفِيِّ، وحُجْر بْنِ عَنْبَس، وَابْنِ أبزَى نَحْوُ هَذَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا قُرَّة، عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ صَلاتُهُمْ عِنْدَ الْبَيْتِ إِلا مُكَاءً وَتَصْدِيَةً﴾ قَالَ: الْمُكَاءُ: الصَّفِيرُ. وَالتَّصْدِيَةُ: التَّصْفِيقُ. قَالَ قُرَّةُ: وحَكَى لَنَا عَطِيَّةُ فِعْلَ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، فَصَفَّرَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ، وَأَمَالَ خَدَّهُ، وَصَفَّقَ بِيَدَيْهِ.

وَعَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ أَيْضًا أَنَّهُ قَالَ: كَانُوا يَضَعُونَ خُدُودَهُمْ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ ويُصَفِّقُون ويُصَفِّرُون. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ بِسَنَدِهِ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: كَانُوا يَطُوفُونَ بِالْبَيْتِ عَلَى الشِّمَالِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَإِنَّمَا كَانُوا يَصْنَعُونَ ذَلِكَ لِيَخْلِطُوا بِذَلِكَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ صِلَاتَهُ.

وَقَالَ الزُّهْرِيُّ: يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ بِالْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

وَعَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ: ﴿وَتَصْدِيَة﴾ قَالَ: صدُّهم النَّاسَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وجل.

قَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْفُرُونَ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَابْنُ جُرَيْج، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُوَ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ يَوْمَ بَدْر مِنَ الْقَتْلِ والسَّبْي. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَلَمْ يَحْكِ غَيْرَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: عَذَابُ أَهْلِ الْإِقْرَارِ بِالسَّيْفِ، وَعَذَابُ أَهْلِ التَّكْذِيبِ بِالصَّيْحَةِ وَالزَّلْزَلَةِ.

---

## 8:36-37 — verses 36-37 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: al-Zuhri, Muhammad ibn Yahya ibn Habban, Asim ibn Umar ibn Qatada, and al-Husayn ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Amr ibn Sa'id ibn Mu'adh told me, they said: when Quraysh was struck on the day of Badr and their remnant returned to Mecca, and Abu Sufyan returned with his caravan, Abdullah ibn Abi Rabi'a, Ikrima ibn Abi Jahl, and Safwan ibn Umayya went walking, along with men from Quraysh whose fathers, sons, and brothers had been struck down at Badr, and they spoke to Abu Sufyan ibn Harb and to those of Quraysh who had had merchandise in that caravan. They said: "O assembly of Quraysh, Muhammad has indeed cut you down and killed your best men, so help us with this wealth against fighting him, that we might perhaps attain vengeance from him for those of us who were struck down." And they did so. He said: it was concerning them, as has been mentioned from Ibn Abbas, that Allah, mighty and majestic, revealed: {Indeed, those who disbelieve spend their wealth [to turn people away from the path of Allah]} up to His saying: {and those who disbelieved will be gathered to Hell}.

Likewise it has been narrated from Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Hakam ibn Utayba, Qatada, al-Suddi, and Ibn Abza: that it was revealed concerning Abu Sufyan and his spending of wealth at Uhud for fighting the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

Al-Dahhak said: it was revealed concerning the people of Badr.

On every reckoning, it is general in meaning. Even if the specific occasion of its revelation was particular, Allah, exalted is He, has informed that the disbelievers spend their wealth to turn people away from following the path of truth, and they will indeed do so, then their wealth will vanish, {then it will be a source of regret for them}, that is, remorse, since it will have availed them nothing. For they intended to extinguish the light of Allah and to make their word prevail over the word of truth, while Allah is the perfecter of His light even though the disbelievers dislike it, and the supporter of His religion, the one who proclaims His word and makes His religion manifest above every other religion. So this disgrace is theirs in this world, and theirs in the Hereafter is the punishment of the Fire. Whoever among them lives on will see with his eye and hear with his ear what grieves him, and whoever among them is killed or dies will go on to eternal disgrace and everlasting punishment. For this reason He said: {So they will spend it, then it will be a source of regret for them, then they will be overcome, and those who disbelieved will be gathered to Hell}.

Regarding His saying, exalted is He: {that Allah may separate the vile from the good}, Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying {that Allah may separate the vile from the good}: that He may separate the people of felicity from the people of wretchedness. Al-Suddi said: He separates the believer from the disbeliever. This can be understood to mean that this separation occurs in the Hereafter, as He, exalted is He, said: {Then We will say to those who associated partners with Us, "Remain in your places, you and your partners." Then We will separate them from each other} [Yunus: 28], and He, exalted is He, said: {And on the Day the Hour comes, that Day they will be separated} [al-Rum: 14], and He said in another verse: {That Day they will be split apart} [al-Rum: 43], and He, exalted is He, said: {And separate yourselves today, O you criminals} [Ya-Sin: 59].

It can also be understood that this separation occurs in this world, through what becomes apparent from their deeds to the believers, in which case the letter "lam" would express the purpose behind what Allah granted the disbelievers of wealth which they spend in turning people away from the path of Allah. That is: We only empowered them to do that so that {Allah may separate the vile from the good}, meaning: those who obey Him by fighting His disbelieving enemies, from those who disobey Him by shrinking back from that, as He, exalted is He, said: {And what befell you on the day the two forces met was by permission of Allah, and that He might make known the believers, and that He might make known those who are hypocrites. And it was said to them, "Come, fight in the way of Allah or defend yourselves." They said, "If we knew combat, we would have followed you"} [Al Imran: 166-167], and He, exalted is He, said: {Allah would not leave the believers in the state you are in until He separates the vile from the good. And Allah would not let you know the unseen} [Al Imran: 179], and He, exalted is He, said: {Or do you think that you will enter Paradise while Allah has not yet made known those among you who strive, and made known those who are steadfast} [Al Imran: 142], and its counterpart is also found in Bara'a (al-Tawba).

So the meaning of the verse according to this is: We have only tried you through the disbelievers who fight you, and We empowered them to spend their wealth and expend it in that, so that the vile might be separated from the good, so that the vile would be placed one upon another, {and He heaps it together}, that is, gathers all of it, and that is the gathering of a thing one part upon another, as He, exalted is He, said concerning clouds: {then He makes it into a mass} [al-Nur: 43], meaning piled up and stacked upon each other, {and He puts it into Hell. Those, they are the losers}, meaning: these are the losers in this world and the Hereafter.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي الزُّهْرِيُّ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَحْيَى بْنِ حِبَّان، وَعَاصِمُ بْنُ عُمَرَ بْنِ قَتَادَةَ، والحُصَيْن بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مُعَاذٍ، قَالُوا: لَمَّا أُصِيبَتْ قُرَيْشٌ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَرَجَعَ فَلُّهم إِلَى مَكَّةَ، وَرَجَعَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ بِعِيرِه، مَشَى عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي رَبِيعَةَ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ بْنُ أَبِي جَهْلٍ وَصَفْوَانُ بْنُ أُمَيَّةَ، فِي رِجَالٍ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ أُصِيبَ آبَاؤُهُمْ، وَأَبْنَاؤُهُمْ وَإِخْوَانُهُمْ بِبَدْرٍ، فَكَلَّمُوا أَبَا سُفْيَانَ بْنَ حَرْبٍ وَمَنْ كَانَتْ لَهُ فِي تِلْكَ الْعِيرِ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ تِجَارَةٌ، فَقَالُوا: يَا مَعْشَرَ قُرَيْشٍ، إِنَّ مُحَمَّدًا قَدْ وَتَرَكم وَقَتَلَ خِيَارَكُمْ، فَأَعِينُونَا بِهَذَا الْمَالِ عَلَى حَرْبِهِ، لَعَلَّنَا أَنْ نُدْرِكَ مِنْهُ ثَأْرًا بِمَنْ أُصِيبَ مِنَّا! فَفَعَلُوا. قَالَ: فَفِيهِمْ -كَمَا ذُكِرَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ -أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ [لِيَصُدُّوا عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللهِ] ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِلَى جَهَنَّمَ يُحْشَرُونَ﴾ 

وَهَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، والحَكَم بْنِ عُتَيْبَةَ، وقَتَادَةَ، والسُّدِّي، وَابْنِ أبزَى: أَنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي أَبِي سُفْيَانَ وَنَفَقَتِهِ الْأَمْوَالَ فِي أُحُد لِقِتَالِ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم.

وقال الضَّحَّاكُ: نَزَلَتْ فِي أَهْلِ بَدْرٍ.

وَعَلَى كُلِّ تَقْدِيرٍ، فَهِيَ عَامَّةٌ. وَإِنْ كَانَ سَبَبُ نُزُولِهَا خَاصًّا، فَقَدْ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ الْكُفَّارَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ لِيَصُدُّوا عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ طَرِيقِ الْحَقِّ، فَسَيَفْعَلُونَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ تَذْهَبُ أَمْوَالُهُمْ، ﴿ثُمَّ تَكُونُ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسْرَةً﴾ أَيْ: نَدَامَةً؛ حَيْثُ لَمْ تُجْدِ شَيْئًا؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ أَرَادُوا إِطْفَاءَ نُورِ اللَّهِ وَظُهُورَ كَلِمَتِهِمْ عَلَى كَلِمَةِ الْحَقِّ، وَاللَّهُ مُتِمٌّ نُورَهُ وَلَوْ كَرِهَ الْكَافِرُونَ، وَنَاصِرٌ دِينَهُ، ومُعْلِن كَلِمَتَهُ، وَمُظْهِرٌ دِينَهُ عَلَى كُلِّ دِينٍ. فَهَذَا الْخِزْيُ لَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَلَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ عَذَابُ النَّارِ، فَمَنْ عَاشَ مِنْهُمْ، رَأَى بِعَيْنِهِ وَسَمِعَ بِأُذُنِهِ مَا يَسُوءُهُ، وَمَنْ قُتِل مِنْهُمْ أَوْ مَاتَ، فَإِلَى الخِزْي الْأَبَدِي وَالْعَذَابِ السَّرْمَدِيّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَسَيُنْفِقُونَهَا ثُمَّ تَكُونُ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسْرَةً ثُمَّ يُغْلَبُونَ وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِلَى جَهَنَّمَ يُحْشَرُونَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِيَمِيزَ اللَّهُ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِيَمِيزَ اللَّهُ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ﴾ فَيَمِيزَ أَهْلَ السَّعَادَةِ مِنْ أَهْلِ الشَّقَاءِ وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: يَمِيزُ الْمُؤْمِنَ مِنَ الْكَافِرِ. وَهَذَا يَحْتَمِلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ هَذَا التَّمْيِيزُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ نَقُولُ لِلَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا مَكَانَكُمْ أَنْتُمْ وَشُرَكَاؤُكُمْ فَزَيَّلْنَا بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ [يُونُسَ:٢٨] ،وَقَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَتَفَرَّقُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ١٤] ،وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ يَصَّدَّعُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ٤٣] ،وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَامْتَازُوا الْيَوْمَ أَيُّهَا الْمُجْرِمُونَ﴾ [يس:٥٩] .

وَيَحْتَمِلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ هَذَا التَّمْيِيزُ فِي الدُّنْيَا، بِمَا يَظْهَرُ مِنْ أَعْمَالِهِمْ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَتَكُونُ "اللَّامُ" مُعَلِّلَةً لِمَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ لِلْكُفَّارِ مِنْ مَالٍ يُنْفِقُونَ فِي الصَّدِّ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، أَيْ: إِنَّمَا أَقْدَرْنَاهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ؛ ﴿لِيَمِيزَ اللَّهُ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ يُطِيعُهُ بِقِتَالِ أَعْدَائِهِ الْكَافِرِينَ، أَوْ يَعْصِيهِ بِالنُّكُولِ عَنْ ذَلِكَ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَصَابَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْتَقَى الْجَمْعَانِ فَبِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ وَلِيَعْلَمَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَلِيَعْلَمَ الَّذِينَ نَافَقُوا وَقِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا قَاتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ أَوِ ادْفَعُوا قَالُوا لَوْ نَعْلَمُ قِتَالا لاتَّبَعْنَاكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:١٦٦، ١٦٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيَذَرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى مَا أَنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى يَمِيزَ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُطْلِعَكُمْ عَلَى الْغَيْبِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٧٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتُمْ أَنْ تَدْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ وَلَمَّا يَعْلَمِ اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ جَاهَدُوا مِنْكُمْ وَيَعْلَمَ الصَّابِرِينَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٤٢] وَنَظِيرَتُهَا فِي بَرَاءَةَ أَيْضًا.

فَمَعْنَى الْآيَةِ عَلَى هَذَا: إِنَّمَا ابْتَلَيْنَاكُمْ بِالْكُفَّارِ يُقَاتِلُونَكُمْ، وَأَقْدَرْنَاهُمْ عَلَى إِنْفَاقِ الْأَمْوَالِ وَبَذْلِهَا فِي ذَلِكَ؛ لِيَتَمَيَّزَ الْخَبِيثُ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ، فَيُجْعَلَ الْخَبِيثُ بَعْضُهُ عَلَى بَعْضٍ، ﴿فَيَرْكُمَهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَجْمَعَهُ كُلَّهُ، وَهُوَ جَمْعُ الشَّيْءِ بَعْضِهِ عَلَى بَعْضٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي السَّحَابِ: ﴿ثُمَّ يَجْعَلُهُ رُكَامًا﴾ [النُّورِ:٤٣] أَيْ: مُتَرَاكِمًا مُتَرَاكِبًا، ﴿فَيَجْعَلَهُ فِي جَهَنَّمَ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: هَؤُلَاءِ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

---

## 8:38-40 — verses 38-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Prophet ﷺ: {Say to those who disbelieve, if they cease} that is, from the disbelief, opposition, and obstinacy they are engaged in, and enter into Islam, obedience, and repentance, {what has already passed will be forgiven them}, that is, from their disbelief, sins, and errors, as has come in the sahih (sound) collection, from the hadith of Abu Wa'il from Ibn Mas'ud, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever does well in Islam will not be held accountable for what he did in the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic ignorance), and whoever does evil in Islam will be held accountable for the first and the last." And in the sahih as well: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Islam wipes out what came before it, and repentance wipes out what came before it."

His saying: {And if they return} that is, if they persist in what they are engaged in, {then the precedent of the former peoples has already passed}, that is, Our precedent regarding the former peoples has already passed, that when they denied and persisted in their obstinacy, We hastened the punishment and retribution upon them.

His saying: {then the precedent of the former peoples has already passed}, that is, concerning Quraysh on the day of Badr and other nations besides them. Al-Suddi and Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: that is, on the day of Badr.

His saying: {And fight them until there is no fitnah and the religion, all of it, is for Allah}. Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Ibn 'Umar, that a man came to him and said: O Abu Abd al-Rahman, do you not hear what Allah mentioned in His Book: {And if two parties among the believers fight...} [al-Hujurat: 9], so what prevents you from not fighting as Allah mentioned in His Book? He said: O son of my brother, being reproached with this verse while not fighting is more beloved to me than being reproached with the verse in which Allah, Mighty and Majestic, says: {And whoever kills a believer intentionally...} to the end of the verse [al-Nisa: 93]. He said: But Allah, Exalted is He, says: {And fight them until there is no fitnah}? Ibn 'Umar said: We did that in the time of the Prophet ﷺ, when Islam was few and a man would be persecuted (tried, tempted) in his religion, either they would kill him or they would imprison him, until Islam became numerous and there was no more fitnah. When he saw that the man would not agree with him in what he wanted, he said: What is your view of 'Ali and 'Uthman? Ibn 'Umar said: What is my view of 'Ali and 'Uthman? As for 'Uthman, Allah had pardoned him, but you disliked that He should pardon him. As for 'Ali, he is the cousin of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and his son-in-law, and he pointed with his hand, and this is his daughter, or: her daughter, where you can see.

And he told us: [chain] Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: Ibn 'Umar, may Allah be pleased with them both, came out to us, or: came to us, and a man said: What do you think of fighting in fitnah? He said: Do you know what fitnah is? Muhammad ﷺ used to fight the polytheists, and entering upon them was fitnah, and it is not like your fighting over kingship.

All of this is the wording of al-Bukhari, may Allah have mercy on him.

'Ubaydullah said, from Nafi', from Ibn 'Umar: that two men came to him during the fitnah of Ibn al-Zubayr and said: The people have done what you see, and you are the son of 'Umar ibn al-Khattab, and you are a companion of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, so what prevents you from going out? He said: What prevents me is that Allah has forbidden me the blood of my Muslim brother. They said: Did Allah not say: {And fight them until there is no fitnah and the religion, all of it, is for Allah}? He said: We fought until there was no fitnah, and the religion, all of it, was for Allah, but you want to fight until there is fitnah, and the religion belongs to other than Allah.

Hammad ibn Salamah likewise narrated it, from 'Ali ibn Zayd, from Ayyub ibn Abdullah al-Lakhmi, who said: I was with 'Abdullah ibn 'Umar, may Allah be pleased with them both, when a man came to him and said: Allah says: {And fight them until there is no fitnah and the religion, all of it, is for Allah}. Ibn 'Umar said: I and my companions fought until the religion, all of it, was for Allah, and polytheism went away, and there was no fitnah, but you and your companions fight until there is fitnah, and the religion belongs to other than Allah. Ibn Mardawayh narrated both of these.

Abu 'Awanah said, from al-A'mash, from Ibrahim al-Taymi, from his father, who said: Dhu al-Butayn, meaning Usamah ibn Zayd, said: I will never fight a man who says: There is no god but Allah. He said: Sa'd ibn Malik said: And I, by Allah, will never fight a man who says: There is no god but Allah. A man said: Did Allah not say: {And fight them until there is no fitnah and the religion, all of it, is for Allah}? They both said: We fought until there was no fitnah, and the religion, all of it, was for Allah. Ibn Mardawayh narrated it.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn 'Abbas: {And fight them until there is no fitnah} means: until there is no shirk (polytheism). Abu al-'Aliyah, Mujahid, al-Hasan, Qatadah, al-Rabi' from Anas, al-Suddi, Muqatil ibn Hayyan, and Zayd ibn Aslam said likewise.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: It has reached me from al-Zuhri, from 'Urwah ibn al-Zubayr and others among our scholars: {until there is no fitnah} means until no Muslim is persecuted (tried, tempted) away from his religion.

His saying: {and the religion, all of it, is for Allah}. Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding this verse: it means that monotheism is made sincerely for Allah.

Al-Hasan, Qatadah, and Ibn Jurayj said: {and the religion, all of it, is for Allah} means that it should be said: There is no god but Allah.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: and that monotheism should be sincere for Allah, with no polytheism in it, and that whatever rivals besides Him should be cast off. 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: {and the religion, all of it, is for Allah} means there shall be no disbelief alongside your religion.

What is established in the two sahihs bears witness to this, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "I have been commanded to fight the people until they say: There is no god but Allah. If they say it, they have protected their blood and their wealth from me, except by its right, and their reckoning is upon Allah, Mighty and Majestic." And in the two sahihs, from Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about a man who fights out of courage, and fights out of tribal zeal, and fights to be seen, which of these is in the path of Allah, Mighty and Majestic? He said: "Whoever fights so that the word of Allah is uppermost, he is in the path of Allah, Mighty and Majestic."

His saying: {But if they cease}, that is, from the disbelief they are engaged in, because of your fighting, and they refrain from it, even if you do not know their inner states, {then indeed Allah is All-Seeing of what they do}, as the Almighty says: {But if they repent, establish prayer, and give zakah, then let them go their way. Indeed Allah is Forgiving, Merciful} [al-Tawbah: 5], and in another verse: {then they are your brothers in religion} [al-Tawbah: 11].

And He says: {And fight them until there is no fitnah and the religion is for Allah. But if they cease, then there is no aggression except against the wrongdoers} [al-Baqarah: 193]. And it is established in the sahih that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Usamah, when he had raised his sword over that man, and the man said: "There is no god but Allah," and he struck him and killed him, and that was mentioned to the Messenger of Allah, and he said to Usamah: "Did you kill him after he said: There is no god but Allah? How will you deal with the words 'There is no god but Allah' on the Day of Resurrection?" He said: O Messenger of Allah, he only said it seeking protection. He said: "Did you split open his heart?" And he kept saying, repeating it to him: "Who will vouch for you regarding 'There is no god but Allah' on the Day of Resurrection?" Usamah said: I wished that I had not embraced Islam until that very day.

His saying: {And if they turn away, then know that Allah is your protector. Excellent is the protector, and excellent is the helper}, that is, if they persist in opposing you and warring against you, {then know that Allah is your protector}, your master and your helper against your enemies, so excellent is the protector and excellent is the helper.

Muhammad ibn Jarir said: [chain] Hisham ibn 'Urwah, from 'Urwah: that 'Abd al-Malik ibn Marwan wrote to him asking him about certain matters, so 'Urwah wrote back to him: "Peace be upon you. I praise to you Allah, besides whom there is no god. Now then, you wrote to me asking about the departure of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ from Mecca, and I shall inform you of it. There is no power and no strength except with Allah."

Part of what happened concerning the departure of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ from Mecca was that Allah had granted him prophethood, and what an excellent prophet, what an excellent master, what an excellent kinsman he was. May Allah reward him well, make us recognize his face in Paradise, keep us alive upon his religion, cause us to die upon it, and raise us up in accordance with it.

When he called his people to that guidance and light with which Allah had sent him, which had been revealed to him, they did not at first distance themselves from him when he began calling them to it, and they were close to listening to him, until he mentioned their false gods (tawaghit). Then some people from Quraysh who had wealth came from Ta'if, and the people rejected what he said, grew harsh toward him, disliked what he said, and incited against him those who obeyed them. So the generality of the people turned away from him and abandoned him, except for those whom Allah protected among them, and they were few. He remained in that state for as long as Allah decreed he should remain.

Then their leaders conspired together to persecute those who had followed him away from the religion of their fathers, from among their sons, brothers, and tribesmen, and there was a severe trial of shaking. So whoever was to be tried was tried, and Allah preserved whomever He willed among them. When this was done to the Muslims, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded them to go out to the land of Abyssinia. There was in Abyssinia a righteous king called "the Negus" (al-Najashi), under whom no one was wronged in his land, and he was praised for this. The land of Abyssinia was a place of trade for Quraysh, where they conducted commerce, and it was a dwelling place for their merchants, who found there abundant provision, security, and good trade. So the Prophet ﷺ commanded them to go there, and the majority of them went there when they were oppressed in Mecca and he feared for them the trials. He himself remained and did not leave.

They remained in that state for years, during which the Meccans grew harsher against those among them who had accepted Islam. Then Islam spread there, and men from among their nobles and their protectors entered into it. When the Meccans saw that, they relaxed somewhat in their treatment of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and his companions. It was the first trial that had caused those who left among the companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ to go toward the land of Abyssinia, out of fear of it and in flight from the trials and shaking they were experiencing. When this easing occurred and those among them who entered Islam did so, news of this easing spread. It reached those companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ who were in the land of Abyssinia that things had eased for those of them who were in Mecca and that they were no longer being persecuted, so they returned to Mecca, and they were nearly safe there, and they began to increase in number.

Then many people among the Ansar in Medina accepted Islam, and Islam spread in Medina, and the people of Medina began coming to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in Mecca. When Quraysh saw that, they conspired to persecute the Muslims and to be harsh with them. They seized them and were determined to persecute them, so a severe hardship befell them, and this was the last trial. Thus there were two trials: a trial that caused those who left to go out to the land of Abyssinia, when the Prophet ﷺ commanded them to do so and permitted them to go there, and a trial when they returned and saw those coming to them from the people of Medina.

Then seventy leaders (nuqaba') came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ from Medina, the chiefs of those who had accepted Islam. They met with him during the pilgrimage and gave him their pledge at al-Aqabah, giving him their covenants, saying: "We are from you and you are from us, and whoever comes from among your companions, or if you come to us yourself, we will protect you from whatever we protect ourselves from." At that, Quraysh grew harsher against the Muslims, so the Prophet ﷺ commanded his companions to go out to Medina. This was the final trial in which the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sent out his companions and then went out himself, and it was concerning this that Allah, mighty and majestic, revealed: {And fight them until there is no more trial (fitnah) and religion, all of it, belongs to Allah}.

Then he related it from Yunus ibn Abd al-A'la, from Ibn Wahb, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi al-Zinad, from his father, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr: that he wrote to al-Walid, meaning ibn Abd al-Malik ibn Marwan, with this account, and he mentioned the same as it. This is a sound (sahih) chain going back to Urwah, may Allah have mercy on him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: ﴿قُلْ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ يَنْتَهُوا﴾ أَيْ: عَمَّا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالْمُشَاقَّةِ وَالْعِنَادِ وَيَدْخُلُوا فِي الْإِسْلَامِ وَالطَّاعَةِ وَالْإِنَابَةِ، يُغْفَرُ لَهُمْ مَا قَدْ سَلَف، أَيْ: مِنْ كُفْرِهِمْ، وَذُنُوبِهِمْ وَخَطَايَاهُمْ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي وَائِلٍ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: "مَنْ أحْسَن فِي الْإِسْلَامِ، لَمْ يُؤاخَذ بِمَا عَمِلَ فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، وَمَنْ أَسَاءَ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ، أخذ بالأول والآخر" وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ أَيْضًا: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: " الْإِسْلَامُ يَجُبُّ مَا قَبْلَهُ وَالتَّوْبَةُ تَجُبُّ مَا كَانَ قَبْلَهَا".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ يَعُودُوا﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَمِرُّوا عَلَى مَا هُمْ فِيهِ، ﴿فَقَدْ مَضَتْ سُنَّةُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَقَدْ مَضَتْ سُنَّتُنَا فِي الْأَوَّلِينَ أَنَّهُمْ إِذَا كَذَّبُوا وَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى عِنَادِهِمْ، أَنَّا نُعَاجِلُهُمْ بِالْعَذَابِ وَالْعُقُوبَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَقَدْ مَضَتْ سُنَّةُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي قُرَيْشٍ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ وَغَيْرِهَا مِنَ الْأُمَمِ. وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: أَيْ: يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَاتِلُوهُمْ حَتَّى لَا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ وَيَكُونَ الدِّينُ كُلُّهُ لِلَّهِ﴾ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا حَيْوَة بْنُ شُرَيْح، عَنْ بَكْرِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ بُكَيْر، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ رَجُلًا جَاءَهُ فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، أَلَا تَسْمَعُ مَا ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ: ﴿وَإِنْ طَائِفَتَانِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ اقْتَتَلُوا﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْحُجُرَاتِ:٩] ، فَمَا يَمْنَعُكَ أَلَّا تُقَاتِلَ كَمَا ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ؟ فَقَالَ: يَا ابْنَ أَخِي، أُعَيَّر بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ وَلَا أُقَاتِلُ، أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْ أَنْ أُعَيَّر بِالْآيَةِ الَّتِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ:: ﴿وَمَنْ يَقْتُلْ مُؤْمِنًا مُتَعَمِّدًا﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ [النِّسَاءِ:٩٣] ، قَالَ: فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿وَقَاتِلُوهُمْ حَتَّى لَا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ﴾ ؟ قَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: قَدْ فَعَلْنَا عَلَى عَهْدِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ إِذْ كَانَ الْإِسْلَامُ قَلِيلًا وَكَانَ الرَّجُلُ يُفتن فِي دِينِهِ: إِمَّا أَنْ يَقْتُلُوهُ، وَإِمَّا أَنْ يُوثِقُوهُ، حَتَّى كَثُرَ الْإِسْلَامُ فَلَمْ تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى أَنَّهُ لَا يُوَافِقُهُ فِيمَا يُرِيدُ، قَالَ: فَمَا قَوْلُكَ فِي عَلِيٍّ وَعُثْمَانَ؟ قَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: مَا قَوْلِي فِي عَلِيٍّ وَعُثْمَانَ؟ أَمَّا عُثْمَانُ فَكَانَ اللَّهُ قَدْ عَفَا عَنْهُ، وَكَرِهْتُمْ أَنْ يَعْفُوَ عَنْهُ، وَأَمَّا عَلِيٌّ فَابْنُ عَمِّ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وخَتَنُه -وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ -وَهَذِهِ ابْنَتُهُ أَوْ: بِنْتُهُ -حَيْثُ تَرَوْنَ.

وَحَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا زُهَيْر، حَدَّثَنَا بَيَان أَنَّ وَبَرة حَدَّثَهُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر قَالَ: خَرَجَ عَلَيْنَا -أَوْ: إِلَيْنَا -ابْنُ عُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ: كَيْفَ تَرَى فِي قِتَالِ الْفِتْنَةِ؟ فَقَالَ: وَهَلْ تَدْرِي مَا الْفِتْنَةُ؟ كَانَ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ يُقَاتِلُ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَكَانَ الدُّخُولُ عَلَيْهِمْ فِتْنَةً، وَلَيْسَ بِقِتَالِكُمْ عَلَى الْمُلْكِ.

هَذَا كُلُّهُ سِيَاقُ الْبُخَارِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ 

وَقَالَ عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّهُ أَتَاهُ رَجُلَانِ فِي فِتْنَةِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ فَقَالَا إِنَّ النَّاسَ قَدْ صَنَعُوا مَا تَرَى، وَأَنْتَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، وَأَنْتَ صَاحِبُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَمَا يَمْنَعُكَ أَنْ تَخْرُجَ؟ قَالَ: يَمْنَعُنِي أَنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَ عليَّ دَمَ أَخِي الْمُسْلِمِ. قَالُوا: أَوْ لَمْ يَقُلِ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَقَاتِلُوهُمْ حَتَّى لَا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ وَيَكُونَ الدِّينُ كُلُّهُ لِلَّهِ﴾ ؟ قَالَ: قَدْ قَاتَلْنَا حَتَّى لَمْ تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ، وَكَانَ الدِّينُ كُلُّهُ لِلَّهِ، وَأَنْتُمْ تُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تُقَاتِلُوا حَتَّى تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ، وَيَكُونَ الدِّينُ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ.
