وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ التُّسْتَرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَرَ الْقَوَارِيرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سَالِمُ بْنُ غَيْلَانَ، سَمِعْتُ جَعْدًا أَبَا عُثْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو عُثْمَانَ النَّهْدِيُّ، عَنْ سَلْمَانَ الْفَارِسِيِّ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ الْمُسْلِمَ إِذَا لَقِيَ أَخَاهُ الْمُسْلِمَ، فَأَخَذَ بِيَدِهِ، تَحَاتَّتْ عَنْهُمَا ذُنُوبُهُمَا، كَمَا يَتَحَاتُّ الْوَرَقُ عَنِ الشَّجَرَةِ الْيَابِسَةِ فِي يَوْمِ رِيحٍ عَاصِفٍ، وَإِلَّا غُفِرَ لَهُمَا وَلَوْ كَانَتْ ذُنُوبُهُمَا مِثْلَ زَبَدِ الْبِحَارِ

---

## 8:64-66 — verses 64-66 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, urges His Prophet ﷺ and the believers to fight, to press hard against the enemies, and to engage rivals in single combat, and informs them that He is sufficient for them, that is: He suffices them, supports them, and aids them against their enemy, even if the enemy's numbers are great and their reinforcements come one after another, and even if the number of believers is small.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ahmad ibn Uthman ibn Hakim narrated to us, Ubayd Allah ibn Musa narrated to us, Sufyan informed us, from Shawdhab, from al-Sha'bi, concerning His saying: {O Prophet, sufficient for you is Allah and whoever follows you of the believers}, he said: Sufficient for you is Allah, and sufficient is He for whoever bears witness with you.

He said: It has also been related from Ata al-Khurasani and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd [ibn Aslam] the like of this.

Therefore He said: {O Prophet, urge the believers to fight}, that is: incite them and spur them on to it. For this reason the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to urge the fighters on at the time they formed their ranks and faced the enemy, just as he said to his companions on the day of Badr, when the polytheists advanced with their numbers and their equipment: "Rise to a garden as wide as the heavens and the earth." Umayr ibn al-Humam said: A garden as wide as the heavens and the earth? The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Yes." He said: Bakh, bakh (an exclamation of delight)! The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "What moved you to say bakh, bakh?" He said: The hope that I might be among its people. He said: "Indeed you are among its people." So the man advanced, broke the sheath of his sword, took out some dates and began eating from them, then threw the rest from his hand and said: If I were to live until I finished eating these, that would be a long life indeed! Then he advanced and fought until he was killed, may Allah be pleased with him.

It has been related from Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib and Sa'id ibn Jubayr that this verse was revealed when Umar ibn al-Khattab became Muslim, and with him the number of forty was completed.

There is something to consider in this, because this verse is Medinan, and Umar's acceptance of Islam took place in Mecca, after the migration to the land of Abyssinia and before the migration to Medina. And Allah knows best.

Then Allah, exalted is He, said, giving glad tidings to the believers and commanding them: {If there are among you twenty who are steadfast, they will overcome two hundred, and if there are among you a hundred, they will overcome a thousand of those who disbelieve}, each one against ten. Then this command was abrogated, while the glad tidings remained.

Abd Allah ibn al-Mubarak said: Jarir ibn Hazim narrated to us, al-Zubayr ibn al-Khirrit narrated to me, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When {If there are among you twenty who are steadfast, they will overcome two hundred} was revealed, this was hard upon the Muslims, when Allah made it obligatory upon them that not one should flee from ten. Then relief came, and He said: {Now Allah has lightened your burden} up to His saying: {they will overcome two hundred}. He said: Allah lightened the requirement of numbers for them, and reduced the requirement of steadfastness by the same measure that He lightened it for them.

Al-Bukhari related something similar from the hadith of Ibn al-Mubarak.

Sa'id ibn Mansur said: Sufyan narrated to us, from Amr ibn Dinar, from Ibn Abbas, concerning this verse, he said: It was written upon them that twenty should not flee from two hundred. Then Allah lightened this for them, and said: {Now Allah has lightened your burden, and He knows that there is weakness among you}, so it is no longer fitting for a hundred to flee from two hundred.

Al-Bukhari related, from Ali ibn Abd Allah, from Sufyan, the like of this with the same chain.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: Ibn Abi Najih narrated to me, from Ata, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When this verse was revealed it weighed heavily upon the Muslims, and they found it a great matter that twenty should fight two hundred, and a hundred should fight a thousand. So Allah lightened this for them and abrogated it with the other verse, saying: {Now Allah has lightened your burden, and He knows that there is weakness among you} to the end of the verse. So thereafter, if they were faced with half their number of the enemy, it was not fitting for them to flee from their enemy, but if their enemy exceeded that, it was not obligatory upon them to fight them, and it was permissible for them to withdraw from them.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah and al-Awfi related something similar from Ibn Abbas. Ibn Abi Hatim said: It has also been related from Mujahid, Ata, Ikrimah, al-Hasan, Zayd ibn Aslam, Ata al-Khurasani, and al-Dahhak, the like of this.

The hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh related, from the hadith of al-Musayyib ibn Sharik, from Ibn Awn, from Nafi, from Ibn Umar, may Allah be pleased with both of them, concerning {If there are among you twenty who are steadfast, they will overcome two hundred}, he said: It was revealed concerning us, the companions of Muhammad ﷺ.

Al-Hakim related in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of Abu Amr ibn al-Ala, from Nafi, from Ibn Umar, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited: {Now Allah has lightened your burden, and He knows that there is weakness among you}, with the reading rafa (a variant grammatical reading), then he said: It is sound in chain, though the two of them (Bukhari and Muslim) did not include it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُحَرِّضُ تَعَالَى نَبِيَّهُ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَالْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى الْقِتَالِ وَمُنَاجَزَةِ الْأَعْدَاءِ وَمُبَارَزَةِ الْأَقْرَانِ، وَيُخْبِرُهُمْ أَنَّهُ حَسْبُهُمْ، أَيْ: كَافِيهِمْ وَنَاصِرُهُمْ وَمُؤَيِّدُهُمْ عَلَى عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَإِنْ كَثُرَتْ أَعْدَادُهُمْ وَتَرَادَفَتْ أَمْدَادُهُمْ، وَلَوْ قَلَّ عَدَدُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ حَكِيمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُوسَى، أَنْبَأَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ شَوْذَبٍ عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ حَسْبُكَ اللَّهُ وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَكَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ قَالَ: حَسْبُكَ اللَّهُ، وَحَسْبُ مَنْ شَهِدَ مَعَكَ.

قَالَ: وَرُوِيَ عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ [بْنِ أَسْلَمَ] مِثْلَهُ.

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ حَرِّضِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى الْقِتَالِ﴾ أَيْ: حُثَّهُمْ وَذَمِّرْ عَلَيْهِ، وَلِهَذَا كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُحَرِّضُ عَلَى الْقِتَالِ عِنْدَ صَفِّهِمْ وَمُوَاجَهَةِ الْعَدُوِّ، كَمَا قَالَ لِأَصْحَابِهِ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، حِينَ أَقْبَلَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ فِي عَدَدهم وعُدَدهم: "قُومُوا إلى جنة عرضها السموات والأرض". فقال عمير بن الحُمام: عرضها السموات وَالْأَرْضِ؟! فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "نَعَمْ" فَقَالَ: بَخٍ بَخٍ، فَقَالَ: "مَا يَحْمِلُكَ عَلَى قَوْلِكَ بَخٍ بَخٍ؟ " قَالَ رَجَاءَ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا! قَالَ: "فَإِنَّكَ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا" فَتَقَدَّمَ الرَّجُلُ فَكَسَرَ جَفْنَ سَيْفِهِ، وَأَخْرَجَ تَمَرَاتٍ فَجَعَلَ يَأْكُلُ مِنْهُنَّ، ثُمَّ أَلْقَى بَقِيَّتَهُنَّ مِنْ يَدِهِ، وَقَالَ: لَئِنْ أَنَا حَيِيتُ حَتَّى آكُلَهُنَّ إِنَّهَا لَحَيَاةٌ طَوِيلَةٌ! ثُمَّ تَقَدَّمَ فَقَاتَلَ حتى قتل، رضي الله عنه وَقَدْ رُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ: أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ نَزَلَتْ حِينَ أَسْلَمَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ، وَكَمُلَ بِهِ الْأَرْبَعُونَ.

وَفِي هَذَا نَظَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ، وَإِسْلَامُ عُمَرَ كَانَ بِمَكَّةَ بَعْدَ الْهِجْرَةِ إِلَى أَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ وَقَبْلَ الْهِجْرَةِ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُبَشِّرًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَآمِرًا: ﴿إِنْ يَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ عِشْرُونَ صَابِرُونَ يَغْلِبُوا مِائَتَيْنِ وَإِنْ يَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ مِائَةٌ يَغْلِبُوا أَلْفًا مِنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ كُلُّ وَاحِدٍ بِعَشَرَةٍ ثُمَّ نُسِخَ هَذَا الْأَمْرُ وَبَقِيَتِ الْبِشَارَةُ.

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ: حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرُ بْنُ حَازِمٍ، حَدَّثَنِي الزُّبَيْرُ بْنُ الخِرِّيت عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنْ يَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ عِشْرُونَ صَابِرُونَ يَغْلِبُوا مِائَتَيْنِ﴾ شِقَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى الْمُسْلِمِينَ حِينَ فَرَضَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَلَّا يَفِرَّ وَاحِدٌ مِنْ عَشَرَةٍ، ثُمَّ جَاءَ التَّخْفِيفُ، فَقَالَ: ﴿الآنَ خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْكُمْ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَغْلِبُوا مِائَتَيْنِ﴾ قَالَ: خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ مِنَ الْعُدَّةِ، وَنَقَصَ مِنَ الصَّبْرِ بِقَدْرِ مَا خَفَّفَ عَنْهُمْ.

وَرَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ، نَحْوَهُ 

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ قَالَ: كَتَبَ عَلَيْهِمْ أَلَّا يَفِرَّ عِشْرُونَ مِنْ مِائَتَيْنِ، ثُمَّ خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، فَقَالَ: ﴿الآنَ خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْكُمْ وَعَلِمَ أَنَّ فِيكُمْ ضَعْفًا﴾ فَلَا يَنْبَغِي لِمِائَةٍ أَنْ يَفِرُّوا مِنْ مِائَتَيْنِ.

وَرَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللهِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ، بِهِ وَنَحْوَهُ 

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ ثَقُلَتْ عَلَى الْمُسْلِمِينَ، وَأَعْظَمُوا أَنْ يُقَاتِلَ عِشْرُونَ مِائَتَيْنِ، وَمِائَةٌ أَلْفًا، فَخَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ فَنَسَخَهَا بِالْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى فَقَالَ: ﴿الآنَ خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْكُمْ وَعَلِمَ أَنَّ فِيكُمْ ضَعْفًا﴾ الْآيَةَ، فَكَانُوا إِذَا كَانُوا عَلَى الشَّطْرِ مِنْ عَدُوٍّ لَهُمْ لَمْ يَنْبَغِ لَهُمْ أَنْ يَفِرُّوا مِنْ عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَإِذَا كَانُوا دُونَ ذَلِكَ، لَمْ يَجِبْ عَلَيْهِمْ قِتَالُهُمْ، وَجَازَ لَهُمْ أَنْ يَتَحَوَّزُوا عَنْهُمْ.

وَرَوَى عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ وَالْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، نَحْوَ ذَلِكَ. قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: وَرُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَعَطَاءٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَزَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَعَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْمُسَيَّبِ بْنِ شَرِيكٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَوْنٍ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: ﴿إِنْ يَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ عِشْرُونَ صَابِرُونَ يَغْلِبُوا مِائَتَيْنِ﴾ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فِينَا أَصْحَابَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ.

وَرَوَى الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَلَاءِ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَرَأَ: ﴿الآنَ خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ عَنْكُمْ وَعَلِمَ أَنَّ فِيكُمْ ضَعْفًا﴾ رَفْعٌ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ

---

## 8:67-69 — verses 67-69 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Imam Ahmad said: `[chain]` Ali ibn Asim, from Humayd, from Anas, may God be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of God ﷺ consulted the people about the captives on the day of Badr, and said: "God has indeed given you power over them." Then Umar ibn al-Khattab stood up and said: "O Messenger of God, strike their necks." The Prophet ﷺ turned away from him. Then the Messenger of God ﷺ repeated it, saying: "O people, God has indeed given you power over them, and they were but your brothers yesterday." Umar stood up again and said: "O Messenger of God, strike their necks." The Prophet ﷺ turned away from him again. Then the Prophet ﷺ repeated the same words to the people again, and Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, may God be pleased with him, stood up and said: "O Messenger of God, we think you should pardon them and accept ransom from them." He said: the distress that had been on the face of the Messenger of God ﷺ then departed, and he pardoned them and accepted ransom from them. He said: and God, Mighty and Majestic, sent down: {Were it not for a decree from God that preceded} to the end of the verse.

The hadith of Ibn Abbas in similar terms has already preceded at the beginning of the surah, in Sahih Muslim.

Al-A'mash said, from Amr ibn Murrah, from Abu Ubaydah, from Abdullah, who said: On the day of Badr, the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "What do you say about these captives?" Abu Bakr said: "O Messenger of God, they are your people and your kinsfolk. Spare them and give them the chance to repent, perhaps God will turn to them in forgiveness." Umar said: "O Messenger of God, they drove you out and denied you. Bring them forward and strike their necks." Abdullah ibn Rawahah said: "O Messenger of God, you are in a valley abundant with firewood. Set the valley ablaze upon them, then cast them into it." [He said: Then al-Abbas said: "You have severed your ties of kinship."] He said: the Messenger of God ﷺ remained silent and gave them no answer, then he rose and went inside. Some people said: "He will follow the opinion of Abu Bakr." Others said: "He will follow the opinion of Umar." Others said: "He will follow the opinion of Abdullah ibn Rawahah." Then the Messenger of God ﷺ came out to them and said: "God softens the hearts of some men until they become softer than milk, and God hardens the hearts of other men regarding this matter until they become harder than stone. Your likeness, O Abu Bakr, is that of Ibrahim (peace be upon him), who said: {Whoever follows me is of me, and whoever disobeys me, You are indeed Forgiving, Merciful} [Ibrahim: 36]. And your likeness, O Abu Bakr, is that of Isa (peace be upon him), who said: {If You punish them, they are Your servants, and if You forgive them, You are indeed the Mighty, the Wise} [al-Ma'idah: 118]. And your likeness, O Umar, is that of Musa (peace be upon him), who said: {Our Lord, blot out their wealth and harden their hearts so that they will not believe until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 88]. And your likeness, O Umar, is that of Nuh (peace be upon him), who said: {My Lord, leave not upon the earth any dweller among the disbelievers} [Nuh: 26]. You are in need, so let none of them escape except by ransom or by having his neck struck." Ibn Mas'ud said: I said: "O Messenger of God, except Suhayl ibn Baydah, for he speaks favorably of Islam." The Messenger of God ﷺ remained silent, and I never felt myself in greater fear that stones might fall upon me from the sky than I did on that day, until the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Except Suhayl ibn Baydah." Then God, Exalted, sent down: {It is not for a prophet to have captives} to the end of the verse.

This was narrated by Imam Ahmad and al-Tirmidhi from the hadith of Abu Mu'awiyah, from al-A'mash, and by al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, who said: sound in chain, though the two Shaykhs (Bukhari and Muslim) did not include it. Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh narrated something similar from Abdullah ibn Umar and Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with them both, from the Prophet ﷺ. There is also a report on this subject from Abu Ayyub al-Ansari.

Ibn Mardawayh also narrated, and the wording is his, as did al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of Ubaydullah ibn Musa: `[chain]` Isra'il, from Ibrahim ibn Muhajir, from Mujahid, from Ibn Umar, who said: When the captives were taken on the day of Badr, al-Abbas was among those captured; he was captured by a man from the Ansar. He said: the Ansar had threatened to kill him. This reached the Prophet ﷺ, and the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I did not sleep last night because of my uncle al-Abbas, for the Ansar claim they intend to kill him." Umar said to him: "Shall I go to them?" He said: "Yes." So Umar went to the Ansar and said to them: "Release al-Abbas." They said: "No, by God, we will not release him." Umar said to them: "What if the Messenger of God ﷺ would be pleased by it?" They said: "If the Messenger of God ﷺ would be pleased by it, then take him." So Umar took him, and when he had him in his custody he said to him: "O Abbas, embrace Islam, for by God, that you should embrace Islam is dearer to me than that al-Khattab should embrace Islam, and that is only because I saw how pleased the Messenger of God ﷺ was at the thought of your accepting Islam." He said: The Messenger of God ﷺ consulted Abu Bakr, and Abu Bakr said: "They are your kinsfolk, so release them." He consulted Umar, who said: "Kill them." But the Messenger of God ﷺ accepted ransom from them, and God sent down: {It is not for a prophet to have captives until he has thoroughly subdued the land} to the end of the verse.

Al-Hakim said: sound in chain, though the two Shaykhs did not include it.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Hisham, that is, Ibn Hassan, from Muhammad ibn Sirin, from Ubaydah, from Ali, may God be pleased with him, who said: Jibril came to the Prophet ﷺ on the day of Badr and said: "Give your companions the choice concerning the captives: if they wish, ransom, and if they wish, execution, on condition that an equal number of them be killed from among yourselves as they advance." They said: "Ransom, even if some of us are killed."

This was narrated by al-Tirmidhi, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Hibban in his Sahih, from the hadith of al-Thawri, through the same chain, and this is a very gharib (singular) hadith.

Ibn Awn said, [from Muhammad ibn Sirin], from Ubaydah, from Ali, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said concerning the captives of the day of Badr: "If you wish, kill them, and if you wish, ransom them and benefit from the ransom, and an equal number of you will be martyred in return." He said: the last of the seventy was Thabit ibn Qays, who was killed on the day of al-Yamamah, may God be pleased with him.

Some narrated this hadith from Ubaydah as mursal (with a broken chain to the Companion), and God knows best.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Ibn Abi Najih, from Ata, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {It is not for a prophet to have captives}, he read on until he reached {a great punishment}, and said: this refers to the spoils of Badr, before God had made them lawful for them. He is saying: were it not that I do not punish anyone who disobeys Me until I have first given him warning, a great punishment would have touched you for what you took.

Ibn Abi Najih narrated the same from Mujahid.

Al-A'mash said: it had already been decreed by God that He would not punish anyone who was present at Badr. Something similar was narrated from Sa'd ibn Abi Waqqas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and Ata.

Shu'bah said, from Abu Hashim, from Mujahid, regarding {Were it not for a decree from God that preceded}: meaning, for them, of forgiveness. Something similar was narrated from Sufyan al-Thawri, may God have mercy on him.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying {Were it not for a decree from God that preceded}: meaning, in the Mother of the Book from the beginning, that spoils and captives are lawful for you; {a great punishment would have touched you for what you took} of the captives. God, Exalted, said: {So eat of what you have taken as spoils} to the end of the verse. Al-Awfi likewise narrated from Ibn Abbas. Something similar was narrated from Abu Hurayrah, Ibn Mas'ud, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ata, al-Hasan al-Basri, Qatadah, and al-A'mash as well: that what is meant by {Were it not for a decree from God that preceded} is a decree for this ummah (community) permitting the spoils of war, and this is the choice of Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him.

This view is supported by what the two Sahihs (Bukhari and Muslim) recorded from Jabir ibn Abdullah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I have been given five things which no prophet before me was given: I have been aided by terror for the distance of a month's journey, the earth has been made for me a place of prostration and a means of purification, the spoils of war have been made lawful for me, and they were not lawful for anyone before me, I have been given intercession, and every prophet used to be sent to his own people specifically, while I have been sent to all of mankind."

Al-A'mash said, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The spoils of war were not made lawful for any dark-headed people other than us."

For this reason God, Exalted, said: {So eat of what you have taken as spoils, lawful and good, and fear God; indeed God is Forgiving, Merciful}. It was at that point that they took ransom from the captives.

Imam Abu Dawud narrated in his Sunan: `[chain]` Abd al-Rahman ibn al-Mubarak al-Ayshi, `[chain]` Sufyan ibn Habib, `[chain]` Shu'bah, from Abu al-Anbas, from Abu al-Sha'tha, from Ibn Abbas: that the Messenger of God ﷺ set the ransom for the people of the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic ignorance) on the day of Badr at four hundred.

The ruling concerning captives has been settled, according to the majority of scholars, as follows: the imam (leader) has the choice regarding them. If he wishes, he may execute them, as was done with Banu Qurayzah. If he wishes, he may ransom them for wealth, as was done with the captives of Badr, or exchange them for Muslims who have been captured, as the Messenger of God ﷺ did with that slave girl and her daughter who were among the captives taken by Salamah ibn al-Akwa', where he returned the two of them and took in exchange for them Muslims who were in the hands of the polytheists. Or if he wishes, he may enslave whomever he has captured. This is the school of Imam al-Shafi'i and a group of scholars. There is further disagreement among the imams on this matter, which is established in its proper place in the books of fiqh (jurisprudence).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: اسْتَشَارَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ النَّاسَ فِي الْأُسَارَى يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَمْكَنَكُمْ مِنْهُمْ" فَقَامَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، اضْرِبْ أَعْنَاقَهُمْ. فَأَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، ثُمَّ عَادَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَمْكَنَكُمْ مِنْهُمْ، وَإِنَّمَا هُمْ إِخْوَانُكُمْ بِالْأَمْسِ". فَقَامَ عُمَرُ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، اضْرِبْ أَعْنَاقَهُمْ. فَأَعْرَضَ عَنْهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، ثُمَّ عَادَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَقَالَ لِلنَّاسِ مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، فَقَامَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، نَرَى أَنْ تَعْفُوَ عَنْهُمْ، وَأَنْ تَقْبَلَ مِنْهُمُ الْفِدَاءَ. قَالَ: فَذَهَبَ عَنْ وَجْهِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَا كَانَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْغَمِّ، فَعَفَا عَنْهُمْ، وَقَبِلَ مِنْهُمُ الْفِدَاءَ. قَالَ: وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿لَوْلا كِتَابٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ سَبَقَ﴾ الْآيَةَ 

وَقَدْ سَبَقَ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ حَدِيثُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ بِنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّةَ، عَنْ أَبِي عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمُ بَدْرٍ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا تَقُولُونَ فِي هَؤُلَاءِ الْأُسَارَى؟ " قَالَ: فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَوْمُكَ وَأَهْلُكَ، اسْتَبْقِهِمْ وَاسْتَتِبْهُمْ، لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَتُوبَ عَلَيْهِمْ. قَالَ: وَقَالَ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَخْرَجُوكَ، وَكَذَّبُوكَ، فَقَدِّمْهُمْ فَاضْرِبْ أَعْنَاقَهُمْ. قَالَ: وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ رَوَاحَةَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَنْتَ فِي وَادٍ كَثِيرِ الْحَطَبِ، فَأَضْرِمِ الْوَادِي عَلَيْهِمْ نَارًا، ثُمَّ أَلْقِهِمْ فِيهِ. [قَالَ: فَقَالَ الْعَبَّاسُ: قَطَعْتَ رَحِمَكَ] قَالَ: فَسَكَتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَلَمْ يَرُدَّ عَلَيْهِمْ شَيْئًا، ثُمَّ قَامَ فَدَخَلَ فَقَالَ نَاسٌ: يَأْخُذُ بِقَوْلِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ. وَقَالَ نَاسٌ: يَأْخُذُ بِقَوْلِ عُمَرَ. وَقَالَ نَاسٌ: يَأْخُذُ بِقَوْلِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَوَاحَةَ. ثُمَّ خَرَجَ عَلَيْهِمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَيُلِينُ قُلُوبَ رِجَالٍ حَتَّى تَكُونَ أَلْيَنَ مِنَ اللَّبَنِ، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَيُشَدِّدُ قُلُوبَ رِجَالٍ فِيهِ حَتَّى تَكُونَ أَشَدَّ مِنَ الْحِجَارَةِ، وَإِنَّ مَثَلَكَ يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ كَمَثَلِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: ﴿فَمَنْ تَبِعَنِي فَإِنَّهُ مِنِّي وَمَنْ عَصَانِي فَإِنَّكَ غَفُورٌرَحِيمٌ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ٣٦] ،وَإِنَّ مَثَلَكَ يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ كَمَثَلِ عِيسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ تُعَذِّبْهُمْ فَإِنَّهُمْ عِبَادُكَ وَإِنْ تَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ فَإِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ١١٨] ، وَإِنَّ مَثَلَكَ يَا عُمَرُ مَثَلُ موسى عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا اطْمِسْ عَلَى أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَاشْدُدْ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ فَلا يُؤْمِنُوا حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٨٨] ،وَإِنَّ مَثَلَكَ يَا عُمَرُ كَمَثَلِ نُوحٍ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: ﴿رَبِّ لَا تَذَرْ عَلَى الأرْضِ مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ دَيَّارًا﴾ [نُوحٍ: ٢٦] ،أَنْتُمْ عَالَةٌ فَلَا يَنْفَلِتَنَّ أَحَدٌ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا بِفِدَاءٍ أَوْ ضَرْبَةِ عُنُقٍ". قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِلَّا سُهَيْلُ بْنُ بَيْضَاءَ، فَإِنَّهُ يَذْكُرُ الْإِسْلَامَ، فَسَكَتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَمَا رَأَيْتُنِي فِي يَوْمٍ أَخْوَفَ أَنْ تَقَعَ عَلَيَّ حِجَارَةٌ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مِنِّي فِي ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمِ، حَتَّى قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إلا سُهَيْلُ بْنُ بَيْضَاءَ" فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِنَبِيٍّ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ أَسْرَى﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ.

رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، وَقَالَ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، وَأَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ نَحْوَهُ وَفِي الْبَابِ عَنْ أَبِي أَيُّوبَ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ أَيْضًا -وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ -وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُوسَى: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: لَمَّا أُسِرَ الْأُسَارَى يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، أُسِرَ الْعَبَّاسُ فِيمَنْ أُسِرَ، أَسَرَهُ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، قَالَ: وَقَدْ أَوْعَدَتْهُ الْأَنْصَارُ أَنْ يَقْتُلُوهُ. فَبَلَغَ ذَلِكَ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي لَمْ أَنَمِ اللَّيْلَةَ مِنْ أَجْلِ عَمِّي الْعَبَّاسِ، وَقَدْ زَعَمَتِ الْأَنْصَارُ أَنَّهُمْ قَاتِلُوهُ" فَقَالَ لَهُ عُمَرُ: فَآتِهِمْ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ" فَأَتَى عُمَرُ الْأَنْصَارَ فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: أَرْسِلُوا الْعَبَّاسَ فَقَالُوا: لَا وَاللَّهِ لَا نُرْسِلُهُ. فَقَالَ لَهُمْ عُمَرُ: فَإِنْ كَانَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ رِضًى؟ قَالُوا: فَإِنْ كَانَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ رِضًى فَخُذْهُ. فَأَخَذَهُ عُمَرُ فَلَمَّا صَارَ فِي يَدِهِ قَالَ لَهُ: يَا عَبَّاسُ، أَسْلِمْ، فَوَاللَّهِ لَأَنْ تُسْلِمَ أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْ أَنْ يُسْلِمَ الْخَطَّابُ، وَمَا ذَاكَ إِلَّا لَمَّا رَأَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُعْجِبُهُ إِسْلَامُكَ، قَالَ: فَاسْتَشَارَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَبَا بَكْرٍ، فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: عَشِيرَتُكَ. فَأَرْسِلْهُمْ، فَاسْتَشَارَ عُمَرَ، فَقَالَ: اقْتُلْهُمْ، فَفَادَاهُمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِنَبِيٍّ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ أَسْرَى حَتَّى يُثْخِنَ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

قَالَ الْحَاكِمُ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ 

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ -هُوَ ابْنُ حَسَّانَ -عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ، عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: جَاءَ جِبْرِيلُ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ فَقَالَ: خَيِّر أَصْحَابَكَ فِي الْأُسَارَى: إِنْ شَاءُوا الْفِدَاءَ، وإن شاؤوا الْقَتْلَ عَلَى أَنْ يُقْتَلَ مِنْهُمْ مُقْبِلًا مِثْلَهُمْ. قَالُوا: الْفِدَاءُ وَيُقْتَلُ مِنَّا.

رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ حِبَّانَ فِي صَحِيحِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، به وهذا حديث غريب جِدًّا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَوْنٍ [عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ] عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم في أُسَارَى يَوْمِ بَدْرٍ: "إِنْ شِئْتُمْ قَتَلْتُمُوهُمْ، وَإِنْ شِئْتُمْ فَادَيْتُمُوهُمْ وَاسْتَمْتَعْتُمْ بِالْفِدَاءِ، وَاسْتَشْهَدَ مِنْكُمْ بِعِدَّتِهِمْ". قَالَ: فَكَانَ آخِرُ السَّبْعِينَ ثَابِتَ بْنَ قَيْسٍ، قُتِلَ يَوْمَ الْيَمَامَةِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ 

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ رَوَى هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ مُرْسَلًا فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابن عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِنَبِيٍّ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ أَسْرَى﴾ فَقَرَأَ حَتَّى بَلَغَ: ﴿عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ قَالَ: غَنَائِمُ بَدْرٍ، قَبْلَ أَنْ يُحِلَّهَا لَهُمْ، يَقُولُ: لَوْلَا أَنِّي لَا أُعَذِّبُ مَنْ عَصَانِي حَتَّى أَتَقَدَّمَ إِلَيْهِ، لَمَسَّكُمْ فِيمَا أَخَذْتُمْ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ: سَبَقَ مِنْهُ أَلَّا يُعَذِّبَ أَحَدًا شَهِدَ بَدْرًا. وَرُوِيَ نَحْوُهُ عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ أَبِي وَقَّاصٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَعَطَاءٍ.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي هَاشِمٍ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿لَوْلا كِتَابٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ سَبَقَ﴾ أَيْ: لَهُمْ بِالْمَغْفِرَةِ وَنَحْوُهُ عَنْ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَوْلا كِتَابٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ سَبَقَ﴾ يَعْنِي: فِي أُمِّ الْكِتَابِ الْأَوَّلِ أَنَّ الْمَغَانِمَ وَالْأُسَارَى حَلَالٌ لَكُمْ، ﴿لَمَسَّكُمْ فِيمَا أَخَذْتُمْ﴾ مِنَ الْأُسَارَى ﴿عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِمَّا غَنِمْتُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ. وَكَذَا رَوَى الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَرُوِيَ مِثْلُهُ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، وَابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَعَطَاءٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ وَالْأَعْمَشِ أَيْضًا: أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ ﴿لَوْلا كِتَابٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ سَبَقَ﴾ لِهَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ بِإِحْلَالِ الْغَنَائِمِ وَهُوَ اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَيُسْتَشْهَدُ لِهَذَا الْقَوْلِ بِمَا أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا، لَمْ يُعْطَهُنَّ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ قَبْلِي: نُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ، وَجُعِلَتْ لِي الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وَطَهُورًا، وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلِي، وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ، وَكَانَ النَّبِيُّ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ وَبُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً" 

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لم تحل الغنائم لسود الرؤوس غَيْرِنَا" 

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِمَّا غَنِمْتُمْ حَلالا طَيِّبًا وَاتَّقُوااللَّهَ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ أَخَذُوا مِنَ الْأُسَارَى الْفِدَاءَ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي سُنَنِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ الْعَيْشِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ حَبِيبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَنْبَسِ، عَنْ أَبِي الشَّعْثَاءِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَعَلَ فِدَاءَ أَهْلِ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ أَرْبَعَمِائَةٍ 

وَقَدِ اسْتَقَرَّ الْحُكْمُ فِي الْأَسْرَى عِنْدَ جُمْهُورِ الْعُلَمَاءِ: أَنَّ الْإِمَامَ مُخَيَّرٌ فِيهِمْ: إِنْ شَاءَ قَتَلَ -كَمَا فَعَلَ بِبَنِي قُرَيْظَةَ -وَإِنْ شَاءَ فَادَى بِمَالٍ -كَمَا فَعَلَ بِأَسْرَى بَدْرٍ -أَوْ بِمَنْ أُسِرَ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ -كَمَا فِعْلِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي تِلْكَ الْجَارِيَةِ وَابْنَتِهَا اللَّتَيْنِ كَانَتَا فِي سَبْيِ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ الْأَكْوَعِ، حَيْثُ رَدَّهُمَا وَأَخَذَ فِي مُقَابَلَتِهِمَا مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا عِنْدَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَإِنْ شَاءَ اسْتَرَقَّ مَنْ أَسَرَ. هَذَا مَذْهَبُ الْإِمَامِ الشَّافِعِيِّ وَطَائِفَةٍ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ، وَفِي الْمَسْأَلَةِ خِلَافٌ آخَرُ بَيْنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ مُقَرَّرٌ في موضعه من كتب الفقه.

---

## 8:70-71 — verses 70-71 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: al-Abbas ibn Abdullah ibn Mughaffal narrated to me, from some of his family, from Abdullah ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with them both, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said on the day of Badr: "I know that some men from Banu Hashim and others were brought out unwillingly, having no wish to fight us. So whoever among you meets any of them, that is, from Banu Hashim, let him not kill him. And whoever meets Abu al-Bakhtari ibn Hisham, let him not kill him. And whoever meets al-Abbas ibn Abdul Muttalib, let him not kill him, for he was brought out only under compulsion." Abu Hudhayfah ibn Utbah said: "Shall we kill our fathers, our sons, our brothers, and our clansmen, and spare al-Abbas? By God, if I meet him I will strike his face with the sword!" This reached the Messenger of God ﷺ, and he said to Umar ibn al-Khattab: "O Abu Hafs," Umar said: "By God, that was the first day the Messenger of God ﷺ ever addressed me by that name," "shall the face of the uncle of the Messenger of God ﷺ be struck with the sword?" Umar said: "O Messenger of God, give me leave and I will strike his neck, for by God he has spoken as a hypocrite." After that, Abu Hudhayfah used to say: "By God, I have never felt safe from that word I spoke, and I remain fearful of it, unless God should atone for it from me through martyrdom." He was killed a martyr on the day of al-Yamamah, may God be pleased with him.

And by the same chain, from Ibn Abbas, he said: When evening came on the day of Badr, and the captives were held bound, the Messenger of God ﷺ spent the first part of the night wakeful. His companions said to him: "O Messenger of God, why do you not sleep?" For al-Abbas had been captured by a man from the Ansar. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I heard the groaning of my uncle al-Abbas in his bonds." So they released him, and he fell silent, and the Messenger of God ﷺ slept.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: The captive of Badr whose ransom was largest was al-Abbas ibn Abdul Muttalib, for he was a wealthy man, and he ransomed himself for one hundred uqiyyah (ounces) of gold.

In Sahih al-Bukhari, from the hadith of Musa ibn Uqbah, Ibn Shihab said: Anas ibn Malik narrated to me that men from the Ansar sought permission from the Messenger of God ﷺ, saying: "Allow us to forgo the ransom owed by our sister's son, al-Abbas." He said: "No, by God, you shall not leave out even a single dirham of it."

Yunus ibn Bukayr said, from Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from Yazid ibn Ruman, from Urwah, and from al-Zuhri, from a group he named, they said: Quraysh sent to the Messenger of God ﷺ regarding the ransom of their captives, and every group ransomed their captive for whatever they agreed upon. Al-Abbas said: "O Messenger of God, I was already a Muslim!" The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "God knows best about your Islam. If it is as you say, then God will reward you for it. But as for your outward state, it was against us, so ransom yourself and your two nephews: Nawfal ibn al-Harith ibn Abdul Muttalib and Aqil ibn Abi Talib ibn Abdul Muttalib, and your ally Utbah ibn Amr, brother of Banu al-Harith ibn Fihr." He said: "I have nothing for that, O Messenger of God!" He said: "Then where is the wealth that you and Umm al-Fadl buried? You said to her: 'If I am struck down on this journey of mine, this wealth I have buried is for my sons al-Fadl, Abdullah, and Qutham.'" He said: "By God, O Messenger of God, I truly know that you are the Messenger of God. This is something no one knew of except me and Umm al-Fadl. So reckon for me, O Messenger of God, what you have taken from me: twenty uqiyyah of wealth that was with me." The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "No, that is something God Most High has given us from you." So he ransomed himself and his two nephews and his ally. And God, Mighty and Majestic, revealed concerning him: {O Prophet, say to those captives who are in your hands: if God knows in your hearts any good, He will give you better than what was taken from you, and He will forgive you. And God is Forgiving, Merciful.} Al-Abbas said: "So God gave me, in place of the twenty uqiyyah, twenty slaves in Islam, each of them having wealth in hand with which he trades, along with what I hope for of the forgiveness of God, Mighty and Majestic."

Ibn Ishaq also related, from Ibn Abi Najih, from Ata, from Ibn Abbas, something similar to the above concerning this verse.

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: Ibn Wakee narrated to us, Ibn Idris narrated to us, [from Ibn Ishaq], from Ibn Abi Najih, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Al-Abbas said: "Concerning me was revealed: {It is not fitting for a prophet that he should have captives until he has thoroughly subdued the land.} So I informed the Prophet ﷺ of my Islam, and I asked him to credit me for the twenty uqiyyah he had taken from me, but he refused. So God gave me in its place twenty slaves, all of them merchants, my wealth in their hands."

Ibn Ishaq also said: al-Kalbi narrated to me, from Abu Salih, from Ibn Abbas, from Jabir ibn Abdullah ibn Ri'ab, who said: al-Abbas ibn Abdul Muttalib used to say: "Concerning me, by God, was this revealed, when I mentioned my Islam to the Messenger of God ﷺ." Then he related something similar to the previous hadith.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Ata al-Khurasani, from Ibn Abbas: {O Prophet, say to those captives who are in your hands}, meaning al-Abbas and his companions. He said: They said to the Prophet ﷺ: "We believe in what you have brought, and we bear witness that you are the Messenger of God. We will surely be sincere counselors for you against our own people." So God revealed: {if God knows in your hearts any good, He will give you better than what was taken from you}, meaning faith and belief in the truth, He will replace for you better than what was taken from you, {and He will forgive you} the association of partners with God that you were formerly upon. He said: al-Abbas used to say: "I would not wish that this verse had not been revealed concerning us, even if I had all the world in exchange. He said: {He will give you better than what was taken from you}, and indeed He gave me better than what was taken from me, a hundred times over. And He said: {and He will forgive you}, and I hope that I have been forgiven."

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning this verse: Al-Abbas was captured on the day of Badr, and he ransomed himself for forty uqiyyah of gold. When this verse was read, al-Abbas said: "God, Mighty and Majestic, has granted us two qualities that I would not exchange for all the world: I was captured on the day of Badr and ransomed myself for forty uqiyyah, and He gave me forty slaves in return, and I hope for the forgiveness that God, exalted be His praise, has promised us."

Qatadah said, in explaining this verse: It was mentioned to us that when the wealth of Bahrain arrived to the Messenger of God ﷺ, eighty thousand in amount, he had already performed ablution for the noon prayer. He did not that day give to anyone silently nor deprive any petitioner, and he did not pray that day until he had distributed it all. He commanded al-Abbas to take from it and scoop up as much as he could, and he did so. Qatadah said: al-Abbas used to say: "This is better than what was taken from us, and I hope for forgiveness."

Ya'qub ibn Sufyan said: Amr ibn Asim narrated to us, Sulayman ibn al-Mughirah narrated to us, from Humayd ibn Hilal, who said: Ibn al-Hadrami sent to the Messenger of God ﷺ from Bahrain eighty thousand, no wealth greater than it ever came to him, neither before nor after. He said: It was scattered upon a mat, and the call to prayer was made. He said: The Messenger of God ﷺ came and stood over the wealth, and the people of the mosque came, and that day there was no counting or weighing, it was only handfuls taken. He said: And al-Abbas ibn Abdul Muttalib came, scooping into a cloak he was wearing, and he went to stand up but could not. He said: He raised his head to the Messenger of God ﷺ and said: "O Messenger of God, lift it up for me." He said: The Messenger of God ﷺ smiled until his eye tooth showed, or it was said, his laughter, and said to him: "Return part of the wealth, and take up as much as you are able to carry." He said: So he did that, and al-Abbas began saying, as he went off: "As for one of the two things God promised us, we have obtained it, and we do not know what He will do concerning the other:" {O Prophet, say to those captives who are in your hands} the verse. Then he said: "This is better than what was taken from us, and I do not know what God will do concerning the other." The Messenger of God ﷺ continued to be occupied with that wealth until not a dirham remained of it, and he did not send even a single dirham to his own household, then he went to the prayer and prayed.

Another hadith on this matter: al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi said: Abu Abdullah al-Hafiz informed us, Abu al-Tayyib Muhammad ibn Muhammad ibn Abdullah al-Sa'idi informed me, Mahmash ibn Isam narrated to us, Hafs ibn Abdullah narrated to us, Ibrahim ibn Tahman narrated to us, from Abdul Aziz ibn Suhayb, from Anas ibn Malik, who said: Wealth from Bahrain was brought to the Messenger of God ﷺ, and he said: "Scatter it in the mosque."

He said: It was the largest amount of wealth ever brought to the Messenger of God ﷺ. He went out to the prayer and did not turn his attention to it. When he had finished the prayer, he came and sat beside it. He did not see anyone without giving him from it, until al-Abbas came and said: "O Messenger of God, give me, for I ransomed myself, and I ransomed Aqil." The Messenger of God ﷺ said to him: "Take." So he scooped it into his garment, then went to lift it but could not. He said: "Order one of them to lift it up onto me." He said: "No." He said: "Then lift it up onto me yourself." He said: "No." So he scattered some of it, then carried it upon his shoulder, then went off. The Messenger of God ﷺ kept following him with his gaze until he was out of sight, marveling at his eagerness. The Messenger of God ﷺ did not get up while there was even a dirham of it remaining.

Al-Bukhari related it in several places in his Sahih as a suspended report stated with certainty, saying: "Ibrahim ibn Tahman said," and relating it, and in some versions it is more complete than this.

His saying: {And if they intend to betray you}, meaning in what they outwardly showed you in words, {they have already betrayed God before}, meaning before Badr, through disbelief in Him, {so He gave power over them}, meaning through their capture on the day of Badr, {and God is Knowing, Wise}, meaning Knowing of what He does, Wise in it.

Qatadah said: It was revealed concerning Abdullah ibn Sa'd ibn Abi Sarh, the scribe, when he apostatized and joined the polytheists.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Ata al-Khurasani, from Ibn Abbas: It was revealed concerning al-Abbas and his companions, when they said: "We will surely be sincere counselors for you against our own people."

Al-Suddi explained it in a general sense, and this is more comprehensive and more apparent, and God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي الْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُغَفَّلٍ، عَنْ بَعْضِ أَهْلِهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ: "إِنِّي قَدْ عَرَفْتُ أَنَّ أُنَاسًا مِنْ بَنِي هَاشِمٍ وَغَيْرِهِمْ، قَدْ أُخْرِجُوا كُرْهًا، لَا حَاجَةَ لَهُمْ بِقِتَالِنَا، فَمَنْ لَقِيَ مِنْكُمْ أَحَدًا مِنْهُمْ -أَيْ: مِنْ بَنِي هَاشِمٍ -فَلَا يَقْتُلُهُ، وَمَنْ لَقِيَ أَبَا الْبَخْتَرِيِّ بْنَ هِشَامٍ فَلَا يَقْتُلُهُ، وَمَنْ لَقِيَ الْعَبَّاسَ بْنَ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ فَلَا يَقْتُلُهُ، فَإِنَّهُ إِنَّمَا أُخْرِجَ مُسْتَكْرَهًا". فَقَالَ أَبُو حُذَيْفَةَ بْنُ عُتْبَةَ: أَنَقْتُلُ آبَاءَنَا وَأَبْنَاءَنَا وَإِخْوَانَنَا وَعَشَائِرَنَا وَنَتْرُكُ الْعَبَّاسَ؟ ! وَاللَّهِ لَئِنْ لَقِيتُهُ لَأَلْجِمَنَّهُ بِالسَّيْفِ؟ فَبَلَغَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ لِعُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ: "يَا أَبَا حَفْصٍ" -قَالَ عُمَرُ: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لَأَوَّلُ يَوْمٍ كَنَّانِي فِيهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ -"أَيُضْرَبُ وَجْهُ عَمِّ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالسَّيْفِ؟ " فَقَالَ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ائْذَنْ لِي فَأَضْرِبَ عُنُقَهُ، فَوَاللَّهِ لَقَدْ نَافَقَ. فَكَانَ أَبُو حُذَيْفَةَ يَقُولُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا آمَنُ مِنْ تِلْكَ الْكَلِمَةِ الَّتِي قُلْتُ، وَلَا أَزَالُ مِنْهَا خَائِفًا، إِلَّا أَنْ يُكَفِّرَهَا اللَّهُ عَنِّي بِشَهَادَةٍ. فَقُتِلَ يَوْمَ اليمامة شهيدا، رضي الله عنه.

وَبِهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا أَمْسَى رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم يوم بَدْرٍ، وَالْأُسَارَى مَحْبُوسُونَ بِالْوِثَاقِ، بَاتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ سَاهِرًا أَوَّلَ اللَّيْلِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ أَصْحَابُهُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا لَكَ لَا تَنَامُ؟ -وَقَدْ أَسَرَ الْعَبَّاسَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ -فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "سَمِعْتُ أَنِينَ عَمِّيَ الْعَبَّاسِ فِي وِثَاقِهِ" فَأَطْلَقُوهُ، فَسَكَتَ، فَنَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَكَانَ أَكْثَرُ الْأُسَارَى يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ فِدَاءً الْعَبَّاسَ بْنَ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ رَجُلًا مُوسرا فَافْتَدَى نَفْسَهُ بِمِائَةِ أُوقِيَّةٍ ذَهَبًا 

وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُوسَى بْنِ عُقْبَةَ، قَالَ ابْنُ شِهَابٍ: حَدَّثَنِي أَنَسُ بْنُ مَالِكٍ أَنَّ رِجَالًا مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ اسْتَأْذَنُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالُوا: ائذَنْ لَنَا فَلْنَتْرُكْ لِابْنِ أُخْتِنَا عَبَّاسٍ فِدَاءَهُ. قَالَ لَا وَاللَّهِ لَا تَذَرون مِنْهُ دِرْهَمًا" 

وَقَالَ يُونُسُ بْنُ بُكَيْر، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ رُومان، عَنْ عُرْوَة -وَعَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ جَمَاعَةٍ سَمَّاهُمْ قَالُوا: بَعَثَتْ قُرَيْشٌ إِلَى رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم في فِدَاءِ أَسْرَاهُمْ، فَفَدَى كُلُّ قَوْمٍ أَسِيرَهُمْ بِمَا رَضُوا، وَقَالَ الْعَبَّاسُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَدْ كُنْتُ مُسْلِمًا! فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِإِسْلَامِكَ، فَإِنْ يَكُنْ كَمَا تَقُولُ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَجْزِيكَ، وَأَمَّا ظَاهِرُكَ فَقَدْ كَانَ عَلَيْنَا، فَافْتَدِ نَفْسَكَ وابنيْ أَخِيكَ: نَوْفَلَ بْنَ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، وعَقيل بْنَ أَبِي طَالِبِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، وَحَلِيفَكَ عُتْبَةَ بْنَ عَمْرٍو أَخِي بَنِي الْحَارِثِ بْنِ فِهْرٍ" قَالَ: مَا ذَاكَ عِنْدِي يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ! قَالَ: "فَأَيْنَ الْمَالُ الَّذِي دَفَنْتَهُ أَنْتَ وَأُمُّ الْفَضْلِ؟ فَقُلْتَ لَهَا: إِنْ أصبتُ فِي سَفَرِي هَذَا، فَهَذَا الْمَالُ الَّذِي دَفَنْتُهُ لبَني: الْفَضْلِ، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ، وقُثم". قَالَ: وَاللَّهِ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي لِأَعْلَمُ أَنَّكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ مَا عَلِمَهُ أَحَدٌ غَيْرِي وغيرُ أُمِّ الْفَضْلِ، فَاحْسِبْ لِي يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ مَا أَصَبْتُمْ مِنِّي: عِشْرِينَ أُوقِيَّةً مِنْ مَالٍ كَانَ مَعِي فَقَالَ؟ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا ذَاكَ شَيْءٌ أَعْطَانَا اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مِنْكَ". فَفَدَى نَفْسَهُ وَابْنَيْ أَخَوَيْهِ وَحَلِيفَهُ، وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فِيهِ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لِمَنْ فِي أَيْدِيكُمْ مِنَ الأسْرَى إِنْ يَعْلَمِ اللَّهُ فِي قُلُوبِكُمْ خَيْرًا يُؤْتِكُمْ خَيْرًا مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنْكُمْ وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ قَالَ الْعَبَّاسُ: فَأَعْطَانِي اللَّهُ مَكَانَ الْعِشْرِينَ الْأُوقِيَّةَ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ عِشْرِينَ عَبْدًا، كُلُّهُمْ فِي يَدِهِ مَالٌ يَضْرِبُ بِهِ، مَعَ مَا أَرْجُو مِنْ مَغْفِرَةِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ أَيْضًا، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الآية بنحو مما تقدم.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ إِدْرِيسَ [عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ] عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ الْعَبَّاسُ: فِيَّ نَزَلَتْ: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِنَبِيٍّ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ أَسْرَى حَتَّى يُثْخِنَ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ فَأَخْبَرْتُ النبيَّ ﷺ بِإِسْلَامِي، وَسَأَلْتُهُ أَنْ يُحَاسِبَنِي بِالْعِشْرِينِ الْأُوقِيَّةِ الَّتِي أَخَذَ مِنِّي، فَأَبَى، فَأَبْدَلَنِي اللَّهُ بِهَا عِشْرِينَ عَبْدًا، كُلُّهُمْ تَاجِرٌ، مَالِي فِي يَدِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنِي الْكَلْبِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عن جابر بن عبد الله ابن رِئَابٍ قَالَ: كَانَ الْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ يَقُولُ: فيَّ نَزَلَتْ -وَاللَّهِ -حِينَ ذَكَرْتُ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِسْلَامِي -ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ نَحْوَ الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي قَبْلَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُريج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لِمَنْ فِي أَيْدِيكُمْ مِنَ الأسْرَى﴾ عَبَّاسٌ وَأَصْحَابُهُ. قَالَ: قَالُوا لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ: آمَنَّا بِمَا جِئْتَ بِهِ، وَنَشْهَدُ أَنَّكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، لَنَنْصَحَنَّ لَكَ عَلَى قَوْمِنَا. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿إِنْ يَعْلَمِ اللَّهُ فِي قُلُوبِكُمْ خَيْرًا يُؤْتِكُمْ خَيْرًا مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنْكُمْ﴾ إِيمَانًا وَتَصْدِيقًا، يُخْلِفْ لَكُمْ خَيْرًا مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنْكُمْ ﴿وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ﴾ الشَّرْكَ الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ. قَالَ: فَكَانَ الْعَبَّاسُ يَقُولُ: مَا أُحِبُّ أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ لَمْ تَنْزِلْ فِينَا، وَأَنَّ لِيَ الدُّنْيَا، لَقَدْ قَالَ: ﴿يُؤْتِكُمْ خَيْرًا مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنْكُمْ﴾ فَقَدْ أَعْطَانِي خَيْرًا مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنِّي مِائَةَ ضِعْفٍ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ﴾ وَأَرْجُو أَنْ يَكُونَ غُفر لِي.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: كَانَ الْعَبَّاسُ أُسِرَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فَافْتَدَى نَفْسَهُ بِأَرْبَعِينَ أُوقِيَّةً مِنْ ذَهَبٍ، فَقَالَ الْعَبَّاسُ حِينَ قُرِئَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: لَقَدْ أَعْطَانَا اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، خَصلتين، مَا أُحِبُّ أَنَّ لِي بِهِمَا الدُّنْيَا: إِنِّي أُسِرْتُ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ فَفَدَيت نَفْسِي بِأَرْبَعِينَ أُوقِيَّةً. فَآتَانِي أَرْبَعِينَ عَبْدًا، وَأَنَا أَرْجُو الْمَغْفِرَةَ الَّتِي وَعَدَنَا اللَّهُ، جَلَّ ثَنَاؤُهُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ذُكر لَنَا أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا قَدِمَ عَلَيْهِ مَالُ الْبَحْرَيْنِ ثَمَانُونَ أَلْفًا، وَقَدْ تَوَضَّأَ لِصَلَاةِ الظُّهْرِ، فَمَا أَعْطَى يومئذ ساكتًا وَلَا حَرَمَ سَائِلًا وَمَا صَلَّى يَوْمَئِذٍ حَتَّى فَرَّقَهُ، فَأَمَرَ الْعَبَّاسَ أَنْ يَأْخُذَ مِنْهُ وَيَحْتَثِيَ، فَأَخَذَ. قَالَ: فَكَانَ الْعَبَّاسُ يَقُولُ: هَذَا خَيْرٌ مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنَّا، وَأَرْجُو الْمَغْفِرَةَ.

وَقَالَ يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ سُفْيَانَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ حُمَيْدِ بْنِ هِلَالٍ قَالَ: بَعَثَ ابْنُ الْحَضْرَمِيِّ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنَ الْبَحْرَيْنِ ثَمَانِينَ أَلْفًا، مَا أَتَاهُ مَالٌ أَكْثَرَ مِنْهُ لَا قَبلُ وَلَا بَعدُ. قَالَ: فَنُثِرَتْ عَلَى حَصِيرٍ وَنُودِيَ بِالصَّلَاةِ. قَالَ: وَجَاءَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَمَثُلَ قَائِمًا عَلَى الْمَالِ، وَجَاءَ أَهْلُ الْمَسْجِدِ فَمَا كَانَ يَوْمَئِذٍ عددٌ وَلَا وزنٌ، مَا كَانَ إِلَّا قَبْضًا، [قَالَ] وَجَاءَ الْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ يَحْثِي فِي خَميصة عَلَيْهِ، وَذَهَبَ يَقُومُ فَلَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ، قَالَ: فَرَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ارْفَعْ عَلَيَّ. قَالَ: فَتَبَسَّمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى خَرَجَ ضَاحِكُهُ -أَوْ: نَابُهُ -وَقَالَ لَهُ: "أعدْ مِنَ الْمَالِ طَائِفَةً، وَقُمْ بِمَا تُطِيقُ". قَالَ: فَفَعَلَ، وَجَعَلَ الْعَبَّاسُ يَقُولُ -وَهُوَ مُنْطَلِقٌ -: أَمَّا إِحْدَى اللَّتَيْنِ وَعَدَنَا اللَّهُ فَقَدْ أَنْجَزْنَا، وَمَا نَدْرِي مَا يَصْنَعُ فِي الْأُخْرَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيّ قُلْ لِمَنْ فِي أَيْدِيكُمْ مِنَ الأسْرَى﴾ الْآيَةَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: هَذَا خَيْرٌ مِمَّا أُخِذَ مِنَّا، وَلَا أَدْرِي مَا يَصْنَعُ اللَّهُ فِي الْأُخْرَى فَمَا زَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَائِلًا عَلَى ذَلِكَ الْمَالِ، حَتَّى مَا بَقِيَ مِنْهُ دِرْهَمٌ، وَمَا بَعَثَ إِلَى أَهْلِهِ بِدِرْهَمٍ، ثُمَّ أَتَى الصَّلَاةَ فَصَلَّى 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ فِي ذَلِكَ: قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: أَنْبَأَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْحَافِظُ، أَخْبَرَنِي أَبُو الطَّيِّبِ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ السَّعِيدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مَحْمَش بْنُ عِصَامٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ طَهْمَان، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ صُهَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: أَتَى رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِمَالٍ مِنَ الْبَحْرَيْنِ، فَقَالَ: "انْثُرُوهُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ".

قَالَ: وَكَانَ أَكْثَرُ مَالٍ أُتِيَ بِهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَخَرَجَ إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ وَلَمْ يَلْتَفِتْ إِلَيْهِ، فَلَمَّا قَضَى الصَّلَاةَ جَاءَ فَجَلَسَ إِلَيْهِ. فَمَا كَانَ يَرَى أَحَدًا إِلَّا أَعْطَاهُ، إِذْ جَاءَ الْعَبَّاسُ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَعْطِنِي فَإِنِّي فَادَيْتُ نَفْسِي، وَفَادَيْتُ عَقيلا. فَقَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "خُذْ". فَحَثَا فِي ثَوْبِهِ، ثُمَّ ذَهَبَ يُقِلُّه فَلَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ، فَقَالَ: مُرْ بَعْضَهُمْ يَرْفَعُهُ إليَّ. قَالَ: "لَا". قَالَ: فَارْفَعْهُ أَنْتَ عليَّ. قَالَ: "لَا" فَنَثَرَ مِنْهُ ثُمَّ احْتَمَلَهُ عَلَى كَاهِلِهِ، ثُمَّ انْطَلَقَ، فَمَا زَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُتْبِعُهُ بَصَرَهُ حَتَّى خَفِيَ عَنْهُ، عَجَبًا مِنْ حِرْصه، فَمَا قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وثَمَّ مِنْهَا دِرْهَمٌ 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي مَوَاضِعَ مِنْ صَحِيحِهِ تَعْلِيقًا بِصِيغَةِ الْجَزْمِ، يَقُولُ: "وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ طَهْمَانَ" وَيَسُوقُهُ، وَفِي بَعْضِ السِّيَاقَاتِ أَتَمُّ مِنْ هَذَا 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ يُرِيدُوا خِيَانَتَكَ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا أَظْهَرُوا لَكَ مِنَ الْأَقْوَالِ، ﴿فَقَدْ خَانُوا اللَّهَ مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ قَبْلِ بَدْرٍ بِالْكُفْرِ بِهِ، ﴿فَأَمْكَنَ مِنْهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْإِسَارِ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، ﴿وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَلِيمٌ بِمَا يَفْعَلُهُ، حَكِيمٌ فِيهِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: نَزَلَتْ فِي عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَعْدِ بْنِ أَبِي سَرْح الْكَاتِبِ حِينَ ارْتَدَّ، وَلَحِقَ بِالْمُشْرِكِينَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: نَزَلَتْ فِي عَبَّاسٍ وَأَصْحَابِهِ، حِينَ قَالُوا: لَنَنْصَحَنَّ لَكَ عَلَى قَوْمِنَا.

وَفَسَّرَهَا السُّدِّيّ عَلَى الْعُمُومِ، وَهُوَ أَشْمَلُ وَأَظْهَرُ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 8:72 — verse 72

### Translation

He, exalted be He, mentioned the categories of the believers and divided them into: the emigrants, who left their homes and their wealth and came to support God and His Messenger and to establish His religion, and who expended their wealth and their lives in that; and the helpers, who were the Muslims of the people of Medina at that time, who sheltered their brothers the emigrants in their dwellings, shared their wealth with them, and supported God and His Messenger by fighting alongside them. So these, "some of them have more right to one another," meaning each of them has more claim upon the other than anyone else has. For this reason the Messenger of God ﷺ made brotherhood between the emigrants and the helpers, each two of them becoming brothers, and they used to inherit from one another by this bond, an inheritance that took precedence over blood kinship, until God, exalted be He, abrogated that by the rulings of inheritance. This is established in Sahih al-Bukhari from Ibn Abbas, and it was also related by al-Awfi and by Ali ibn Abi Talha from him, and Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Hasan, Qatadah and others said the same.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Jarir, that is, Ibn Abdullah al-Bajali, may God be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The emigrants and the helpers are allies of one another, and the freed captives of Quraysh and the freed captives of Thaqif are allies of one another until the Day of Resurrection." Ahmad alone transmitted this.

Al-Hafiz Abu Ya'la said: [chain] Ibn Mas'ud said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "The emigrants and the helpers, and the freed captives of Quraysh and the freed captives of Thaqif, are allies of one another in this world and the next." Thus he related it in the Musnad of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud. God and His Messenger have praised the emigrants and the helpers in more than one verse in His Book. He said: {And the first forerunners among the emigrants and the helpers and those who followed them in righteousness, God is pleased with them and they are pleased with Him, and He has prepared for them gardens beneath which rivers flow} [al-Tawbah: 100], and He said: {Indeed God has turned in mercy to the Prophet and the emigrants and the helpers who followed him in the hour of hardship} [al-Tawbah: 117], and He, exalted be He, said: {For the poor emigrants who were expelled from their homes and their wealth, seeking bounty from God and His pleasure, and supporting God and His Messenger, those are the truthful ones. And those who had settled in the abode and in faith before them love those who emigrated to them, and find in their hearts no need for what they were given, and prefer them over themselves even though they were in want} [al-Hashr: 8, 9].

The best that has been said concerning His saying {and find in their hearts no need for what they were given} is that they did not envy them for the superiority God had granted them because of their emigration, for the apparent meaning of these verses is that the emigrants are given precedence over the helpers. This is a matter upon which the scholars are agreed, without dispute. For this reason the Imam Abu Bakr Ahmad ibn Amr ibn Abd al-Khaliq al-Bazzar said in his Musnad: [chain] Hudhayfah said: The Messenger of God ﷺ gave me the choice between emigration and being one of the helpers, and I chose emigration.

Then he said: We do not know it except by this route.

His saying: {And those who believed but did not emigrate, you have no duty of protection toward them} (Hamzah read it "wilayatihim" with a kasrah, and the rest read it "walayatihim" with a fatha, and the two are one, like "dilalah" and "dalalah") {in anything, until they emigrate}. This is the third category of the believers, those who believed but did not emigrate, but rather remained in their desert dwellings. These have no share in the spoils of war, nor in the fifth of it, except for what they were present for in fighting, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Buraydah ibn al-Husayb al-Aslami, may God be pleased with him, said: Whenever the Messenger of God ﷺ sent forth a commander over a raiding party or an army, he would charge him particularly to fear God, and to treat well the Muslims who were with him, and he would say: "Wage war in the name of God, in the path of God. Fight those who disbelieve in God. When you meet your enemy among the polytheists, call them to one of three things, or matters, and whichever of them they respond to, accept it from them and hold back from them. Call them to Islam, and if they respond to you, accept it from them and hold back from them. Then call them to move from their land to the land of the emigrants, and inform them that if they do so they will have what the emigrants have and will be subject to what the emigrants are subject to. If they refuse and choose to remain in their own land, then inform them that they will be like the bedouin Muslims, subject to the ruling of God that applies to the believers, and they will have no share in the spoils of war or the booty unless they fight alongside the Muslims. If they refuse that, then call them to pay the jizyah. If they respond, accept it from them and hold back from them. If they refuse, then seek the help of God and fight them."

Muslim alone transmitted this, and he has additional wordings besides.

His saying: {And if they seek your help in religion, then it is your duty to help them, except against a people between whom and you there is a covenant. And God is All-Seeing of what you do}. He, exalted be He, is saying: if these bedouins, who did not emigrate, seek your help in a religious conflict against an enemy of theirs, then help them, for it is obligatory upon you to help them, since they are your brothers in religion, unless they seek your help against a people among the disbelievers {between whom and you there is a covenant}, meaning a truce for a fixed term. In that case do not betray your pledge of protection, nor break your oaths with those with whom you have made a covenant. This has been related from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَصْنَافَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَقَسَمَهُمْ إِلَى مُهَاجِرِينَ، خَرَجُوا مِنْ دِيَارِهِمْ وَأَمْوَالِهِمْ، وجاؤوا لِنَصْرِ اللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، وَإِقَامَةِ دِينِهِ، وَبَذَلُوا أَمْوَالَهُمْ وَأَنْفُسَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ. وَإِلَى أَنْصَارٍ، وَهُمُ: الْمُسْلِمُونَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ إِذْ ذَاكَ، آوَوْا إِخْوَانَهُمُ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ فِي مَنَازِلِهِمْ، وَوَاسَوْهُمْ فِي أَمْوَالِهِمْ، وَنَصَرُوا اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ بِالْقِتَالِ مَعَهُمْ، فَهَؤُلَاءِ بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلَى بِبَعْضٍ أَيْ: كُلٌّ مِنْهُمْ أَحَقُّ بِالْآخَرِ مِنْ كُلِّ أَحَدٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا آخَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالْأَنْصَارِ، كُلُّ اثْنَيْنِ أخَوَان، فَكَانُوا يَتَوَارَثُونَ بِذَلِكَ إِرْثًا مُقَدَّمًا عَلَى الْقَرَابَةِ، حَتَّى نَسَخَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى ذَلِكَ بِالْمَوَارِيثِ، ثَبَتَ ذَلِكَ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَرَوَاهُ العَوْفي، وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنْهُ وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ شَرِيكٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ، عَنْ جَرير -هُوَ ابْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْبَجَلِيُّ -رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ -قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم: "المهاجرون والأنصار أولياء بعضهم لِبَعْضٍ، وَالطُّلَقَاءُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ وَالْعُتَقَاءُ مِنْ ثَقِيفٍ بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ" تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا شَيْبَانُ حَدَّثَنَا عِكْرِمة -يَعْنِي ابْنَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْأَزْدِيَّ -حَدَّثَنَا عَاصِمٌ، عَنْ شَقِيق، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "الْمُهَاجِرُونَ وَالْأَنْصَارُ، وَالطُّلَقَاءُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ وَالْعُتَقَاءُ مِنْ ثَقِيفَ، بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ". هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ فِي مُسْنَدِ عَبْدِ الله بن مسعود وَقَدْ أَثْنَى اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ عَلَى الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالْأَنْصَارِ فِي غَيْرِ مَا آيَةٍ فِي كِتَابِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّابِقُونَ الأوَّلُونَ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالأنْصَارِ وَالَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوهُمْ بِإِحْسَانٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَرَضُوا عَنْهُ وَأَعَدَّ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي تَحْتَهَا الأنْهَارُ﴾ الْآيَةَ [التَّوْبَةِ: ١٠٠] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ وَالْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالأنْصَارِ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوهُ فِي سَاعَةِ الْعُسْرَةِ﴾ الْآيَةَ. [التَّوْبَةِ: ١١٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِلْفُقَرَاءِ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ الَّذِينَ أُخْرِجُوا مِنْ دِيارِهِمْ وَأَمْوَالِهِمْ يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلا مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرِضْوَانًا وَيَنْصُرُونَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصَّادِقُونَ وَالَّذِينَ تَبَوَّءُوا الدَّارَ وَالإيمَانَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ يُحِبُّونَ مَنْ هَاجَرَ إِلَيْهِمْ وَلا يَجِدُونَ فِي صُدُورِهِمْ حَاجَةً مِمَّا أُوتُوا وَيُؤْثِرُونَ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ وَلَوْ كَانَ بِهِمْ خَصَاصَةٌ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْحَشْرِ: ٨، ٩] .

وَأَحْسَنُ مَا قِيلَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا يَجِدُونَ فِي صُدُورِهِمْ حَاجَةً مِمَّا أُوتُوا﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَحْسُدُونَهُمْ عَلَى فَضْلِ مَا أَعْطَاهُمُ اللَّهُ عَلَى هِجْرَتِهِمْ، فَإِنَّ ظَاهِرَ الْآيَاتِ تَقْدِيمُ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ عَلَى الْأَنْصَارِ، وَهَذَا أَمْرٌ مُجْمَعٌ عَلَيْهِ بَيْنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ، لَا يَخْتَلِفُونَ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَبْدِ الْخَالِقِ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مَعْمَر، حَدَّثَنَا مُسْلِمُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ قَالَ: خَيَّرني رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ الْهِجْرَةِ وَالنُّصْرَةِ، فَاخْتَرْتُ الْهِجْرَةَ 

ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَلَمْ يُهَاجِرُوا مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ وَلايَتِهِمْ﴾ [قَرَأَ حَمْزَةُ: "وِلَايَتِهِمْ" بِالْكَسْرِ، وَالْبَاقُونَ بِالْفَتْحِ، وَهُمَا وَاحِدٌ كالدِّلالة والدَّلالة] ﴿مِنْ شَيْءٍ حَتَّى يُهَاجِرُوا﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الصِّنْفُ الثَّالِثُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَلَمْ يُهَاجِرُوا، بَلْ أَقَامُوا فِي بَوَاديهم، فَهَؤُلَاءِ لَيْسَ لَهُمْ فِي الْمَغَانِمِ نَصِيبٌ، وَلَا فِي خُمسها إِلَّا مَا حَضَرُوا فِيهِ الْقِتَالَ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا وَكيع، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَلْقَمَةَ بْنِ مَرْثَد، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ بُرَيْدة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: بُرَيْدة بْنِ الحُصَيب الْأَسْلَمِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا بَعَثَ أَمِيرًا عَلَى سَرِيَّةٍ أَوْ جَيْشٍ، أَوْصَاهُ فِي خَاصَّةِ نَفْسِهِ بِتَقْوَى اللَّهِ وَمَنْ مَعَهُ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ خَيْرًا، وَقَالَ: "اغْزُوا بِاسْمِ اللَّهِ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، قَاتِلُوا مَنْ كَفَرَ بِالْلَّهِ، إِذَا لَقِيتَ عَدُوَّكَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ فَادْعُهُمْ إِلَى إِحْدَى ثَلَاثِ خِصَالٍ -أَوْ: خِلَالٍ -فَأَيَّتُهُنَّ مَا أَجَابُوكَ إِلَيْهَا فَاقْبَلْ مِنْهُمْ، وكُفَّ عَنْهُمْ: ادْعُهُمْ إِلَى الْإِسْلَامِ، فَإِنْ أَجَابُوكَ فَاقْبَلْ مِنْهُمْ، وَكُفَّ عَنْهُمْ، ثُمَّ ادْعُهُمْ إِلَى التَّحَوُّلِ مِنْ دَارِهِمْ إِلَى دَارِ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ، وَأَعْلِمْهُمْ إِنْ فَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ أَنَّ لَهُمْ مَا لِلْمُهَاجِرِينَ، وَأَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ مَا عَلَى الْمُهَاجِرِينَ. فَإِنْ أَبَوْا وَاخْتَارُوا دَارَهُمْ فَأَعْلِمْهُمْ أَنَّهُمْ يَكُونُونَ كأعراب الْمُسْلِمِينَ، يَجْرِي عَلَيْهِمْ حُكْمُ اللَّهِ الَّذِي يَجْرِي عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَلَا يَكُونُ لَهُمْ فِي الْفَيْءِ وَالْغَنِيمَةِ نَصِيبٌ، إِلَّا أَنْ يُجَاهِدُوا مَعَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، فَإِنْ هُمْ أَبَوْا فَادْعُهُمْ إِلَى إِعْطَاءِ الْجِزْيَةِ. فَإِنْ أَجَابُوا فَاقْبَلْ مِنْهُمْ وَكُفَّ عَنْهُمْ، فَإِنْ أَبَوْا فَاسْتَعِنْ بِاللَّهِ ثُمَّ قَاتِلْهُمْ".

انْفَرَدَ بِهِ مُسْلِمٌ، وَعِنْدَهُ زِيَادَاتٌ أُخَرُ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنِ اسْتَنْصَرُوكُمْ فِي الدِّينِ فَعَلَيْكُمُ النَّصْرُ إِلا عَلَى قَوْمٍ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ مِيثَاقٌ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَإِنِ اسْتَنْصَرُوكُمْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْأَعْرَابُ، الَّذِينَ لَمْ يُهَاجِرُوا فِي قِتَالٍ دِينِيٍّ، عَلَى عَدُوٍّ لَهُمْ فَانْصُرُوهُمْ، فَإِنَّهُ وَاجِبٌ عَلَيْكُمْ نَصْرُهُمْ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ إِخْوَانُكُمْ فِي الدِّينِ، إِلَّا أَنْ يَسْتَنْصِرُوكُمْ عَلَى قَوْمٍ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ ﴿بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ مِيثَاقٌ﴾ أَيْ: مُهَادَنَةٌ إِلَى مُدَّةٍ، فَلَا تَخْفِرُوا ذِمَّتَكُمْ، وَلَا تَنْقُضُوا أَيْمَانَكُمْ مَعَ الَّذِينَ عَاهَدْتُمْ. وَهَذَا مَرْوِيٌّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

---

## 8:73 — verse 73

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned that the believers are allies of one another, He cut off allegiance between them and the disbelievers, as al-Hakim said in his Mustadrak:

[chain] Muhammad ibn Salih ibn Hani', Abu Sa'd Yahya ibn Mansur al-Harawi, Muhammad ibn Aban, Muhammad ibn Yazid and Sufyan ibn Husayn, from al-Zuhri, from Ali ibn al-Husayn, from Amr ibn Uthman, from Usama, that the Prophet ﷺ said: "The people of two religions do not inherit from one another, a Muslim does not inherit from a disbeliever, nor does a disbeliever inherit from a Muslim." Then he recited: {And those who disbelieve are allies of one another. If you do not do so, there will be turmoil in the land and great corruption.} Then al-Hakim said: its chain is sound, and the two of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) did not record it.

I say: this hadith is found in the two Sahihs from the narration of Usama ibn Zayd, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "A Muslim does not inherit from a disbeliever, nor does a disbeliever inherit from a Muslim." And in the Musnad and the Sunan, from the hadith of Amr ibn Shu'ayb, from his father, from his grandfather, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The people of two separate religions do not inherit from one another." And al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (a sound, acceptable report).

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] Muhammad, [from Muhammad ibn Thawr], from Ma'mar, from al-Zuhri: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ took a pledge from a man who entered Islam, saying: "You will establish prayer, give zakat, perform pilgrimage to the House, fast Ramadan, and you will not see the fire of a polytheist without being at war with him."

This is mursal (a report with a missing link at the end, here missing the Companion) from this route, but it has been narrated as connected from another route, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "I am free of responsibility for every Muslim who dwells among the polytheists." Then he said: "Their two fires should not be visible to one another."

Abu Dawud said at the end of the Book of Jihad: [chain] Muhammad ibn Dawud ibn Sufyan, Yahya ibn Hassan informed me, Sulayman ibn Musa Abu Dawud reported to us, Ja'far ibn Sa'd ibn Samura ibn Jundub told us [Khubayb ibn Sulayman told me, from his father Sulayman ibn Samura], from Samura ibn Jundub: as for what follows, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever associates with a polytheist and dwells with him is like him."

The Hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh mentioned, from the hadith of Hatim ibn Isma'il, from Abdullah ibn Hurmuz, from Muhammad and Sa'id, the two sons of Ubayd, from Abu Hatim al-Muzani, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When someone comes to you whose religion and character you are satisfied with, then marry your daughter to him. If you do not do so, there will be turmoil in the land and widespread corruption." They said: O Messenger of Allah, even if he is such and such? He said: "When someone comes to you whose religion and character you are satisfied with, then marry your daughter to him," three times.

Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi both recorded it, from the hadith of Hatim ibn Isma'il, through him, in a similar wording.

It was also narrated from the hadith of Abd al-Hamid ibn Sulayman, from Ibn Ajlan, from Ibn Wathima al-Nasri, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When someone comes to you whose character and religion you are satisfied with, then give him your daughter in marriage. If you do not do so, there will be turmoil in the land and widespread corruption."

The meaning of the Exalted's saying: {If you do not do so, there will be turmoil in the land and great corruption} is: if you do not keep away from the polytheists and give your allegiance to the believers instead, then turmoil will occur among the people. That is, confusion of affairs and the mixing of the believer with the disbeliever, so that widespread, long lasting, and extensive corruption will occur among the people.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بعضُهم أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ، قَطَعَ الْمُوَالَاةَ بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ الْكُفَّارِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ صَالِحِ بْنِ هَانِئٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعْدٍ يَحْيَى بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ الْهَرَوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبَانٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ وَسُفْيَانُ بْنُ حُسَيْنٍ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ عُثْمَانَ، عَنْ أُسَامَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَا يَتَوَارَثُ أَهْلُ مِلَّتَيْنِ، وَلَا يَرِثُ مُسْلِمٌ كَافِرًا، وَلَا كَافِرٌ مُسْلِمًا"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ إِلا تَفْعَلُوهُ تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ فِي الأرْضِ وَفَسَادٌ كَبِيرٌ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ الْحَاكِمُ: صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ 

قُلْتُ: الْحَدِيثُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ أُسَامَةَ بْنِ زَيْدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا يَرِثُ الْمُسْلِمُ الْكَافِرَ وَلَا الْكَافِرُ الْمُسْلِمَ" وَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ وَالسُّنَنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثُ عَمْرِو بْنِ شُعَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا يَتَوَارَثُ أَهْلُ مِلَّتَيْنِ شَتَّى" وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ، [عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ ثَوْرٍ] عَنْ مَعْمَرٍ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ: أَنَّ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَخَذَ عَلَى رَجُلٍ دَخَلَ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ فَقَالَ: "تُقِيمُ الصَّلَاةَ، وَتُؤْتِي الزَّكَاةَ، وَتَحُجُّ الْبَيْتَ، وَتَصُومُ رَمَضَانَ، وَأَنَّكَ لَا تَرَى نَارَ مُشْرِكٍ إِلَّا وَأَنْتَ لَهُ حَرْبٌ" 

وَهَذَا مُرْسَلٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مُتَّصِلًا مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "أَنَا بَرِيءٌ مِنْ كُلِّ مُسْلِمٍ بَيْنَ ظَهْرَانَيِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ"، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "لَا يَتَرَاءَى نَارَاهُمَا" 

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي آخِرِ كِتَابِ الْجِهَادِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ بْنِ سُفْيَانَ، أَخْبَرَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ حَسَّانَ، أَنْبَأَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ مُوسَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ سَعْدِ بن سَمُرَة بن جُنْدُب [حدثني خبيب بن سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ سَمُرَةَ] عَنْ سمرة بن جندب: أما بعد، قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ جَامَعَ الْمُشْرِكَ وَسَكَنَ مَعَهُ فَإِنَّهُ مِثْلُهُ" 

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُوَيه، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَاتِمِ بْنِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ هُرْمُزَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ وَسَعِيدٍ ابْنَيْ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ الْمُزَنِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا أَتَاكُمْ مَنْ تَرْضون دِينَهُ وَخُلُقَهُ فَأَنْكِحُوهُ إِلَّا تَفْعَلُوا تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَفَسَادٌ عَرِيضٌ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ؟ قَالَ: "إِذَا أَتَاكُمْ مَنْ تَرْضَوْنَ دِينَهُ وَخُلُقَهُ فَأَنْكِحُوهُ" ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ.

وَأَخْرَجَهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَاتِمِ بْنِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، بِهِ بِنَحْوِهِ 

ثُمَّ رُويَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَجْلان، عَنِ ابْنِ وَثيمةَ النَّصْري عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا أَتَاكُمْ مَنْ تَرْضَوْنَ خُلُقَهُ وَدِينَهُ فَزَوِّجُوهُ، إِلَّا تَفْعَلُوا تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَفَسَادٌ عَرِيضٌ" 

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِلا تَفْعَلُوهُ تَكُنْ فِتْنَةٌ فِي الأرْضِ وَفَسَادٌ كَبِيرٌ﴾ أَيْ: إِنْ لَمْ تُجَانِبُوا الْمُشْرِكِينَ وَتُوَالُوا الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَإِلَّا وَقَعَتِ الْفِتْنَةُ فِي النَّاسِ، وَهُوَ الْتِبَاسُ الْأَمْرِ، وَاخْتِلَاطُ الْمُؤْمِنِ بِالْكَافِرِ، فَيَقَعُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ فَسَادٌ مُنْتَشِرٌ طَوِيلٌ عَرِيضٌ.

---

## 8:74-75 — verses 74-75 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the ruling concerning the believers in this world, He followed it by mentioning what awaits them in the Hereafter. So He informed about them by way of the reality of faith, as preceded at the beginning of the surah, and that He would reward them with forgiveness and pardon for whatever sins there might be, and with noble provision, which is good, abundant, pure, and honorable provision, lasting and continuing forever, never cut off nor ending, and never causing weariness or boredom because of its goodness and variety.

Then He mentioned that the followers who remained in this world upon the same faith and righteous deeds that the believers held would be with them in the Hereafter, as He said: {And the first forerunners among the Muhajirun and the Ansar, and those who followed them with excellence, Allah is pleased with them and they are pleased with Him, and He has prepared for them Gardens beneath which rivers flow} [al-Tawbah: 100], and He said: {And those who came after them say: Our Lord, forgive us and our brothers who preceded us in faith, and put not in our hearts any rancor toward those who believe. Our Lord, You are indeed Full of Kindness, Most Merciful} [al-Hashr: 10]. And in the hadith agreed upon, indeed mutawatir (mass-transmitted) through authentic chains, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he said: "A man is with whomever he loves." And in another hadith: "Whoever loves a people will be gathered with them."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Jarir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The Muhajirun and the Ansar are allies of one another, and the Tulaqa' (those freed at the conquest of Makkah) among the Quraysh and the 'Utaqa' (those freed) among Thaqif are allies of one another until the Day of Resurrection." Sharik said: al-A'mash narrated to us from Tamim ibn Salamah, from 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Hilal, from Jarir, from the Prophet ﷺ, the like of it.

Ahmad alone transmitted it through these two chains.

As for His statement, the Exalted: {And those of blood relationship are more entitled to one another in the Book of Allah}, meaning: in the ruling of Allah. And what is meant by His statement {and those of blood relationship} is not the specific meaning that the scholars of inheritance shares (fara'id) apply to relatives who have no fixed share and are not agnatic heirs ('asabah), but rather are connected through an heir, such as the maternal aunt, the maternal uncle, the paternal aunt, the children of daughters, the children of sisters, and the like, as some claim, citing this verse as evidence and holding this explicitly as their position in the matter. Rather, the truth is that the verse is general, encompassing all kinds of blood relations, as Ibn 'Abbas, Mujahid, 'Ikrimah, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and more than one other stated explicitly, namely that it abrogates inheritance by alliance (hilf) and by the brotherhood-pact by which they used to inherit from one another previously. On this basis it encompasses the possessors of blood relationship (dhawu al-arham) under this specific designation. And those who do not grant them inheritance argue with evidences, the strongest of which is the hadith: "Indeed Allah has given every rightful possessor his right, so there is no bequest for an heir." They said: had he been a rightful possessor, he would have had a named, fixed share in the Book of Allah; since this is not the case, he is not an heir. And Allah knows best.

End of the tafsir of Surat al-Anfal. To Allah belongs all praise and grace, and upon Him is reliance and trust, and He is sufficient for us and the best of guardians.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى حُكْمَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ مَا لَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ، فَأَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ بِحَقِيقَةِ الْإِيمَانِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ، وَأَنَّهُ سَيُجَازِيهِمْ بِالْمَغْفِرَةِ وَالصَّفْحِ عَنْ ذُنُوبٍ إِنْ كَانَتْ، وَبِالرِّزْقِ الْكَرِيمِ، وَهُوَ الْحَسَنُ الْكَثِيرُ الطَّيِّبُ الشَّرِيفُ، دَائِمٌ مُسْتَمِرٌّ أَبَدًا لَا يَنْقَطِعُ وَلَا يَنْقَضِي، وَلَا يُسْأَمُ وَلَا يُمَلُّ لِحُسْنِهِ وَتَنَوُّعِهِ.

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ أَنَّ الْأَتْبَاعَ لَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا عَلَى مَا كَانُوا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْإِيمَانِ وَالْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ فَهُمْ مَعَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّابِقُونَ الأوَّلُونَ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالأنْصَارِ وَالَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوهُمْ بِإِحْسَانٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَرَضُوا عَنْهُ وَأَعَدَّ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي تَحْتَهَا الأنْهَارُ﴾ الْآيَةَ [التَّوْبَةِ: ١٠٠] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ جَاءُوا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ يَقُولُونَ رَبَّنَااغْفِرْ لَنَا وَلإخْوَانِنَا الَّذِينَ سَبَقُونَا بِالإيمَانِ وَلا تَجْعَلْ فِي قُلُوبِنَا غِلا لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا رَبَّنَا إِنَّكَ رَءُوفٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ:١٠] وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْمُتَّفِقِ عَلَيْهِ، بَلِ الْمُتَوَاتِرِ مِنْ طُرُقٍ صَحِيحَةٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "الْمَرْءُ مَعَ مَنْ أَحَبَّ"، وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "مَنْ أَحَبَّ قَوْمًا حُشر معهُم" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ شَرِيكٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ، عَنْ جَرِيرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الْمُهَاجِرُونَ والأنصار أولياء بعضهم لبعض، والطلقاء من قريش وَالْعُتَقَاءُ مِنْ ثَقِيفٍ بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ". قَالَ شَرِيكٌ: فَحَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ تَمِيمِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ هِلَالٍ، عَنْ جَرِيرٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مِثْلَهُ.

تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ هَذَيْنَ الْوَجْهَيْنِ 

وَأَمَّا قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأُوْلُوا الأرْحَامِ بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلَى بِبَعْضٍ فِي كِتَابِ اللهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي حُكْمِ اللَّهِ، وَلَيْسَ الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأُوْلُوا الأرْحَامِ﴾ خُصُوصِيَّةَ مَا يُطْلِقُهُ عُلَمَاءُ الْفَرَائِضِ عَلَى الْقَرَابَةِ، الَّذِينَ لَا فَرْضَ لَهُمْ وَلَا هُمْ عَصَبَةٌ، بَلْ يُدْلون بِوَارِثٍ، كَالْخَالَةِ، وَالْخَالِ، وَالْعَمَّةِ، وَأَوْلَادِ الْبَنَاتِ، وَأَوْلَادِ الْأَخَوَاتِ، وَنَحْوِهِمْ، كَمَا قَدْ يَزْعُمُهُ بَعْضُهُمْ وَيَحْتَجُّ بِالْآيَةِ، وَيَعْتَقِدُ ذَلِكَ صَرِيحًا في المسألة، بل الحق أن الآية عَامَّةٌ تَشْمَلُ جَمِيعَ الْقِرَابَاتِ. كَمَا نَصَّ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وقَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: عَلَى أَنَّهَا نَاسِخَةٌ لِلْإِرْثِ بِالْحِلْفِ وَالْإِخَاءِ اللَّذَيْنِ كَانُوا يَتَوَارَثُونَ بِهِمَا أَوْ لَا وَعَلَى هَذَا فَتَشْمَلُ ذَوِي الْأَرْحَامِ بِالِاسْمِ الْخَاصِّ. وَمَنْ لَمْ يُوَرِّثْهُمْ يَحْتَجُّ بِأَدِلَّةٍ مِنْ أَقْوَاهَا حَدِيثُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَعْطَى كُلَّ ذِي حَقٍّ حَقَّهُ، فَلَا وصِيَّة لِوَارِثٍ"، قَالُوا: فَلَوْ كَانَ ذَا حَقٍّ لَكَانَ لَهُ فَرْضٌ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ مُسَمًّى، فَلَمَّا لَمْ يَكُنْ كَذَلِكَ لَمْ يَكُنْ وَارِثًا، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

آخِرُ [تَفْسِيرِ] سُورَةِ "الْأَنْفَالِ"، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ، وَعَلَيْهِ [الثِّقَةُ وَ] التُّكْلَانُ وهو حسبنا ونعم الوكيل.

---
